#Text:Āgniveśyagṛhyasūtra
#Edition:Varma 1940
#Data entry:?
#Notes:Checked and formatted: O. Hellwig



1.1.1.1	upanayanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ / saptame varṣe brāhmaṇam upanayītaikādaśavarṣe rājanyaṃ dvādaśe varṣe vaiśyam
1.1.1.2	vasante brāhmaṇaṃ grīṣme rājanyaṃ śaradi vaiśyam
1.1.1.3	āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre viśeṣeṇa puṃnāmadheye yugmān brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā aśitasya kumārasya keśān vāpayitvā snātam alaṅkṛtam ahataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāpya prācīnapravaṇa udīcīnapravane prāgudakpravaṇe same vā deśe uddhatyāvokṣya sikatābhiḥ sthaṇḍilaṃ kṛtvollikhyāgniṃ mathitvā laukikaṃ vāhṛtya nidhāpyopasamādadhāti
1.1.1.4	prāgagrair darbhaiḥ paristṛṇāty api vodagagrāḥ paścāt purastāc ca bhavanti
1.1.1.5	dakṣiṇān uttarān karoty uttarān adharān yadi prāgudagagrāḥ
1.1.1.6	dakṣiṇenāgniṃ brahmāyatane darbhān saṃstīrya mayi gṛhṇāmi yo no agniḥ iti dvābhyām ātmānam agniṃ gṛhītvottareṇāgniṃ darbhān saṃstīryāthāsya dravyāṇi prayunakti
1.1.1.7	aśmānam ahataṃ vāso 'jinaṃ mauñjīmekhalāṃ trivṛtāṃ brāhmaṇasya jyāṃ rājanyasya āvikaṃ vaiśyasya bailvaṃ pālāśaṃ vā daṇḍaṃ brāhmaṇasya naiyagrodhaṃ rājanyasyaudumbaraṃ vaiśyasyaikaviṃśatidārum idhmam asyety āhutiparimāṇaṃ vā
1.1.1.8	etasmin śamyāḥ paridhīn idhma upasaṃnahyati
1.1.1.9	darvīṃ kūrcam ājyasthālīṃ praṇītāpraṇayaṃ yena cānyāni prokṣyate tac ca sakṛd eva sarvāṇi yathopapadaṃ vā
1.1.1.10	etasmin kāle brahmā yajñopavītaṃ kṛtvāpa ācamyāpareṇāgniṃ dakṣiṇātikramya brahmāsanāt tṛṇaṃ nirasyāpa upaspṛśyāgnim abhimukham upaviśati
1.1.1.11	samāvapracchinnāgrau darbhau prādeśamātre pavitre kṛtvā anyena nakhācchittvādbhir anumṛjya pavitrāntarhite pātre 'pa ānīyopabilaṃ pūrayitvā udagagrābhyāṃ pavitrābhyāṃ trir utpūyottareṇāgniṃ darbheṣu sādayitvā darbhair apidadhāti
1.1.1.12	tiraḥ pavitraṃ prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya yathā purastād bilavanty uttānāni kṛtvā viṣāyedhmaṃ triḥ sarvābhiḥ prokṣati
1.1.1.13	darvīṃ niṣṭapya saṃmṛjya punar niṣṭapya nidadhāti
1.1.1.14	saṃmārgān abhyukṣyāgnāv ādadhāti
1.1.1.15	ājyaṃ vilāpya pavitrāntarhitāyām ājyasthālyām ājyaṃ nirupyodīco 'ṅgārān nirūhya teṣv adhiśritya avadyotya darbhatṛṇābhyāṃ pratyasya triḥ paryagnikṛtvā udag udvāsyāṅgārān pratyūhya udagagrābhyāṃ pavitrābhyāṃ punar āhāram ājyaṃ trir utpūya pavitre agnāv ādadhāti
1.1.1.16	śamyābhiḥ paridhibhiḥ paridadhāty apareṇāgnim udīcīnakumbhāṃ madhyamāṃ nidadhāti
1.1.1.17	dakṣīṇenāgniṃ saṃspṛṣṭvā madhyamayā prācīnakumbām uttareṇāgniṃ saṃspṛṣṭvā madhyamayā prācīnakumbām apareṇāgniṃ prāṅmukha upaviśati
1.1.1.18	dakṣiṇato yajñopavīty ācāntaḥ kumāra upaviśyānvārabhate
1.1.1.19	atha pariṣiñcati
1.1.1.20	adite 'numanyasva iti dakṣiṇataḥ prācīnam anumate 'numanyasva iti paścād udīcīnaṃ sarasvate 'numanyasva iti uttarataḥ prācīnaṃ deva savitaḥ prasuva iti sarvataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ pariṣicyedhyam ājyenābhyajyābhyādadhāti
1.1.1.21	ayaṃ ta idhma ātmā jātavedas tenedhyasva vardhasva ceddha vardhaya cāsmān prajayā paśubhiḥ brahmavarcasenānnādyena samedhaya svāhā iti
1.1.1.22	atha darvyā juhoti
1.1.1.23	uttaraṃ paridhisandhim anvavahṛtya prajāpataye manase svāhā iti manasā dhyāyan dakṣiṇāprāñcam udañcam ṛjuṃ saṃtataṃ juhoti
1.1.1.24	dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhim anvavahṛtya indrāya svāhā iti prāñcam udañcam ṛjum āghārāv āghāryājyabhāgau juhoti
1.1.1.25	agnaye svāhā ity uttarārdhapūrvārdhe
1.1.1.26	somāya svāhā iti dakṣiṇārdhapūrvārdhe
1.1.1.27	tāv antareṇetarāhutīr juhoti
1.1.1.28	yukto vaha jātavedaḥ purastād agne viddhi karma kriyamāṇaṃ yathedam / tvaṃ bhiṣag bheṣajasyāsi kartā tvayā gām aśvān puruṣān sanemi svāhā / yā tiraścī nipadyase 'haṃ vidharaṇī iti / tāṃ tvā ghṛtasya dhārayā agnau saṃrādhanyai yaje svāhā / saṃrādhanyai devyai svāhā / prasādhanyai devyai svāhā / bhūḥ svāhā / bhuvaḥ svāhā / svaḥ svāhā / bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā iti / sarvadarvīhomānām eṣa kalpaḥ
1.1.2.1	mantrānte nityaḥ svāhākāro 'mantrāsv amuṣmai svāheti
1.1.2.2	yathādaivatam bhūr bhuvas svariti vyāhṛtibhir juhoty ekaikaśaḥ samastābhiś ca
1.1.2.3	āyurdā agna ity eṣaḥ
1.1.2.4	āyurdā deva jarasaṃ gṛṇāno ghṛtapratīko ghṛtapṛṣṭho agne / ghṛtaṃ pibann amṛtaṃ cāru gavyaṃ piteva putraṃ jarase nayemaṃ svāhā iti
1.1.2.5	imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvan no agne sa tvan no agne tvam agne ayāsy ayāsan manasā hitaḥ ayāsan havyam ūhiṣe ayāno dheiha bheṣajaṃ svāhā / prajāpataya ity eṣā
1.1.2.6	yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricaṃ yad vā nyūnam ihākaram / agniṣ ṭat sviṣṭakṛd vidvān sarvaṃ sviṣṭaṃ suhutaṃ karotu me / agnaye sviṣṭakṛte suhutahute sarvahute sarvaprāyaścittāhutīnāṃ kāmānāṃ samardhayitre svāhā / ity uttarārdhapūrvārdhe 'saṃsaktām itarābhir āhutibhir juhoti
1.1.2.7	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati purastāt sviṣṭakṛtaḥ
1.1.2.8	cittaṃ ca svāhā / cittiś ca svāhā /iti jayāñjuhoti
1.1.2.9	cittāya svāhā / cittaye svāhā iti vā
1.1.2.10	agnir bhūtānām adhipatis sa māvatu ity abhyātānān
1.1.2.11	asmin brahmann asmin kṣatra ity abhyātāneṣv anuyuñjati
1.1.2.12	pitaraḥ pitāmahāḥ pare 'vare iti prācīnāvītī juhoty upatiṣṭhati
1.1.2.13	ṛtāṣāḍ ṛtadhāmā iti rāṣṭrabhṛtaḥ
1.1.2.14	paryāyam anudrutya tasmai svāhā iti pūrvām āhutīṃ juhoti
1.1.2.15	tābhyas svāhā ity uttarām
1.1.2.16	agreṇottaraṃ paridhisandhim aśmānaṃ nidhāya dakṣiṇena pādena kumāram āsthāpayati / ātiṣṭhemam aśmānam aśmeva tvaṃ sthiro bhava / pramṛṇīhi durasyūn sahasva pṛtanāyataḥ / ity etena
1.1.2.17	ahataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāpayati pūrvaṃ nidhāya / yā akṛntann avayan yā atanvata yāś ca devīr antān abhito 'dadanta / tās tvā devīr jarase saṃvyayantv āyuṣmān idaṃ paridhatsva vāsaḥ / paridhatta dhatta vāsasainaṃ śatāyuṣaṃ kṛṇuta dīrgham āyuḥ / bṛhaspatiḥ prāyacchad vāsa etat somāya rājñe paridhātavā u / jarāṃ gacchāsi paridhatsva vāso bhavā kṛṣṭīnām abhiśastipāvā / śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ suvarcā rāyaś ca poṣam upasaṃvyayasva iti
1.1.2.18	paridhāpyābhimantrayate / parīdaṃ vāso adhitā svastaye 'bhūr āpīnām abhiśastipāvā / śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcīr vasūni cāryo vibhajāsi jīvan // ity enaṃ mekhalayā triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ paridadhāti
1.1.2.19	dvir ity eke
1.1.2.20	yā duritāt paribādhamānā śarma varūthaṃ punatī na āgāt / prāṇāpānābhyāṃ balam āvahantī svasā devānāṃ subhagā mekhaleyam / ity uttarato nābhes trivṛtaṃ granthiṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇato nābheḥ parikarṣati
1.1.2.21	athāsmā ajinam uttarīyaṃ karoti
1.1.2.22	mitrasya cakṣurdharuṇaṃ balīyas tejo yaśasvi sthaviraṃ samiddham / anāhanasyaṃ vasanaṃ jariṣṇu parīdaṃ vājyajinaṃ dadhatsva / asāv aditis te kakṣyāṃ badhnātu vedasyānuvaktavai medhāyai śraddhāyā anūktasyānirākaraṇāya brahmaṇe brahmavarcasāya iti
1.1.2.23	kṛṣṇājinaṃ brāhmaṇasya rauravaṃ rājanyasya bastājinaṃ vaiśyasya
1.1.2.24	athainaṃ paridadāti
1.1.2.25	parīmam indraṃ brahmaṇe mahe śrotrāya dadhmasi / yathainaṃ jarimāṇe yo jyok śrotre adhijāgarat / iti brāhmaṇam
1.1.2.26	parīmamindraṃ brahmaṇe mahe rāṣṭrāya dadhmasi / yathainaṃ jarimāṇe yo jyogrāṣṭre adhijāgarat / iti rājanyam
1.1.2.27	parīmam indraṃ brahmaṇe mahe poṣāya dadhmasi / yathainaṃ jarimāṇe yo jyok poṣe adhijāgarat / iti vaiśyam
1.1.2.28	apareṇāgnim udañcam upaveśyāhutoccheṣaṃ prāśayati
1.1.2.29	tvayi medhāṃ tvayi prajāṃ tvayy agnis tejo dadhātu / ity etaiḥ saṃnaddhaiḥ
1.1.2.30	pṛṣadājyam eke prāśayati
1.1.2.31	yoge yoge tavastaram / imam agna āyuṣe varcase kṛdhi iti prāśnantaṃ samīkṣate
1.1.2.32	prāśayaty eke
1.1.2.33	ācāntam upasparśayitvābhimantrayate / śatam in nu śarado anti devā yatrānaś cakrā jarasam tanūnām / putrāso yatra pitaro bhavanti mā no madhyā rīriṣatāyurgantoḥ / iti
1.1.3.1	āgantrā samaganmahi prasumṛtyuṃ yuyotana / ariṣṭās saṃcaremahi svasti caratād iha svastyā gṛhebhyaḥ iti pradakṣinam agnim parikrāmantam abhimantrayate
1.1.3.2	athainam abhivyāhārayati brahmacaryam āgām upa mā nayasva
1.1.3.3	brahmacārī bhavāni devena savitrā prasūtaḥ iti
1.1.3.4	taṃ pṛcchati ko nāmāsi iti
1.1.3.5	asau ity ācaṣṭe yathānāmā bhavati
1.1.3.6	svasti deva savitar ahaṃ yenāmunā ṛcam adhīya iti nāma nigṛhṇāti
1.1.3.7	śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya āpo bhavantu pītaye śaṃyor abhisravantu naḥ ity adbhir mārjayate
1.1.4.1	athāsya dakṣiṇena hastena dakṣiṇam aṃsam anvārabhya savyena savyaṃ vyāhṛtibhiḥ sāvitryeti dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum adhyāsyann upanayate
1.1.4.2	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ puṣṇo hastābhyām upanaye'sau iti ca
1.1.4.3	athāsya dakṣiṇena hastena dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ sāṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhṇāti
1.1.4.4	agnis te hastam agrahīt / somas te hastam agrahīt / savitā te hastam agrahīt / sarasvatī te hastam agrahīt / pūṣā te hastam agrahīt / bṛhaspatis te hastam agrahīt / mitras te hastam agrahīt / varuṇas te hastam agrahīt / tvaṣṭā te hastam agrahīt / dhātā te hastam agrahīt / viṣṇus te hastam agrahīt / prajāpatis te hastam agrahīt / iti mantrair dakṣiṇena hastena kumārasya dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ sāṅguṣṭhaṃ pratimantraṃ gṛhṇāti
1.1.4.5	savitā tvābhirakṣatu / mitras tvam asi śarmaṇā / agnir ācāryas tava / devena savitrā prasūto bṛhaspater brahmacārī bhavāsau / apo 'śāna samidha ādhehi karma kuru mā divā svāpsīḥ ity enaṃ saṃśāsti
1.1.4.6	athāsya dakṣiṇena hastena dakṣiṇam aṃsam uparyupari anvavamṛśya hṛdayadeśam abhimṛśati mama hṛdayaṃ hṛdayaṃ te astu / mama cittaṃ cittenānvehi / mama vācam ekamanā juṣasva / bṛhaspatis tvā niyunaktu mahyaṃ mām evānusaṃgṛhasva / mayi cittāni santu te / mayi sāmīcyam astu te / mahyaṃ vācaṃ niyacchatāt / iti
1.1.4.7	prāṇānāṃ granthir asi / sa mā visrasa iti nābhideśam
1.1.4.8	bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ suprajāḥ prajayā bhūyāsam / suvīro vīraiḥ suvarcā varcasā supoṣā poṣaiḥ sumedhāḥ medhayā subrahmā brahmacāribhiḥ / ity enam abhimantrya bhūr ṛkṣu tvā agnau pṛthivyāṃ vāci brahmaṇi dade 'sau / bhuvo yajuṣṣu tvā vāyāv antarikṣe prāṇe brahmaṇi dade 'sau / svas sāmasu tvā sūrye divi cakṣuṣi brahmaṇi dade 'sau / viṣṇutas te priyo 'sāny asau / analasya te priyo 'sāny asau / idaṃ vatsyāvaḥ / prāṇa āyuṣi vatsyāvaḥ / prāṇa āyuṣi vasāsau iti ca
1.1.4.9	athāsya dakṣiṇena hastena dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ sāṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhṇāti agnir āyuṣmān iti pañcabhiḥ paryāyaiḥ
1.1.4.10	āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhād iti dakṣiṇe karṇe japitvā
1.1.4.11	āyurdā agna ity uttare
1.1.4.12	agnau pṛthivyāṃ pratitiṣṭha vāyāv antarikṣe sūrye divi yāṁ svastim agnir vāyur ādityaś candramā āpo 'nusaṃcaranti tāṃ svastim anusaṃcarāsau prāṇasya brahmacāryabhūr asau ity ubhayatrānuṣajati
1.1.4.13	medhāṃ ma indro dadhātu medhāṃ devī sarasvatī / medhāṃ me aśvināv ubhāv ādhattāṃ puṣkarasrajau // iti tasya mukhena mukhaṃ saṃnidhāya japati
1.1.4.14	athainaṃ paridadāti kaśakāya tvā paridadāmi / antakāya tvā paridadāmi / aghorāya tvā paridadāmi / yamāya tvā paridadāmi / gadāya tvā paridadāmi / makhāya tvā paridadāmi / vaśinyai tvā paridadāmi / pṛthivyai tvā savaiśvānarāyai paridadāmi / adbhyas tvā paridadāmi / oṣadhībhyas tvā paridadāmi / vanaspatibhyas tvā paridadāmi / viśvebhyas tvā bhūtebhyaḥ paridadāmi / sarvebhyas tvā devebhyaḥ paridadāmi / sarvābhyas tvā devatābhyaḥ paridadāmi
1.1.4.15	atra sāvitrīṃ vācayati yadi purastād upeto bhavati
1.1.4.16	yady anupetas tryahe paryapete
1.1.4.17	sadyaḥ puṣkarasādiḥ
1.1.4.18	apareṇāgnim udagagraṃ kūrcaṃ nidhāya tasmin prāṅmukha upaviśati rāṣṭrabhṛd asy ācāryāsandī mā tvad yoṣam iti
1.1.4.19	ādityāyāñjaliṃ kṛtvā ācāryam upasaṃgṛhya dakṣiṇataḥ kumāra upaviśya adhīhi bhoḥ ity uktvā
1.1.4.20	athāsau sāvitrīṃ bho anubrūhi iti
1.1.4.21	gaṇānāṃ tvā gaṇapatiṃ havāmaha ity enam abhimantrya athāsmai paccho 'gre 'nvāhāthārdharcaśo 'tha saṃtatām
1.1.4.22	bhūḥ tat savitur vareṇyam / bhuvaḥ bhargo devasya dhīmahi / svaḥ dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt / bhūr bhuvaḥ tat savitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi / svaḥ dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt / bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ tat savitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi / dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt iti
1.1.5.1	atha sapta pālāśīḥ samidha ārdrā apracchinnāgrāḥ prādeśamātrā ghṛtāktā abhyādhāpayati
1.1.5.2	agnaye samidham āhārṣaṃ bṛhate jātavedase / yathā tvam agne samidhā samidhyasa evaṃ māṃ medhayā prajñayā prajayā paśubhir brahmavarcasenānnādyena samedhaya svāhā ity ekām
1.1.5.3	agnaye samidhau iti dve
1.1.5.4	agnaye samidha iti catasraḥ
1.1.5.5	atha pariṣiñcati yathā purastād anvamaṃsthāḥ māsāvīḥ iti mantrāntān saṃnamayati
1.1.5.6	atha devatā upatiṣṭhate agne vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmi ity agniṃ vāyo vratapata iti vāyum āditya vratapata ity ādityaṃ vratānāṃ vratapata iti vratapatim
1.1.5.7	atra gurave varaṃ dadāti
1.1.5.8	ud āyuṣā ity utthāpya sūryaiṣa te putras taṃ te paridadāmi iti paridāya tac cakṣur devahitaṃ purastācchukram uccarat / paśyema śaradaś śatam / jīvema śaradaś śatam / nandāma śaradaś śatam / modāma śaradaś śatam / bhavāma śaradaś śatam / śṛṇavāma śaradaś śatam / prabravāma śaradaś śatam / ajītāḥ syāma śaradaś śatam / jyok ca sūryaṃ dṛśe ity ādityam upatiṣṭhate
1.1.5.9	agniṣ ṭa āyuḥ pratarāṃ kṛṇotu / agniṣ ṭe puṣṭiṃ pratarāṃ dadhātu / indro marudbhir iha te dadātu / ādityas te vasubhir ādadhātu / iti daṇḍaṃ pradāyāmatraṃ prayacchati
1.1.5.10	athāha bhikṣācaryaṃ cara iti
1.1.5.11	sa mātaram evāgre bhikṣeta
1.1.5.12	ato 'nyeṣu rātikuleṣv āhṛtya bhaikṣam iti prāha
1.1.5.13	yasya te prathamavāsyaṃ harāmas taṃ tvā viśve avantu devāḥ / taṃ tvā bhrātaraḥ suvṛdho vardhamānam anujāyantāṃ bahavas sujātam iti prathamavāsyamasyādatte
1.1.5.14	upasthite 'nna odanasyāpūpānāṃ saktūnāṃ samavadāya sarpirmiśrasya juhoti
1.1.5.15	agnaye svāhā / somāya svāhā / agnaye 'nnādāya svāhā / agnaye 'nnapataye svāhā / prajāpataye svāhā / viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ svāhā / sarvābhyo devatābhyaḥ svāhā / agnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā iti
1.1.5.16	sarvatraivam anādiṣṭadevatam amuṣmai svāhā amuṣmai svāheti
1.1.5.17	yathādaivatam ādiṣṭadaivatam
1.1.5.18	eteṣām evāsāṃ samavadāya prāgagreṣu darbheṣu baliṃ karoti vāstupataye svāhā iti
1.1.5.19	trivṛtā annena brāhmaṇān pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhiṃ vācayitvā tryahavrataṃ caraty akṣāralavaṇam aśamīdhānyaṃ bhuñjānaḥ adhaśśāyī amṛṇmayapāyī aśūdrocchiṣṭamadhumāṃsāśī adivāsvāpī ubhau kālau bhikṣācaryam udakumbham ity āharann aharahaḥ kāṣṭhakalām
1.1.5.20	ubhau kālau sāyaṃ sāyaṃ vā samidho 'bhyādadhāti
1.1.5.21	yathāha tad vasavo gauryam iti pradakṣiṇam agniṃ parimṛjya pariṣiñcati
1.1.5.22	yathā purastād vyāhṛtībhiḥ samidho 'bhyādadhāti ekaikaśaḥ samastābhiś ca
1.1.5.23	eṣā te agna samit tayā vardhasva cāpyāyasva vardhiṣimahi ca vayam ā ca pyāsiṣīmahi svāhā / medhāṃ ma indro dadhātu medhāṃ devī sarasvatī / medhāṃ me aśvināv ubhāv ādhattāṃ puṣkarasrajau svāhā / apsarāsu ca yā medhā gandharveṣu ca yan manaḥ / daivī medhā manuṣyajā sā māṃ medhā surabhir juṣatāṃ svāhā / ā māṃ medhā surabhir viśvarūpā hiraṇyavarṇā jagatī jagamyā / ūrjasvatī payasā pinvamānā sā māṃ medhā supratīkā juṣantāṃ svāhā iti
1.1.5.24	tathaiva parimṛjya pariṣiñcati yathā purastāt
1.1.5.25	yat te agne teja ity etaiḥ mantraiḥ upatiṣṭhate mayi medhāṃ mayi prajām iti ca
1.1.5.26	tryahe paryapete tathaiva trivṛtānnena brāhmaṇān pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā vrataṃ visṛjate agne vratapate vratam acāriṣam ity etair mantraiḥ
1.1.5.27	etad vratam evāta ūrdhvam ācāryakulavāsy aśnāty akṣāralavaṇam aśamīdhānyam iti
1.1.5.28	daṇḍī jaṭī mekhalī śikhājaṭo vā syāt
1.1.5.29	kāṣāyam ajinaṃ vā vaste na striyam upaity aṣṭācatvāriṃśadvarṣāṇi dvādaśa yāvadgrahaṇaṃ vā na tv evāvrataḥ syāt
1.1.5.30	kāṇḍopākaraṇe kāṇḍavisarge ca sadasaspatim adbhutaṃ priyam indrasya kāmyam
1.1.5.31	saniṃ medhām ayāsiṣaṃ svāhā iti kāṇḍarṣidvitīyam imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvan no agne sa tvan no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
1.1.5.32	athaike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati yathā purastāt
1.2.1.1	śravaṇāpakṣasya oṣadhīṣu jātāsu hastena paurṇamāsyāṃ vādhyāyopākarma
1.2.1.2	agnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā pañca kāṇḍaṛṣīn juhoti prajāpataye kāṇḍaṛṣaye svāhā
1.2.1.3	somāya kāṇḍaṛṣaye svāhā / agnaye kāṇḍaṛṣaye svāhā / viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ kāṇḍaṛṣibhyaḥ svāhā / svayambhuve kāṇḍaṛṣaye svāhā iti
1.2.1.4	kāṇḍanāmāni vā sāvitrīm ṛgvedaṃ yajurvedaṃ sāmavedam atharvavedaṃ sadasaspatim iti hutvā tryaham ekāhaṃ vā kṣamya yathādhyāyam adhyetavyam iti vadanti
1.2.1.5	athātaḥ kāṇḍāny ucyante pauroḍāśikaṃ yājamānaṃ hotāraṃ hautraṃ pitṛmedham iti sabrāhmaṇāni sānubrāhmaṇāni prājāpatyāni
1.2.1.6	ādhvaryavaṃ grahadākṣiṇāni samiṣṭayajūṃṣi avabhṛthayajūṃṣi vājapeyaśśukriyāṇi savā iti sabrāhmaṇāni sānubrāhmaṇāni saumyāni
1.2.1.7	āgnyādheyaṃ punarādheyam agnihotram agnyupasthānaṃ sāvitraṃ nāciketaṃ cāturhotrīyaṃ vaiśvasṛjam āruṇaketukam āgnikam iti sabrāhmaṇāni sānubrāhmaṇāny āgneyāni
1.2.1.8	rājasūyaṃ paśubandhā iṣṭayo nakṣatreṣṭayo vā divaśśyenayo 'pāghāḥ sātrāyaṇa upahomāḥ sūktāny aupānuvākyāyājyāśvamedhapuruṣamedhasautrāmaṇyacchidrāṇi paśuhautram upaniṣada iti sabrāhmaṇāni sānubrāhmaṇāni vaiśvadevāni
1.2.1.9	svāyaṃbhuvaṃ svāṅkāṅke paṭhito vidhir iti svayaṃbhūś cātra daivataṃ sarvabhūtapatir iti
1.2.1.10	atha kārīrivrataṃ catūrātram akṣāralavaṇam aśamīdhānyaṃ bhūmau bhuñjīta paśuvad iti
1.2.1.11	atha kārīrirṇāṃ mārutaṃ devā vasavyā agne mārutam iti devāś śarmaṇyā ityādyauṣadhyanuvākam adhīyāno nātra bhuñjīta paśuvad iti
1.2.1.12	atha kārīrāvratam yuñjānaḥ prathamam ārabhya auṣadhyanuvākaṃ prathamam adhīyāno nātra bhūmau bhuñjīta paśuvad iti yadi vā kramam adhīyānaḥ
1.2.2.1	taiṣīpakṣasya rohiṇyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ votsargaḥ
1.2.2.2	sagaṇāḥ prācīm udīcīṃ vā diśam upaniṣkramya yatrāpaḥ sukhāḥ sukhāvagāhās tad avagāhyāghamarṣaṇena trīn prāṇāyāmān dhārayitvā sapavitraiḥ pāṇibhiḥ āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena mārjayante
1.2.2.3	snātvā darbhān anyonyasmai samprayacchanto ditsanta ivānyonyam
1.2.2.4	tataḥ śucau same deśe prācīnapravaṇe prāgagrair darbhair udagapavargāṇy āsanāni kalpayanti
1.2.2.5	brahmaṇe prajāpataye 'gnaye vāyave somāya sūryāya candramase nakṣatrebhya indrāya rājñe yamāya rājñe varuṇāya rājñe somāya rājñe vaiśravaṇāya rājñe vasubhyo rudrebhya ādityebhyo viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ sādhyebhyo ṛbhubhyo bhṛgubhyo marudbhyo 'tharvabhyo 'ṅgirobhya iti devagaṇānām
1.2.2.6	viśvāmitro jamadagnir bharadvājo gautamo 'trir vasiṣṭhaḥ kāśyapa ity ete sapta ṛṣayaḥ
1.2.2.7	nivītina uttarata udīcīnapravaṇa udagagrair darbhaiḥ prāgapavargāṇy āsanāni kalpayanti viśvāmitrāya jamadagnaye bharadvājāya gautamāyātraye vasiṣṭhāya kāśyapāya
1.2.2.8	vasiṣṭhakāśyapayor antarāle arundhatyai kalpayanti
1.2.2.9	dakṣiṇata ekavedyante agastyāya kalpayanti
1.2.2.10	uttarataḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāya jatukarṇāya tarukṣāya tṛṇabindave varmiṇe varūthine vājine śravase satraśravase suśravase stutaśravase somaśuṣmāyaṇāya sanatvānāya bṛhadukthāya vāmadevāya vājarājñāya haritarājñāya udamāyāya gautamāya ṛṇaṃjayāya ṛtaṃjayāya kṛtaṃjayāya dhanaṃjayāya satyaṃjayāya babhrave trivarṇāya trivarṣāya tridhātave parāśarāya viṣṇave rudrāya skandāya kāśīśvarāya jarāya dharmāya arthāya kāmāya krodhāya vasiṣṭhāya indrāya tvaṣṭre kartre dhartre dhātre vidhātre mṛtyave savitre sāvitryai ṛgvedāya yajurvedāya sāmavedāyātharvavedāyetihāsapurāṇebhya iti
1.2.2.11	dakṣiṇataḥ prācīnāvītino dakṣiṇāpravaṇe dakṣiṇāgrair darbhaiḥ pratyagapavargāṇy āsanāni kalpayanti
1.2.2.12	vaiśampāyanāya phaliṅgave tittirāyokhyāya ātreyāya padakārāya kauṇḍinyāya vṛttikārāya sūtrakārebhyaḥ satyāṣāḍhāya pravacanakartṛbhya ācāryebhyo ṛṣibhyo vānaprasthebhya ūrdhvaretobhya ekapatnībhya iti
1.2.2.13	svaṃ svaṃ pitṛbhyaḥ pitāmahebhyaḥ mātṛbhyaḥ pitāmahībhyaḥ prapitāmahībhyaḥ mātāmahebhyo mātuḥ pitāmahebhyo mātuḥ prapitāmahebhyo mātāmahībhyo mātuḥ pitāmahībhyo mātuḥ prapitāmahībhyaḥ kalpayāmy amuṃ kalpayāmy amuṃ kalpayāmīty āsanena amuṃ tarpayāmi amuṃ tarpayāmīty udakena amuṣmai namo 'muṣmai nama iti gandhapuṣpadhūpadīpaiḥ amuṣmai svāhā amuṣmai svāhety annena amuṃ tarpayāmy amuṃ tarpayāmy amuṃ tarpayāmīti phalodakenāmuṣmai namo 'muṣmai namo 'muṣmai nama ity upasthāyāpareṇa vediṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ kalpayitvāgnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā pañca kāṇḍaṛṣīn juhoti
1.2.2.14	kāṇḍanāmāni vā sāvitrīm ṛgvedaṃ yajurvedaṃ sāmavedam atharvavedaṃ sadasaspatim iti hutvā prathamottamānuvākāv adhīte kāṇḍādīn vā sarvān
1.2.2.15	jayādi pratipadyate
1.2.2.16	sviṣṭakṛdantaṃ hutvā tryaham ekāhaṃ vā kṣamya yathādhyāyam adhyetavyam iti vadanti
1.2.2.17	kāṇḍātkāṇḍāt prarohantī iti dvābhyām udakānte dūrvāṃ ropayet
1.2.2.18	udadhim ūrmimantaṃ kṛtvā prācīm udīcīṃ vā diśam ātamitor ājiṃ dhāvanti
1.2.2.19	pratyetyāpūpaiḥ saktubhir odanena brāhmaṇāṃś ca tarpayanti
1.2.2.20	evaṃ pārāyaṇasamāptau kāṇḍādidūrvāropaṇāntam udadhidhāvanavarjaṃ nityam evādbhir devānṛṣīn pitṝṃś ca tarpayanti tarpayanti
1.2.3.1	athāto 'vāntaradīkṣāṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
1.2.3.2	udagayanāpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre keśān vāpayitvā snātvāśitvā agnim audumbarīś catasraḥ samidho 'hataṃ vāso darbhān ājyaṃ ca udakumbham ity etān samādāya bahir grāmād uttarāṃ diśam upaniṣkramyāchadirdarśe 'gnim upasamādhāya paristīrya madantīr adhiśritya pūrvāṃ śāntiṃ kṛtvātha pariṣicyābhyajya samidho 'bhyādadhāti pṛthivī samit ity etābhiś catasṛbhiḥ
1.2.3.3	atha pariṣicya agne vratapate śukriyebhyo vrataṃ cariṣyāmi iti devatā upasthāpyāhatena vāsasā śiraḥ samukham abhiveṣṭayati citaḥ stha paricitaḥ pari tvā girvaṇo gira imā bhavantu viśvataḥ
1.2.3.4	vṛddhāyum anuvṛddhayo juṣṭā bhavantu juṣṭayaḥ
1.2.3.5	indrasya syūr asi indrasya dhruvam asi aindramasi indrāya tvā ity uttarāṃ śāntiṃ kṛtvā vāco yamya grāmaṃ praviśati
1.2.3.6	tiṣṭhann āsīno vā jāgaraṇam
1.2.3.7	atha śvobhūte etām eva diśam upaniṣkramyāchadirdarśe 'gnim upasamādhāya paristīrya madantīr adhiśritya pūrvāṃ śāntiṃ kṛtvā vayaḥ suparṇā iti visṛjya vāsa ādityam upatiṣṭhate ud vayaṃ tamasas pari ud u tyaṃ citraṃ tac cakṣur devahitaṃ ya udagād iti
1.2.3.8	etān anuvīkṣayanty agnim ādityam aśmānam udakumbhaṃ hiraṇyaṃ gāṃ bhūmim iti
1.2.3.9	uttarāṃ śāntiṃ kṛtvā saṃvatsaraṃ vrataṃ carati dvādaśarātram ekāhaṃ vā
1.2.3.10	aṣṭamyāṃ parvaṇi kālasnānam
1.2.3.11	atha yady amedhyaṃ paśyed abaddhaṃ mano daridram iti atha yady abhivarṣeyuḥ undatīr balaṃ dhatta iti japati
1.2.3.12	adhaśśayyā guruśuśrūṣā
1.2.3.13	śukriyāṇy adhīyīta
1.2.3.14	etām eva diśam upaniṣkramyāchadirdarśe 'gnim upasamādhāya paristīrya madantīr adhiśritya pūrvāṃ śāntiṃ kṛtvā dyauḥ samid ity etābhiś catasṛbhiḥ audumbarīḥ samidha ādhāyātha pariṣicya āditya vratapate śukriyebhyo vratam acāriṣam ity etābhir devatā upasthāya gurave gāṃ dadāti
1.2.3.15	uttarāṃ śāntiṃ kṛtvā vratasamāpto bhavati
1.3.1.1	vedam adhītya snāsyann upakalpayate erakāṃ copabarhaṇaṃ ca nāpitaṃ ca kṣuraṃ ca pālāśīṃ ca samidhaṃ dārūṇi copastaraṇaṃ vṛkalāṃś ca dantadhāvanaṃ ca śītāś coṣṇāś cāpaḥ sarvasurabhipiṣṭaṃ candanaṃ cāhataṃ vāsaḥ sāntaraṃ ca prāvāraṃ bādaramaṇiṃ svarṇopahitaṃ sūtram ca pravartau cājyaṃ ca darvī ca mālāṃ cādarśaṃ cāñjanaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ ca chatraṃ copānahau cānaḍuhaṃ carma sarvalohitam ity ete 'sya sambhārā upakḷptā bhavanti
1.3.1.2	snānasya mīmāṃsā
1.3.1.3	rohiṇyāṃ snāyād ity ekam
1.3.1.4	prājāpatyaṃ vā etan nakṣatraṃ tad asya prājāpatye eva nakṣatre snātaṃ bhavati atho sarvān rohān rohati iti
1.3.1.5	tiṣye snāyād ity ekam
1.3.1.6	bārhaspatyaṃ vā etan nakṣatraṃ tad asya bārhaspatya eva nakṣatre snātaṃ bhavati atho bṛhaspatiprasūto 'sāni iti
1.3.1.7	uttarayoḥ phalgunyoḥ snāyād ity ekam
1.3.1.8	bhagasya vā etan nakṣatraṃ tad asya bhagya eva nakṣatre snātaṃ bhavati atho bhagyo 'sāni iti
1.3.1.9	haste snāyād ity ekam
1.3.1.10	sāvitraṃ vā etan nakṣatraṃ tad asya sāvitra eva nakṣatre snātaṃ bhavati atho savitṛprasūto 'sāni iti
1.3.1.11	citrāyāṃ snāyād ity ekam
1.3.1.12	aindraṃ vā etan nakṣatraṃ tad asyaindra eva nakṣatre snātaṃ bhavati atho citro 'sāni iti
1.3.1.13	viśākhāyoḥ snāyād ity ekam
1.3.1.14	aindrāgnaṃ vā etan nakṣatraṃ tad asyaindrāgna eva nakṣatre snātaṃ bhavati atho viśākho 'sānīti prajayā paśubhiḥ iti
1.3.1.15	eteṣām ekatamasmin nakṣatre
1.3.2.1	purādityasyodayād vrajaṃ prapadyeta
1.3.2.2	nainam etad ahar ādityo 'bhitapet
1.3.2.3	tad ahaḥ snātānāṃ mukhaṃ vā etat tejasā yaśasā tapati
1.3.2.4	antarlomnā carmaṇā vrajam abhinighnate tam
1.3.2.5	pūrvārdhe vrajasyāgnim upasamādhāya athāhared etān sambhārān sakṛd eva sarvān yat saha sarvāṇi mānuṣāṇi ity etatasmād brāhmaṇāt
1.3.2.6	paristīryottarataḥ pālāśīṃ samidham upasādya dakṣiṇato nāpitas tiṣṭhati
1.3.2.7	āmadhyandinaṃ bhikṣāṃ dadyāt
1.3.2.8	apīha gāṃ paced vaśā cet syād atraitām
1.3.2.9	pālāśīṃ samidham ājyenāktvā madhyandine 'bhyādadhāti imaṃ stomam arhate jātavedase ratham iva saṃmahemā manīṣayā
1.3.2.10	bhadrā hi naḥ pramatir asya saṃsady agne sakhye mā riṣāmā vayaṃ tava svāhā iti athāpareṇāgnim udīcīpratiṣevaṇām erakām āstṛṇāti
1.3.2.11	tasyām udīcīnaśirā nipadyate tryāyuṣaṃ kaśyapasyāgastyasya tryāyuṣaṃ jamadagnes tryāyuṣaṃ yad devānāṃ tryāyuṣaṃ tan me astu tryāyuṣam iti
1.3.2.12	udyamānam anumantrayate śivā me bhava śaṅkarā iti
1.3.2.13	kṣuram anumantrayate kṣuro nāmāsi svadhitis te pitā namas te astu mā mā hiṃsīḥ iti upyamānam anumantrayate yat kṣureṇa vṛścayasi vaptā vapasi keśaśmaśru varcayā me mukhaṃ mā ma āyuḥ pramoṣīḥ iti
1.3.2.14	śmaśrūṇy agre vaptvāthopapakṣāv atha keśān yathopapādam aṅgāni
1.3.2.15	taddhyeṣā jarasā pūrvā āyuṣe prayānti
1.3.2.16	pūrvāyuṣe 'nnādā bhavanti
1.3.2.17	yasmād evaṃ vidvāṃso lomāni vapante tasmān nu hety u vidvān kāmam eva lomāni vāpayet
1.3.2.18	kāmaṃ nu nakhāni nikṛtya lomāni vāpayet
1.3.2.19	sa yadi lomāni vāpayiṣyamāṇo bhavati tāni brahmacāriṇe prayacchann āha imāni prācīṃ hṛtvā goṣṭhe vā darbhastambe vā nidhattād iti
1.3.2.20	tāni sa nidadhāti
1.3.3.1	athāpareṇāgniṃ prāg upaviśya mekhalāṃ visraṃsayati imaṃ viṣyāmi varunasya pāśam iti
1.3.3.2	sa yas tatra rātiḥ syāt tasmai prayacchann āha imāṃ prācīṃ hṛtvā nyagrodhe vaudumbare vā nidhattād iti
1.3.3.3	tām u sa tatra nidadhāti idam aham amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasya pāpmānam apagūhāmy uttarasya dviṣadbhya iti
1.3.3.4	vṛkalaiḥ pradhāvya dantān pradhāvate
1.3.3.5	annādyāya vyūhadhvaṃ bhago rājā yam āgamat / sa me mukhaṃ prasarpatu āyuṣe ca bhagāya ca iti
1.3.3.6	athobhayīr apaḥ saṃniṣiñcati uṣṇāsu śītā ānayati devamānuṣasya vyāvṛttyā iti
1.3.3.7	tāsām añjalinā trir abhiṣiñcati āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ ṣoḍhā vihito vai puruṣa ity etasmād brāhmaṇāt
1.3.3.8	nidhāya etad vāsaḥ svā mā tanūr āviśa iti sāntaraṃ vāsaḥ paridhatte
1.3.3.9	athaitasya sarvasurabhipiṣṭaṃ samudāyutyāñjalinā triḥ pariṣiñcati namaḥ śākajañjabhābhyāṃ namas tābhyo devatābhyo vā abhigrāhiṇīḥ iti
1.3.3.10	evaṃ candanasya
1.3.3.11	evam evāta ūrdhvaṃ nidhāya etad vāsaḥ svā mā tanūr āviśa ity ahataṃ vāsaḥ paridhatte
1.3.3.12	evam āsaṅgyam evamuṣṇīṣam evam evāta ūrdhvam
1.3.3.13	athainaṃ bādaramaṇiṃ suvarṇopahitaṃ sūtre protya darvyām ādāya darvīdaṇḍasūtreṇa paryasya juhoti
1.3.4.1	iyam oṣadhe trāyamāṇā sahamānā sahasvatī / sā mā pitur iva nāmāgrahaṃ sā mā karotu somavarcasaṃ karotu sūryavarcasaṃ brahmavarcasinam annādaṃ karotu svāhā iti
1.3.4.2	athainam udapātre pariplāvayati viśvā uta tvayā vayam iti
1.3.4.3	apāśo 'si ity uktvākṣṇayā pariharati
1.3.4.4	vadhyaṃ hi pratyañcaṃ pratimuñcanti vyāvṛttyai ity etasmād brāhmaṇāt
1.3.4.5	athaitau pravartau sūtre protya darvyām ādhāya darvīdaṇḍe sūtreṇa paryasya juhoti āyuṣyaṃ varcasyaṃ rāyaspoṣam udbhidam / idaṃ hiraṇyaṃ varcase jaitryāyāviśatād imaṃ rayiṃ svāhā iti
1.3.4.6	dvitīyāṃ juhoti śunam ivāhaṃ hiraṇyasya pitur iva nāmāgraham / taṃ mā karotu somavarcasaṃ karotu sūryavarcasaṃ brahmavarcasinam annādaṃ karotu svāhā iti
1.3.4.7	tṛtīyāṃ juhoti uccairvāji pṛtanāsāhaṃ sabhāsāhaṃ dhanañjayam / sarvāḥ samṛddhīr ṛddhaya hiraṇye yāḥ samāhitāḥ svāhā iti
1.3.4.8	caturthīṃ juhoti virājaṃ ca svarājaṃ ca abhiśrīr yā ca no gṛhe / śrī rāṣṭrasya yā mukhe tayā mā saṃsṛja svāhā iti
1.3.4.9	pañcamīṃ juhoti yaśo mā kuru brāhmaṇeṣu yaśo rājasu mā kuru / yaśo viśyeṣu śūdreṣv aham asmi yaśastapāḥ svāhā iti
1.3.4.10	athaināv udapātre pariplāvayati viśvā uta tvayā vayam iti
1.3.4.11	apāśo 'si ity uktvānyataraṃ pravartaṃ prakṣālya dakṣiṇe karṇe āmūhati
1.3.5.1	āyuṣyaṃ varcasyam ity etābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ sahānukaroti ṛtubhis tvārtavaiḥ saṃvatsarasya dhāyasā tais tvā sahānukaromi iti
1.3.5.2	evam evottaram
1.3.5.3	apāśo 'si ity uktvākṣṇayaiva srajaṃ pariharati śubhike śira āroha śobhayantī mukhaṃ mama / mukhaṃ hi mama śobhaya bhūyāṃsaṃ ca bhagaṃ kuru / yāṃ me jahāra jamadagniḥ śraddhāyai rāgāyānyai / imāṃ tāṃ pratimuñce 'ham āyuṣe ca bhagāya ca iti
1.3.5.4	ādarśe samavekṣate yan me manaḥ parāgatam ātmānam ādarśe paripaśyati / idaṃ tat punar ādade 'ham āyuṣe ca bhagāya ca iti
1.3.5.5	athāñjanenāṅkte yadāñjanaṃ traikakudaṃ jātaṃ himavata upari / tena māṃ cāyuṣyaṃ varcasyaṃ me astu iti
1.3.5.6	daṇḍam ādatte sakhā me gopāya iti
1.3.5.7	chatram ādatte dyaur asi suparṇo 'ntarikṣān mā gopāya iti
1.3.5.8	athopānahāv upamuñcate dyaur asi iti dakṣiṇāṃ pṛthivy asi ity uttarām
1.3.5.9	diśam upaniṣkramya diśam upatiṣṭhate devīṣ ṣaḍ urvīr uru ṇaḥ kṛṇota viśve devāsa iha vīrayadhvam iti
1.3.5.10	mā hāsmahi prajayā mā tanūbhir mā radhāma dviṣate soma rājan iti candramasam upasthāyaiva diśo yatra kāmayate tad eti
1.4.1	itarat samāvartanam
1.4.2	athetarat tūṣṇīm eva tīrthe snātvodeti
1.4.3	athāsmāyāryopaveśanam āhāryodakam āhārayati
1.4.4	tat pratīkṣate ā mā gāt tejasā varcasā yaśasā saṃsṛja payasā ca iti
1.4.5	tad upaspṛśya prāk sektavā ity āha
1.4.6	tasmād anyad āhārayati
1.4.7	tenāsya pādau prakṣālyāthāsmai madhv āhārayati
1.4.8	tat pratīkṣate
1.4.9	yan madhuno madhavyaṃ priyaṃ paramam annādo rūpaṃ tenāhaṃ madhuno madhavyena priyeṇa pareṇānnādo 'sāni iti pratigṛhṇāti
1.4.10	priyaḥ prajānām adhipatiḥ paśūnām iti brāhmaṇam priyaḥ paśūnām adhipatiḥ prajānām iti rājanyam
1.4.11	tad aśnāti brahma tvāśnātu brahma tvāśnātu iti
1.4.12	athāsmai dadhy āhārayati
1.4.13	tad aśnāti brahma tvāśnātu brahma tvāśnātu iti
1.4.14	asmā odanam āhārayati
1.4.15	tad aśnāti brahma tvāśnātu brahma tvāśnātu iti
1.4.16	athāsmai mantham āhārayati
1.4.17	tad aśnāti brahma tvāśnātu brahma tvāśnātu iti
1.4.18	athāsmai gām upākaroti tām udvāsṛjata kuruteti vā
1.4.19	athāsmai tad ahaṃ putro vā bhrātaro vāntevāsī vopanayeteyaṃ vā saiva sahate
1.4.20	yadi vā rathaṃ labhate rathantaram asi iti dakṣiṇaṃ cakram abhimṛśati bṛhad asi ity uttaraṃ vāmadevyam asi iti madhyamam
1.4.21	āruhya pravartamānam anumantrayate ayaṃ vām aśvinā ratho mā duḥkhe mā sukhe riṣad iti
1.4.22	sa yadi śabdaṃ kuryāt pratibudhya yajñopavītaṃ kṛtvā apa ācamya bhūmim abhimṛśati mayi dhṛtiṃ mayi vidhṛtiṃ mayi svadhṛtiṃ mayi rantiṃ mayi ramatiṃ mayi puṣṭiṃ puṣṭipatirdadhātu iti
1.5.1.1	anṛkṣarā ṛjavaḥ santu panthā yebhiḥ sakhāyo yanti no vareṇyam / sam aryamā saṃ bhago no ninīyāt sañjāspatyaṃ suyamam astu devāḥ / ayaṃ kūrcaḥ
1.5.1.2	mayi gṛhṇāmy agre agniṃ rāyaspoṣāya suprajāstvāya suvīryāya / mayi prajāṃ mayi varco dadhāmy ariṣṭāḥ syāma tanuvā suvīrāḥ / yo no agniḥ pitaro hṛtsv antar amartyo martyāṁ āviveśa / tam ātman parigṛhṇīmahe vayaṃ mā so asmāṁ avahāya parāgāt
1.5.1.3	bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ / prajāpatiḥ striyāṃ yaśo muṣkayor adadhāt sapam / kāmasya tṛptim ānandaṃ tasyāgne bhājayeha mā / modaḥ pramoda ānando muṣkayor nihitaḥ sapaḥ / sṛtveva kāmasya tṛpyāṇi dakṣiṇānāṃ pratigrahe / manasaś cittam ākūtiṃ vācaḥ satyam aśīmahi / paśūnāṃ rūpam annasya yaśaḥ śrīḥ śrayatāṃ mayi / yathāham asyā atṛpaṃ striyai pumān yathā strī tṛpyati puṃsi priye priyā / evaṃ bhagasya tṛpyāṇi yajñasya kāmyaḥ priyām / dadāmīty agnir vadati / tatheti vāyur āha tat / hanteti satyaṃ candramāḥ / ādityaḥ satyam om iti / āpas tat satyam ābharan / yaśo yajñasya dakṣiṇām / asau me kāmaḥ samṛdhyatām
1.5.1.4	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjanaḥ ity etenānuvākena
1.5.1.5	yā akṛntann avayan yā atanvata yāś ca devīr antān abhito 'dadanta / tās tvā devīr jarasā saṃdhyayantv āyuṣmatīdaṃ paridhatsva vāsaḥ / paridhatta dhatta vāsasaināṃ śatāyuṣīṃ kṛṇuta dīrgham āyuḥ / bṛhaspatiḥ prāyacchad vāsa etat somāya rājñe paridhātavā u / jarāṃ gacchāsi paridhatsva vāso bhavā kṛṣṭīnām abhiśastipāvatī / śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ suvarcā rāyaś ca poṣam upasaṃvyayasva / parīdaṃ vāso adhidhāḥ svastaye 'bhūr āpīnām abhiśastipāvatī / śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcīr vasūni cāryo vibhajāsu jīvatī
1.5.1.6	anayā saha mayā karmāṇi kartavyāni
1.5.1.7	prajāś cotpādayitavyāḥ
1.5.1.8	tadartham enāṃ pariṇeṣye
1.5.1.9	indrāya namaḥ / agnaye namaḥ / yamāya namaḥ / nirṛtaye namaḥ / varuṇāya namaḥ / vāyave namaḥ / somāya namaḥ / īśānāya namaḥ / brahmaṇe namaḥ / adbhyo namaḥ / agnaye namaḥ / ātmane namaḥ
1.5.1.10	adite 'numanyasva / anumate 'numanyasva / sarasvate 'numanyasva / deva savitaḥ prasuva
1.5.1.11	ayaṃ ta idhma ātmā jātavedas tenedhyasva vardhasva ceddha vardhaya cāsmān prajayā paśubhir brahmavarcasenānnādyena samedhaya svāhā / prajāpataye svāhā / indrāya svāhā / agnaye svāhā / somāya svāhā / bhūḥ svāhā / bhuvaḥ svāhā / svaḥ svāhā / bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā
1.5.1.12	yā tiraścī nipadyase 'haṃ vidharaṇī iti / tāṃ tvā ghṛtasya dhārayā juhomi vaiśvakarmaṇi svāhā / yānūcī nipadyase 'haṃ vidharaṇī iti / tāṃ tvā ghṛtasya dhārayā agnau saṃrādhanyai devyai svāhā / prasādhanyai devyai svāhā
1.5.2.1	yukto vaha jātavedaḥ purastād agne viddhi karma kriyamāṇaṃ yathedam / tvaṃ bhiṣag bheṣajasyāsi kartā tvayā gā aśvān puruṣān sanemi svāhā / virūpākṣāya svāhā / dantān yaje svāhā / virūpākṣam ahaṃ yaje nijaṅghaṃ śabalodaram / yo māyaṃ paribādhate śriyai puṣṭyai ca tasmai svāhā / paribādha mā vibādhiṣṭhā mā vibādha vibādhithāḥ / nirṛtyai tvā putram āhuḥ sa naḥ karmāṇi sādhaya svāhā / sadasaspatim adbhutaṃ priyam indrasya kāmyam / saniṃ medhām ayāsiṣaṃ svāhā / yāvanto devās tvayi jātavedaḥ striyaṃ codghnanti puruṣasya karma / tebhya etaddhūyate bhāgadheyaṃ te mā tṛptās tarpayantu kāmaiḥ svāhā / ākūtyai tvā kāmāya tvā samṛdhe tvā / puro dadhe amṛtatvāya jīvase svāhā / ākūtim asyāvase / kāmam asya samṛddhyai / indrasya yuñjate dhiyaḥ svāhā / ākūtiṃ devīṃ manasaḥ puro dadhe / yajñasya mātā suhavā me astu / yad icchāmi manasā sa kāmaḥ / videyam enaddhṛdaye niviṣṭaṃ svāhā
1.5.2.2	iṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā / vaṣaḍaniṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā / bheṣajaṃ duriṣṭyai svāhā / niṣkṛtyai svāhā / daurādhyai svāhā / devībhyas tanūbhyaḥ svāhā / ṛddhyai svāhā / samṛddhyai svāhā
1.5.2.3	cittāya svāhā / cittaye svāhā / ākūtāya svāhā / ākūtyai svāhā / vijñātāya svāhā / vijñānāya svāhā / manase svāhā / śakvarībhyaḥ svāhā / darśāya svāhā / pūrṇamāsāya svāhā / bṛhate svāhā / rathantarāya svāhā / prajāpatir jayān indrāya vṛṣṇe prāyacchad ugraḥ pṛtanājyeṣu / tasmai viśaḥ samanamanta sarvāḥ sa ugraḥ sa hi havyo babhūva svāhā
1.5.2.4	agnir bhūtānām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / pitaraḥ pitāmahāḥ indro jyeṣṭhānām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / yamaḥ pṛthivyā adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / vāyur antarikṣasyādhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / sūryo divo 'dhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / candramā nakṣatrāṇām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / bṛhaspatir brahmaṇo 'dhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / mitraḥ satyānām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / varuṇo 'pām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / samudraḥ srotyānām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / annaṃ sāmrājyānām adhipati tan māvatu svāhā / soma oṣadhīnām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / savitā prasavānām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / rudraḥ paśūnām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / tvaṣṭā rūpāṇām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / viṣṇuḥ parvatānām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā / maruto gaṇānām adhipatayas te māvantu svāhā / pitaraḥ pitāmahāḥ pare 'vare tatās tatāmahā iha māvata / asmin brahmann asmin kṣatre 'syām āśiṣy asyāṃ purodhāyām asmin karmann asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā
1.5.2.5	ṛtāṣāḍ ṛtadhāmāgnir gandharvas tasyauṣadhayo 'pasarasa ūrjo nāma sa idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pātu tā idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pāntu tasmai svāhā / tābhyaḥ svāhā / saṃhito viśvasāmā sūryo gandharvas tasya marīcayo 'psarasa āyuvo nāma sa idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pātu tā idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pāntu tasmai svāhā / tābhyaḥ svāhā / suṣumnaḥ sūryaraśmiś candramā gandharvas tasya nakṣatrāṇy apsaraso bekurayo nāma sa idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pātu tā idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pāntu tasmai svāhā / tābhyaḥ svāhā / bhujyuḥ suparṇo yajño gandharvas tasya dakṣiṇā apsarasaḥ stavā nāma sa idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pātu tā idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pāntu tasmai svāhā / tābhyaḥ svāhā / prajāpatir viśvakarmā mano gandharvas tasyarksāmāny apsaraso bahvayo nāma sa idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pātu tā idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pāntu tasmai svāhā / tābhyaḥ svāhā / iṣiro viśvavyacā vāto gandharvas tasyāpo 'psaraso mudā nāma sa idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pātu tā idaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ pāntu tasmai svāhā / tābhyaḥ svāhā
1.5.2.6	agnir etu prathamo devatānāṃ so 'syai prajāṃ muñcatu mṛtyupāśāt / tad ayaṁ rājā varuṇo 'numanyatāṃ yatheyaṃ strī pautram aghaṃ na rodāt svāhā / imām agnis trāyatāṃ gārhapatyaḥ prajām asyai nayatu dīrgham āyuḥ / aśūnyopasthā jīvatām astu mātā pautram ānandam abhiprabuddhyatām iyaṃ svāhā / mā te gṛhe niśi ghoṣa utthād anyatra tvadrudatyaḥ saṃviśantu / mā tvaṃ vikeśy ura āvadhiṣṭhā jīvapatnī patiloke virāja paśyantī prajāṃ saumanasyamānāṃ svāhā
1.5.3.1	stanandhayataste putrān savitābhirakṣatu / ā vāsasaḥ paridhānād bṛhaspatir viśvedevā abhirakṣantu paścāt svāhā / aprajastāṃ pautramṛtyuṃ pāpmānam uta vāgham / śīrṣṇaḥ srajam ivonmucya dviṣadbhyaḥ pratimuñcāmi pāśaṃ svāhā / brāhmaṇaṃ devakṛtaṃ kalpamānaṃ tena hanye niṣadaḥ piśācāt / kravyādo mṛtyur adharān pātayāmi dīrgham āyus tava jīvantu putrān svāhā
1.5.3.2	śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya āpo bhavantu pītaye śaṃyor abhisravantu naḥ / devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyām / hastena hastaṃ gṛbhṇāmi saubhagatvāya mayā patyā jaradaṣṭir yathāsat
1.5.3.3	bhago aryamā savitā purandhis te tvā devā adur mahyaṃ patnīm / aghoracakṣur apatighny edhi śivā paśubhyaḥ sumanāḥ suvarcāḥ / yāṃ pūṣan śivatamām erayasva yasyāṃ bījaṃ manuṣyā vapanti / yā na ūrū uśatī visrayātai yasyām uśantaḥ praharema śepham / somo 'dadād gandharvāya gandharvo 'gnaye 'dadāt / paśūṃś ca mahyaṃ putrāṃś ca dadātv agnir atho tvā asāv aham / somaḥ prathamo vivide gandharvo vivida uttaraḥ / tṛtīyo agniṣ ṭe patis turyo 'haṃ manuṣyajāḥ / sarasvati predam ava subhage vājinīvati / tāṃ tvā viśvasya bhūtasya pragāyāmasyagrataḥ / ātiṣṭhemam aśmānam aśmeva tvaṃ sthirā bhava / pramṛṇīhi durasyūn sahasva pṛtanāyataḥ / viśvā uta tvayā vayaṃ dhārā udanyā iva / atigāhemahi dviṣaḥ
1.5.4.1	imān lājān āvapāmi samṛddhikaraṇān mama / mama tubhyaṃ ca saṃvananaṃ tad agnir anumanyatām / bhagena tvā saṃsṛjāmi māsarena surām iva / iyaṃ nāry upabrūte agnau lājān āvapantī / dīrghāyur astu me patir edhantāṃ jñātayo mama svāhā / imaṃ me varuṇa śrudhī havam adyā ca mṛḍaya / tvām avasyur ācake svāhā / tat tvā yāmi brahmaṇā vandamānas tad āśāste yajamāno havirbhiḥ / aheḍamāno varuṇeha bodhy uruśaṃsa mā na āyuḥ pramoṣīḥ svāhā
1.5.4.2	tvaṃ no agne varuṇasya vidvān devasya heḍo 'vayāsisīṣṭhāḥ / yajiṣṭho vahnitamaḥ śośucāno viśvā dveṣāṃsi pramumugdhy asmat svāhā / sa tvaṃ no agne 'vamo bhavotī nediṣṭho asyā uṣaso vyuṣṭau / avayakṣva no varuṇaṃ rarāṇo vīhi mṛḍīkaṃ suhavo na edhi svāhā / tvam agne ayāsyayāsanmanasā hitaḥ / ayāsan havyam ūhiṣe 'yāno dhehi bheṣajaṃ svāhā / prajāpate na tvad etāny anyo viśvā jātāni pari tā babhūva / yatkāmās te juhumas tan no astu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇāṃ svāhā / yan ma ātmano mindābhūd agnis tat punarāhārjātavedā vicarṣaṇiḥ svāhā / punar agniś cakṣur adāt punar indro bṛhaspatiḥ / punar me aśvinā yuvaṃ cakṣur ādhattam akṣyoḥ svāhā / anājñātaṃ yad ājñātaṃ yajñasya kriyate madhu / agne tad asya kalpaya tvaṃ hi vettha yathātathaṃ svāhā / puruṣasammito yajño yajñaḥ puruṣasammitaḥ / agne tad asya kalpaya tvaṃ hi vettha yathātathaṃ svāhā / yat pākatrā manasā dīnadakṣāna yajñasya manvate martāsaḥ / agniṣ ṭaddhotā kratuvid vijānan yajiṣṭho devāṁ kratuśo yajāti svāhā
1.5.4.3	pāhi no agna enase svāhā / pāhi no viśvavedase svāhā / yajñaṃ pāhi vibhāvaso svāhā / sarvaṃ pāhi śatakrato svāhā / bhūr agnaye ca pṛthivyai ca mahate ca svāhā / bhuvo vāyave cāntarikṣāya ca mahate ca svāhā / suvar ādityāya ca dive ca mahate ca svāhā / bhūr bhuvaḥ svaś candramase ca nakṣatrebhyaś ca digbhyaś ca mahate ca svāhā / namo devebhyaḥ svadhā pitṛbhyo / bhūr bhuvaḥ svar mahar oṃ svāhā / oṃ svāhā / bhūḥ svāhā / bhuvaḥ svāhā / svaḥ svāhā / bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā / yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricaṃ yad vā nyūnam ihākaram / agniṣ ṭat sviṣṭakṛd vidvān sarvaṃ sviṣṭaṃ suhutaṃ karotu me / agnaye sviṣṭakṛte suhutahute sarvahute sarvaprāyaścittāhutīnāṃ kāmānāṃ samardhayitre svāhā
1.5.4.4	adite'nvamaṃsthāḥ / anumate 'nvamaṃsthāḥ / sarasvate 'nvamaṃsthāḥ / deva savitaḥ prāsāvīḥ
1.5.4.5	agne vratapate vratam cariṣyāmi tacchakeyaṃ tanme rādhyatām / vāyo vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmi tacchakeyaṃ tanme rādhyatām / āditya vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmi tacchakeyaṃ tanme rādhyatām / vratānāṃ vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmi tacchakeyaṃ tanme rādhyatām
1.5.4.6	amūhamasmi sā tvaṃ sā tvam asy amūham ṛg aham asmi sā tvaṃ dyaurahaṃ pṛthivī tvam / mama hṛdaye hṛdayaṃ te astu / mama citte cittamastu te / mama vācamekamanāḥ śṛṇu / mām evānuvratā sahacrayā mayā bhava / cākravākaṃ saṃvananaṃ yan nadībhya udāhṛtam / yad devagandharvo vittaḥ saṃvananaṃ tena saṃvaninau svaḥ
1.5.4.7	ekam iṣe viṣṇus tvānvetu dve ūrje viṣṇus tvānvetu trīṇi vratāya viṣṇus tvānvetu catvāri māyobhavāya viṣṇus tvānvetu pañca paśubhyo viṣṇus tvāndhetu ṣaḍ rāyaspoṣāya viṣṇus tvānvetu sapta saptabhyo hotrābhyo viṣṇus tvānvetu / sakhāyau saptapadāvabhūva sakhyaṃ te gameyaṃ sakhyāt te mā yoṣaṃ sakhyān me māṃ yoṣṭhāḥ
1.5.4.8	saptaṛṣayaḥ prathamāṃ kṛttikānām arundhatīm / dhruvatāṃ ye ha ninyuḥ / ṣaṭ kṛttikā mukhyayogaṃ vahantīyam asmākaṃ bhrājatv aṣṭamī / dhruvaṃ namasyāmi manasā dhruveṇa dhruvaṃ no sakhyaṃ dīrgham āyuś ca bhūyāt / adrugdhāv asmiṃśca pare ca loke dhruvaṃ praviṣṭau syāma śaraṇaṃ sukhārtau / śaṃ na edhi dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade / iha gāvo niṣīdantv ihāśvā iha pūruṣāḥ / iho sahasradakṣiṇo adhi pūṣā niṣīdatu
1.5.5.1	agne prāyaścitte tvaṃ devānāṃ prāyaścittir asi brāhmaṇastvā nāthakāma upadhāvāmi yāsyai patighnī tanūstāmito nāśayāmasi svāhā / vāyo prāyaścitte tvaṃ devānāṃ prāyaścittir asi yāsyai putraghnī tanūstāmito nāśayāmasi svāhā / āditya prāyaścitte tvaṃ devānāṃ prāyaścittirasi brāhmaṇas tvā nāthakāma upadhāvāmi yāsyai paśughnī tanūstāmito nāśayāmasi svāhā / sarva prāyaścitte tvaṃ prāyaścittirasi brāhmaṇastvā nāthakāma upadhāvāmi yāsyai patighnī putraghnī paśughnī ninditā tanūstāmito nāśayāmasi svāhā
1.5.5.2	agne vratapate vratam acāriṣam ityādi vratānāṃ vratapate vratamacāriṣam ityantam
1.5.5.3	āvābhyāṃ dampatibhyāṃ svasti bhavanto bruvantu
1.5.5.4	yuvābhyāṃ dampatibhyāṃ svasti
1.5.5.5	śivena tvābhimṛśāmi hastenāvidviṣāṇinā / yathā na vidviṣemahi na hi ye ca kadācana / ṛṣabheṇa skandāmi vyasya yoniṃ patireto gṛhāṇa / pumāṃstrī jāyatāṃ garbho antaḥ / ā te yoniṃ garbha etu pumāṃsaṃ garbham ādhatsva / yaṃ tubhyaṃ śimivāsasi pumāṃste putro nāritaṃ pumān anujāyatām / sa saṃvadhatāṃ garbho daśame māsi sūtave
1.6.1.1	atha samāvṛtte bhāryām upayaccheta
1.6.1.2	prajānantuṃ mā vyavacchetsīḥ iti guruśāsanāt sarvāṅginīṃ manojñāṃ yavīyasīṃ brahmacāriṇīṃ kanyām asagotrāṃ mātur asapiṇḍām anuktām agarhitāṃ nakṣatranadīvṛkṣābhidhānāsaṃyuktām
1.6.1.3	atha dūtān prahiṇoti anṛkṣarā ṛjava iti
1.6.1.4	vadhūmantaṃ yācayati amuṣmai amukagotrāya amūm amukagotrīṃ dharmaprajārthaṃ vadhūṃ dadātu iti
1.6.1.5	tathety ukte vadhūm
1.6.1.6	āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre śobhanāny agārāṇi kalpayitvā baddhakautukaḥ kṛtamaṅgalasvastyayanaḥ padātir vadhūgṛhaṃ gatvā gṛhītamadhuparkaḥ uddhananādyasaṃbhārasaṃbharaṇān kṛtvā lājān aśmānam ahataṃ vāsaś ca saṃbhṛtya brahmapraveśanādyāparidhānāntaṃ karoti
1.6.1.7	etasmin kāle vadhūṃ baddhakautukāṃ kṛtapuṇyāhinīṃ yajñopavītinīm ācāntām agner uttareṇa pareṇa ca gatvā dakṣiṇataḥ prācīṃ tiṣṭhantīṃ varo 'gner uttareṇa pūrveṇa ca gatvā purastāt pratyak tiṣṭhan sapavitrena pāṇinā vyāhṛtibhiḥ prajāpatiḥ striyām iti ṣaḍbhir enāṃ dakṣiṇata udaṅmukhas tiṣṭhan amūm amukagotrīm amuṣmai amukagotrāya tubhyaṃ prajāsahatvakarmabhyaḥ pratipādayāmi iti vadhūmatādbhir dattāṃ pratigṛhṇāti strīdhanaṃ ca
1.6.1.8	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena mārjayitvā yathāprapannam apareṇāgnim upaveśyāthainām ahataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāpayati pūrvaṃ nidhāya yā akṛntann avayan iti tisṛbhiḥ
1.6.1.9	parīdaṃ vāsa ity etayā abhimantrayate
1.6.1.10	athainām ācāntāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ prācīm upaveśya tasyām anvārabdhāyāṃ gandhādināgnim alaṅkṛtya pariṣiñcati adite 'numanyasva iti dakṣiṇataḥ prācīnam anumate 'numanyasva iti paścādudīcīnaṃ sarasvate 'numanyasva iti uttarataḥ prācīnaṃ deva savitaḥ prasuva iti sarvataḥpradakṣiṇaṃ pariṣicya ūrdhve samidhāv anūyājārthaṃ cādadhāti
1.6.1.11	idhmād evoddhṛtya dakṣiṇaṃ paridhim agniṃ cāntareṇa uttaraṃ paridhiṃ cāgniṃ cāntarena praṇītāpraṇayane 'nūyājārthaṃ cādadhāti
1.6.1.12	ayaṃ ta idhmam aktvābhyādadhāti
1.6.1.13	apa upaspṛśya idhmasya mūlam upasaṃspṛśya darvyā juhoti prajāpataye svāhā ity udañcam indrāya svāhā iti prāñcam āghārāv āghārya
1.6.1.14	ājyabhāgau juhoti agnaye svāhā iti uttarataḥ somāya svāhā iti dakṣiṇataḥ
1.6.1.15	madhye vyāhṛtibhir hutvā yā tiraścī nipadyase 'ham iti trayodaśahutīr juhoti
1.6.2.1	athāṣṭau samṛddhihomān juhoti iṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā iti
1.6.2.2	atha jayāñ juhoti cittaṃ ca cittiś ca ity evaṃ vā juhoti
1.6.2.3	nānāsruvāhutīḥ cittāya svāhā cittaye svāhā ity evam
1.6.2.4	athābhyātānāñ juhoti agnir bhūtānām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu svāhā iti
1.6.2.5	atha prācīnāvītaṃ kṛtvādhivadate pitaraḥ pitāmahā iti
1.6.2.6	upavītī bhūyo bhavati
1.6.2.7	sa evam etān saptadaśābhyātānān sādhivādān juhoti
1.6.2.8	atha svāhākṛtāḥ ṣaḍ rāṣṭrabhṛto juhoti
1.6.2.9	ṛtāṣāḍ ṛtadhāmā iti
1.6.2.10	agnir etu prathama iti ṣaṭ pradhānāhutīr juhoti
1.6.2.11	śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya ity ubhau mārjayate
1.6.2.12	athāsya dakṣiṇena hastena dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ sāṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhṇāty abhīvalomāni devasya tvā iti
1.6.2.13	athopotthāpayati bhago aryamā ity etābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ
1.6.2.14	atrāsauśabdaprathamayā nāma gṛhṇīyāt
1.6.2.15	uttareṇottarārdhaparidhisandhim aśmānaṃ nidhāya dakṣiṇena pādena vadhūm āsthāpayati ātiṣṭhemam aśmānam iti
1.6.2.16	viśvā uta tvayā vayam iti pradakṣiṇam agniṃ parikrāmataḥ
1.6.2.17	athāsyā añjalāv upastīrya dvir lājān āvapati
1.6.2.18	triḥ pañcāvattinām
1.6.2.19	imān lājān āvapāmi iti
1.6.2.20	abhighārya darvyā saṃsṛjati bhagena tvā saṃsṛjāmi iti
1.6.2.21	atha juhoti iyaṃ nārī iti
1.6.3.1	evaṃ dvitīyam āsthāpya parītya juhoti
1.6.3.2	tathā tṛtīyam
1.6.3.3	yathāyatanam upaveśya anūyājasamidham ādāya darvyā vāruṇyau cāgnivāruṇyau bheṣajavanaspatiṃ prājāpatyaṃ sauviṣṭakṛtaṃ ca hutvā purastāt sviṣṭakṛtaṃ prāyaścittaṃ juhoti yan ma ātmana iti pañca
1.6.3.4	pāhi no agna enasa iti caiṣo 'nuvākaḥ
1.6.3.5	atra mahāvyāhṛtibhir hutvā bhūr agnaye ca pṛthivyai ca mahate ca svāhā iti atraiva praṇavaṃ juhuyād vyāhṛtibhiḥ samastābhiś ca
1.6.3.6	atha madhyamaṃ paridhim aktvā dakṣiṇārdhe ca apa upaspṛśya uttarārdhaṃ ca paristaraṇebhyo 'rdham ardham ādāya darvyām agram anakti madhyaṃ ca ājyasthālyāṃ mūlam anakti
1.6.3.7	punar api darvyām agraṃ madhyaṃ ca ājyasthālyāṃ mūlam anakti
1.6.3.8	punar api ājyasthāalyāṃ mūlaṃ madhyaṃ cāgraṃ ca darvyām
1.6.3.9	athaikaṃ tṛṇaṃ nidhāyāpa upaspṛśya śiṣṭam agnau praharet
1.6.3.10	nātyagraṃ praharet yad atyagraṃ prahared iti brāhmaṇam
1.6.3.11	trir udyatya tṛṇam apy anupraharet
1.6.3.12	aṅguliṃ trir udyamya prāṇasthānaṃ cakṣvādi saṃmiśya paridhīn ādāya madhyamaṃ prathamaṃ praharet
1.6.3.13	yugapad dakṣiṇam uttaraṃ ca
1.6.3.14	ūrdhve samidhau praharati
1.6.3.15	uttarārdham aṅgāreṣūpohati
1.6.3.16	saṃsrāveṇābhijuhuyāt
1.6.3.17	atha pariṣiñcati
1.6.3.18	yathā purastād anvamaṃsthāḥ prāsāvīḥ iti mantrāntān saṃnamati
1.6.3.19	praṇītāpraṇayanam ādāyāgreṇāgniṃ parihṛtya dakṣiṇenāgniṃ cāpareṇāgniṃ cāśmano deśe nidhāya yathāśakti dakṣiṇāṃ brahmaṇe dattvā prāgādi pratidiśaṃ tūṣṇīṃ mārjayate
1.6.3.20	kiṃcid avasicya hastena mārjayet
1.6.3.21	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena kayā naś citra ābhuvad iti tisṛbhiḥ prājāpatyaṃ pavitram iti dvābhyām
1.6.3.22	etasmin kāle brahmā yathāprapannam upaniṣkrāmaṇam iti
1.6.3.23	prāyaścittādi ā brahmaṇa upaniṣkrāmaṇāt sarvadarvīhomānām eṣa samānam
1.6.3.24	atra gurave varaṃ dadāti
1.6.3.25	atha devatām upatiṣṭhate agne vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmi ity etaiḥ
1.6.3.26	amūhamasmi ity athāsyā dakṣiṇe karṇe japati
1.6.3.27	athāsyā dakṣiṇena hastena dakṣiṇam aṃsam uparyupari avamṛśya hṛdayadeśam abhimṛśati mama hṛdaye hṛdayaṃ te astu iti dvābhyām
1.6.3.28	athāpareṇāgnim idaṃviṣṇukramāt prakrāmati ekam iṣe viṣṇus tvānvetu iti
1.6.3.29	manāg dakṣiṇaṃ pūrve pādaṃ praharati
1.6.3.30	savyenānuniṣkrāmati
1.6.3.31	atraiva saptamaṃ padaṃ vikramate
1.6.3.32	nāgnim ati pracyavate
1.6.3.33	sakhāyau saptapadāv abhūva iti saptame pade japati
1.6.3.34	athāpareṇāgnim udaṅmukhas tiṣṭhan saptaṛṣīn upaniṣṭhate sapta ṛṣayaḥ prathamāṃ kṛttikānām iti
1.6.3.35	atha dhruvam upatiṣṭhate dhruvaṃ namasyāmi iti
1.6.3.36	muhūrtam upaviśya aupāsanāgnim āhavanīyākāre kuṇḍe nidhāyātra sadasyā āśīrvādaṃ kurvanti
1.6.3.37	atha vrajaṃ prapadyate
1.6.3.38	athāsyā dakṣiṇena hastena dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇiṃ parigṛhya dakṣiṇāṃ dvāreyīm abhimṛśati śaṃ na edhi dvipade śaṃ catuṣpada iti
1.6.3.39	evam uttarām
1.6.3.40	agāraṃ praviśyānaḍuhe carmaṇy uttare lomny upaviśati iha gāvo niṣīdantu iti
1.6.3.41	jñātisaṃbhāṣāvāsāte
1.6.3.42	brahmacāriṇāv alaṃkurvaṇau tryahaṃ vrataṃ careyātām akṣāralavaṇam aśamīdhānyaṃ bhuñjānāv adhaḥśāyināv asaṃvartamānau sahacaryātām
1.6.3.43	sāyaṃprātaraupāsane juhoti vrīhibhir yavair vā
1.6.3.44	sāyaṃ prathamam agnim upasamādhāya paristīrya prakṣālya sthālīṃ niṣṭapya saṃmṛjya ekamuṣṭiṃ vrīhīn opya paryagnikṛtvā gandhapuṣpair agnim alaṃkṛtya indrāyāgraye yamāya nirṛtyai varuṇāya vāyave somāyeśānāyeti prāgādi pratidiśaṃ paścād ātmānam alaṃkṛtya apa upaspṛśya sapavitrapāṇiḥ adite 'numanyasva iti pariṣicya samidham abhyādhāya prajvalayitvā hastena vrīhīn juhuyād agnaye svāhā prajāpataye svāhā iti sāyaṃ sūryāya svāhā prajāpataye svāhā iti prātaḥ
1.6.3.45	adite 'nvamaṃsthā iti pariṣicya kanīyas tasya pūrvaṃ hutvottaraṃ bhūyo juhuyād iti brāhmaṇam
1.6.3.46	evam aupāsane juhoti
1.6.3.47	athāparaṃ patnīṃ bhojayet
1.6.3.48	tasmān nityo dhāryo 'nugato manthyaḥ śrotriyāgārād vāhāryaḥ
1.6.3.49	prāyaścittaṃ juhoti ayāś cāgner anabhiśastīś ca satyamitvamayā asi / ayasā manasā dhṛto 'yasā havyam ūhiṣe 'yāno dhehi bheṣajaṃ svāhā iti
1.6.3.50	tryahe paryapete niśy agnipratiṣṭhāpanādi prasiddhaṃ dārvihomikam ā rāṣṭrabhṛdbhyo vivāhaprakṛtiṃ nayel lājādisaṃbhāravarjaṃ pratigrahamārjanavāsaḥparidhānavarjam evam eṣa sarveṣāṃ vivāhaprakṛtim
1.6.3.51	ākālaṃ prāyaścittaṃ juhoti agne prāyaścitta iti catasṛbhiḥ
1.6.3.52	vāruṇyādi samānam
1.6.3.53	vratavisargaḥ
1.6.3.54	atha vrataṃ visṛjate agne vratapate vratam acāriṣam ity etaiḥ
1.6.3.55	atha puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā āvābhyāṃ dampatibhyāṃ svasti bhavanto bruvantu iti
1.6.3.56	yuvābhyāṃ dampatibhyāṃ svasti iti prativacanam
1.6.3.57	athāsyā upastham abhimṛśati śivena tvābhimṛśāmi iti
1.6.3.58	pratisaṃviśati ṛṣabheṇa skandāmi iti
1.6.3.59	ratyantaṃ kṛtvā japet ā te yoniṃ garbha etu iti tisṛbhiḥ
1.6.3.60	evameva māsi māsy ṛtuvelāyāṃ saṃtiṣṭhate bhāryopayamanam
1.7.1.1	athātaḥ sthāgaramalaṅkāraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
1.7.1.2	ādarśaṃ cāñjanaṃ cāhataṃ vāsaḥ sarvasurabhitaṃ vrīhīn dṛṣadupale ity ete 'sya saṃbhārā upakḷptā bhavanti
1.7.1.3	pāṇigrahaṇād ūrdhvaṃ śvobhūte śvaśrūr vā śvaśuro vā syālo vā gomayena gocarmamātraṃ caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya prokṣya lakṣaṇam ullikhyādbhir abhyukṣya śuci śuklam anārdram ācchādya suprakṣālitapāṇipādāv apa ācamya pavitrapāṇī sthaṇḍilasyāparārdhe dampatī upaviśataḥ
1.7.1.4	pūrvārdhe vrīhīn avakīrya dṛṣadupale pratiṣṭhāpyāhatena vāsasā pariveṣṭayati
1.7.1.5	gandhapuṣpadhūpadīpaiḥ yavākṣatataṇḍulair abhyarcya purastād daśahotāraṃ sagṛhaṃ japati cittiḥ srug iti caturhotāraṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pṛthivī iti pañcahotāraṃ paścād agnir hotā iti ṣaḍḍhotāram uttarataḥ sūryaṃ te cakṣuḥ iti saptahotāram upariṣṭād mahāhavir hotā iti
1.7.1.6	etasmin kāle varasya bhaginyapareṇa dṛṣadupalābhyāṃ prāṅ upaviśya sarvasurabhitaṃ piṣṭvā devatābhyo nivedyāñjanenāṅkte
1.7.1.7	ādarśam avekṣayitvā śeṣeṇa duhitaram alaṅkṛtya mukhe agnir yajurbhiḥ senendrasya iti paścāj jāmātaram
1.7.1.8	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
1.7.1.9	sā priyā bhavati
1.7.1.10	priyo haiva bhavati iti brāhmaṇam
1.7.2.1	atha vaiśvadevasyānnasāvaupāsane 'gnau juhuyāt
1.7.2.2	gṛhye 'gnau vā
1.7.2.3	agnaye svāhā iti sāyam
1.7.2.4	sūryāya svāhā iti prātaḥ
1.7.2.5	somāya dhanvantaraye 'nupataye prajāpataye viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ sarvābhyo devatābhyo 'gnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā iti
1.7.2.6	atha baliharaṇaṃ yathādiśaṃ haret brahmaṇe brahmapuruṣebhya indrāyendrapuruṣebhyo 'gnaye yamāya yamapuruṣebhyo nirṛtyai varuṇāya varuṇapuruṣebhyo vāyave somāya somapuruṣebhya īśānāya iti
1.7.2.7	atha gṛhadevatābhyo baliṃ harati
1.7.2.8	ulūkhalamusalābhyām iti ulūkhalamusale dṛṣadupalābhyām iti dṛṣadupale udadhānyā ity udadhānyām oṣadhivanaspatibhyām iti dvāre antarikṣe divācāribhya iti divā naktaṃcāribhya iti naktam
1.7.2.9	dakṣiṇataḥ prācīnāvītī pitṛbhyaḥ pitāmahebhyaḥ prapitāmahebhyaḥ svadhā pitṛbhya iti
1.7.2.10	śeṣaṃ dakṣiṇā ninayet
1.7.3.1	athātaḥ pañcadaśyāṃ prātarhomaṃ hutvā idhmābarhiś ca sambhṛtya uktalakṣaṇenedhmam idhmapravraścanaṃ ca yoktreṇa saṃnahya yatra bhuktaṃ manyate tan nidadhāty agnim anvādadhāti
1.7.3.2	apareṇāgniṃ prācīnāgrāś catasraḥ samidha ādadhāti
1.7.3.3	tāv ubhābhyāṃ hatābhyām ādāyayāgnāv ādadhāti
1.7.3.4	tūṣṇīm upasthāyāpare samidhāv ādadhāti
1.7.3.5	śvo yajñāya ramatāṃ devatābhyo yajñāya tvā gṛhṇāmi devayajyāyā ity upasthāyāpakālahomaṃ hutvā agniṃ paristīrya tāṃ rātrim anaśnann apareṇāgnim udakchirāḥ saṃviśati
1.7.3.6	śvobhūte yathoditaṃ snānaṃ kṛtvā prātarhomaṃ ca prāgādipratidiśaṃ darbhaiḥ paristṛṇāti prāgudagagraiḥ
1.7.3.7	dakṣiṇān uttarān karoty uttarān adharān
1.7.3.8	tataḥprabhṛti saṃbhārasambharaṇān kṛtvā vrīhīn carusthālīṃ juhūṃ ca mekṣaṇaṃ ca sambhṛtya brahmapraveśanādy ā praṇītābhyaḥ kṛtvā prokṣaṇīṃ ca saṃskṛtya vrīhīn nirvapati apareṇāgniṃ tiraḥpavitraṃ juhvāḥ
1.7.3.9	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyām agnaye juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi agnīṣomābhyām iti paurṇamāsyām agnaye juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi indrāgnibhyām ity amāvāsyāyāṃ trīn muṣṭīn yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
1.7.3.10	patny avahanti
1.7.3.11	triṣphalīkṛtya triḥ prakṣālya tiraḥpavitraṃ sthālyām āvapati
1.7.3.12	tasminn agnau śrapayitvā darvīniṣṭapanakāle juhūṃ ca niṣṭapya nidadhāti
1.7.3.13	ājyaṃ ca saṃskṛtyābhighārya carum udvāsyābhighārayati
1.7.3.14	paridhānaprabhṛti vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā haviṣā juhoti
1.7.3.15	āgneyam agnīṣomīyaṃ sauviṣṭakṛtam iti paurṇamāsyām
1.7.3.16	āgneyam aindrāgnaṃ sauviṣṭakṛtam ity amāvāsyāyām
1.7.3.17	ājyena juhūm upastīrya dvir avadyati sakṛd abhighārayati
1.7.3.18	triḥ pañcāvattinām
1.7.3.19	sauviṣṭakṛtaṃ sakṛd upastṛṇāti sakṛd avadyati
1.7.3.20	dviḥ pañcāvattinām
1.7.3.21	dvir abhighārayati
1.7.3.22	avatte sviṣṭakṛti pārvaṇahomau juhoti ṛṣabhaṃ vājinaṃ vayaṃ pūrṇamāsaṃ yajāmahe / sa no dohatāṃ suvīryaṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ sahasriṇaṃ prāṇāya surādhase pūrṇamāsāya svāhā pūrṇā paścād uta pūrṇā iti paurṇamāsyām
1.7.3.23	amāvāsyā subhagā suśevā dhenuriva bhūya āpyāyamānā / sā no dohatāṃ suvīryaṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ sahasriṇam apānāya surādhase 'māvāsyāyai svāhā yat te devā adadhur bhāgadheyam ity amāvāsyāyām
1.7.3.24	uttarārdhapūrvārdhe 'saṃsaktām itarābhyām āhutibhyāṃ juhoti
1.7.3.25	mekṣaṇaṃ cānuprahṛtyāpa upaspṛśya juhūm adbhiḥ pūrayitvā prācīnāvīty avācīnapāṇiḥ dakṣiṇāpavargaṃ sakṛd antaraparidhisaṃkṣālanaṃ ninayati vaiśvānare havir idaṃ juhomi sāhasram utsaṃ śatadhāram etam / tasminn eṣa pitaraṃ pitāmahaṃ prapitāmahaṃ svarge loke 'bibharat pinvamānaṃ svāhā iti
1.7.3.26	nirṇijya sruvaṃ ca niṣṭapya bahiḥparidhyapāṃ pūrṇāṃ srucaṃ juhoty uttarāpavargam imaṃ samudraṃ śatadhāram utsaṃ vyacyamānaṃ bhuvanasya madhye / ghṛtaṃ duhānām aditiṃ janāyāgne mā hiṃsīḥ parame vyoman svāhā iti
1.7.3.27	idhmasaṃnahanam apa upaspṛśya juhuyāt
1.7.3.28	vāruṇyādijayaprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
1.7.3.29	purastāt sviṣṭakṛtam idhmapravraścanaṃ prakṣipet
1.7.3.30	saṃtiṣṭhate darśapūrṇamāsaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate darśapūrṇamāsaḥ
1.7.4.1	vrīhyāgrayaṇena vā yakṣyamāṇo bhavati āśvayujyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ kārttikyāṃ śātabhiṣajyāṃ vā
1.7.4.2	anvādhānakāle yajñāya ramatāṃ devatābhyo yajñāya tvā gṛhṇāmi devayajyāyā ity upasthāya saṃbhārasambharaṇakāle navadhānyaṃ saṃbhṛtyākūpatoyena poṣitaṃ nirvapaṇakāla indrāgnibhyāṃ juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi viśvebhyo devebhyo dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi iti homakāla aindrāgnaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ dyāvāpṛthivyaṃ sauviṣṭakṛtam iti
1.7.4.3	varapradānakāle prathamajaṃ vatsaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
1.7.4.4	śeṣaṃ prasiddhaṃ sthālīpākavat
1.7.4.5	hutaśeṣam annaṃ prāśnāti bhadrān naḥ śreyaḥ samanaiṣṭa devā iti
1.7.4.6	evam eva saṃvatsarasyartuṣu tadṛtuphalamiśreṇānnena pratyṛtu hotavyam
1.7.4.7	pradhānakāle madhuś ca mādhavaś ca śukraś ca śuciś ca nabhaś ca nabhasyaś ca iṣaś corjaś ca sahaś ca sahasyaś ca tapaś ca tapasyaś ca iti ṣaḍṛtudvandvaṃ yajeta
1.7.4.8	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛtivat śeṣaṃ ca
2.1.1.1	athātaḥ puṃsavanam
2.1.1.2	tṛtīyamāsy āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre 'gnim upasamādhāya paristīrya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā dhātā dadātu no rayim iti catasro dhātrīr juhoti
2.1.1.3	imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
2.1.1.4	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati
2.1.1.5	yathā purastād brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā snātāṃ prayatavastrām alaṃkṛtāṃ brāhmaṇasambhāṣām patnīm apareṇāgniṃ maṇḍalākāre prācīm upaveśya vṛṣāsi iti dakṣiṇe pāṇau yavam ādadhāti āṇḍau stha ity abhito yavasarṣapau dhānyamāṣau vā
2.1.1.6	śvāpṛtad iti dadhidrapsaṃ tadaināṃ prāśayati
2.1.1.7	ācāntāyā udraram abhimṛśati ābhiṣ ṭvāhaṃ daśabhir abhimṛśāmi daśamāsyāya sūtave iti
2.1.1.8	nyagrodhaśṛṅgaṃ vā ghṛtena kośakārīṃ vā praiyaṅgaveṇa saṃyāvena yūpaśakalaṃ vottarapūrvasyābhiṣṭer agniṃ vā nirmathya mūrmapadhānāya iti tasyā dakṣiṇe nāsikācchidre praṇayet
2.1.1.9	yadi garbhaḥ sraved ārdreṇāsyāḥ pāṇinā trir ūrdhvaṃ nābher unmārṣṭi
2.1.1.10	parāñcaṃ tvā nārvāñcaṃ tvaṣṭā badhnātu bandhane
2.1.1.11	sa ṛtūn upaśeṣvā daśa māso avīrahā iti
2.1.2.1	athātaḥ sīmantonnayanam
2.1.2.2	prathamagarbhāyāś caturthe māsy āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre agnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā dhātā dadātu no rayim iti catasro dhātrīr juhoti
2.1.2.3	imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
2.1.2.4	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati
2.1.2.5	yathā purastād brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā snātāṃ prayatavastrām alaṅkṛtāṃ brāhmanasaṃbhāṣām apareṇāgniṃ maṇḍalākāre prāṅmukham upaveśya traiṇyā śalalyā śalāludrapsam upasaṃgṛhya purastāt pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan vyāhṛtibhī rākām ahaṃ yās te rāka iti dvābhyām ūrdhvaṃ sīmantam unnīyābhimantrayate soma eva no rājety āhur brāhmaṇīḥ prajāḥ / vivṛttacakrā āsīnās tīre tubhyaṃ gaṅge / viśvā uta tvayā vayaṃ dhārā udanyā iva / atigāhemahi dviṣaḥ iti
2.1.3.1	vijananakāle kṣipraṃ suvanam
2.1.3.2	śirasta udakumbhaṃ nidhāya pattas tūryantīm athāsyā udaram abhimṛśati
2.1.3.3	yathaiva vāyuḥ pavate yathā samudra ejati / evaṃ te garbha ejatu saha jarāyuṇāpasarpatu ity adbhir mārṣṭi
2.1.3.4	jāte aśmani paraśuṃ nidhāyopariṣṭāddhiraṇyaṃ teṣūpariṣṭāt kumāraṃ dhārayati
2.1.3.5	aśmā bhava paraśur bhava hiraṇyam astṛtaṃ bhava / vedo vai putranāmāsi jīva tvaṃ śaradaḥ śatam
2.1.3.6	aṅgād aṅgāt saṃbhavasi hṛdayād adhi jāyase / ātmā vai putranāmāsi sa jīva śaradaḥ śatam iti
2.1.3.7	yady aparā na patet tad añjalinā udakam ādāya mūrdhānam asyā visiñcet tilade 'vapadyasva na māṃsam asi no dalam avapadyasva svastyā iti
2.1.3.8	upanirharanty aupāsanāgnim atiharanti sūtakāgnim
2.1.3.9	sa eṣa uttapanīya eva
2.1.3.10	nāsmin kiṃcana karma kriyate 'nyatroddhūpanāt
2.1.3.11	athainaṃ kaṇaiḥ sarṣapamiśrair dhūpayati
2.1.3.12	śaṇḍo marka upavīraḥ śāṇḍikera ulūkhalaḥ / cyavano naśyatād itaḥ svāhā / ālikhavilikhann animiṣan kiṃ vadanta upaśruti svāhā / aryamṇaḥ kumbhiśatruṃ pātrapāṇiṃ nipuṇiṃ svāhā / āntramukhaṃ sarṣapāṇiruṇo naśyatād itaḥ svāhā / keśinī svalominī khajāpojopakāśinī apeta naśyatād itaḥ svāhā / kauverikā viśvavāsā rakṣorājena preṣitāḥ / grāmaṃ sajānayo yantīpsanto 'parijākṛtān svāhā / etān ghnataitān badhnītety ayaṃ brahmaṇo dūtaḥ / tān agniḥ paryasarat tān indras tān bṛhaspatiḥ / tān ahaṃ veda brāhmaṇān pramṛśataḥ kūṭadantān vikeśān lambanastanān svāhā / naktaṃcāriṇa uraspeśān śūlahastān kapālapān svāhā / pūrva eṣāṃ pitety uccaiḥśrāvyakarṇakaḥ / mātā jaghanyā gacchantī grāme mithunam icchantī svāhā / naktaṃcāriṇī svasā saṃdhinā prekṣate kulam / yā svapatsu jāgarti tasyai vijātāyāṃ manaḥ svāhā / tāsāṃ tvaṃ kṛṣṇavartmane klomānaṃ hṛdayaṃ yakṛt / agne akṣīṇi nirdaha svāhā iti pratimantram aṅgāreṣv āvapati
2.1.3.13	tataḥ pāṇiṃ prakṣālya bhūmim ālabhate yat te susīme hṛdayaṃ divi candram asi śritam / tasyāmṛtasya no dhehi māhaṃ pautram aghaṃ rudam / vedase bhūmi hṛdayaṃ divi candramasi śritam / tasyāmṛtasya no dhehi māhaṃ pautram aghaṃ rudam iti
2.1.4.1	athāto medhājananam
2.1.4.2	atha darbheṇa hiraṇyaṃ pravadhya tad antardhāya prāñcaṃ dhāryamāṇaṃ ghṛtaṃ prāśayati bhūr ṛcas tvayi juhomi svāhā / bhuvo yajūṃṣi juhomi svāhā / svaḥ sāmāni tvayi juhomi svāhā / bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ atharvāṅgirasas tvayi juhomi svāhā iti
2.1.4.3	athainam uṣṇaśītābhir adbhiḥ snāpayati kṣetriyai tvā nirṛtyai tvā druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt / anāgasaṃ brahmaṇe tvā karomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime / śaṃ te agniḥ sahādbhir astu śaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī sahauṣadhībhiḥ / śam antarikṣaṃ saha vātena te śaṃ te catasraḥ pradiśo bhavantu / sūryam ṛtaṃ tamaso grāhyā yad devā amuñcann asṛjan vyenasaḥ / evam aham imaṃ kṣetriyājyāmi śaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśād iti
2.1.4.4	athainaṃ mātur upastha ādadhāti yā devīś catasraḥ pradiśo vātapatnīr abhi sūryo vicaṣṭe / tāsāṃ tvā jarasa ādadhāmi prayakṣma etu nirṛtiṃ parācaiḥ iti
2.1.4.5	ādhāyābhimantrayate mā te putraṃ rakṣo hiṃsīr mā dhenur atidhāriṇī / priyā dhanasya bhūyā edhamānā sve vaśe iti
2.1.4.6	prakṣālya dakṣiṇaṃ stanam ādhāpayati ayaṃ kumāro jarāṃ dhayati sarvam āyur eti / yasmai tvaṃ stana prapyāyāyuḥ kīrtir varco yaśo balam iti
2.1.4.7	evaṃ savyaṃ stanaṃ ca
2.1.4.8	nāmayati na rudati yatra vayaṃ vadāmasi / yatra cābhimṛśāma iti mātāpitarau kumāram abhimṛśataḥ
2.1.4.9	āpo gṛheṣu jāgrata / yathā deveṣu jāgrata / evam asyai suputrāyai jāgrata iti saṃpūrya mātuḥ śiraḥsthāne apihitam udakumbhaṃ nidadhāti
2.1.4.10	pratidivasaṃ kaṇair uddhūpanaṃ kartavyam
2.1.5.1	dvādaśyāṃ mātāputrayoḥ snānānantaraṃ gṛham alaṃkaroti
2.1.5.2	sūtakāgnim udvāsyaupāsanāgniṃ nidhāya jātasya kumārasya nāma dhāsyāvaḥ iti mātāpitarau saṃkalpaṃ kurutaḥ
2.1.5.3	anantaram aupāsanāgnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā dhātā dadātu no rayim iti catasra āhutīḥ sīmantavaddhutvā anu no 'dyānumatir yajñaṃ deveṣu manyatām / agniś ca havyavāhano bhavatāṃ dāśuṣe payaḥ svāhā / anumatyā idam / anvidanumate tvaṃ manyāsai śaṃ ca naḥ kṛdhi
2.1.5.4	kratve dakṣāya no hinu praṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣaḥ svāhā / anumatyā idam / anumanyatām anumanyamānā prajāvantaṃ rayim akṣīyamāṇam / tasyai vayaṃ heḍasi māpi bhūma sā no devī suhavā śarma yacchatu svāhā / anumatyā idam / yasyām idaṃ pradiśi yad virocate 'numatiṃ pratibhūṣanty āyavaḥ
2.1.5.5	yasyā upastha urv antarikṣaṃ sā no devī suhavā śarma yacchatu svāhā / anumatyā idam / rākām ahaṃ suhavāṃ suṣṭutī huve śṛṇotu naḥ subhagā bodhatu tmanā / sīvyatv apaḥ sūcyācchidyamānayā dadātu vīraṃ śatadāyam ukthyaṃ svāhā / rākāyā idam / yās te rāke sumatayaḥ supeśaso yābhir dadāsi dāśuṣe vasūni / tābhir no adya sumanā upāgahi sahasrapoṣaṃ subhagā rarāṇā svāhā / rākāyā idam / sinīvāli pṛthuṣṭuke yā devānām asi svasā / juṣasva havyam āhutaṃ prajāṃ devī didiḍḍhi naḥ svāhā / sinīvālyā idam / yā supāṇiḥ svaṅguriḥ suṣūmā bahusūvarī / tasyai viśpatnyai haviḥ sinīvālyai juhotana svāhā / sinīvālyā idam / kuhūm ahaṃ subhagāṃ vidmanāpasamasmin yajñe suhavāṃ johavīmi / sā no dadātu śravaṇaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tasyās te devi haviṣā vidhema svāhā / kuhvā idam / iti dvādaśa trayodaśa vāhutīr hutvā imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāyate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
2.1.5.6	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati
2.1.5.7	yathā purastāt brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā putrasya nāma dadyāt
2.1.5.8	dvyakṣaraṃ caturakṣaraṃ vā ghoṣavadādyantarantasthaṃ dīrghābhiniṣṭānāntam
2.1.5.9	yatra vā svityupasargaḥ syāt taddhi pratiṣṭhitam iti vijñāyate
2.1.5.10	pitā mātety agne 'bhivyāhareyātām
2.1.5.11	vijñāyate ca mama nāma prathamaṃ jātaveda iti
2.1.5.12	dve nāmanī kuryāt
2.1.5.13	vijñāyate ca tasmād dvināmā brāhmaṇo 'rdhuka iti
2.1.5.14	nakṣatranāma dvitīyaṃ syāt
2.1.5.15	anyatarad guhyaṃ syāt
2.1.5.16	anyatareṇainam āmantrayeran
2.1.5.17	somayājī tṛtīyaṃ nāma kurvīta iti vijñāyate
2.1.5.18	pravāsād etya āgataṃ vā putram abhimṛśati somasya tvā dyumnenābhimṛśāmy agnes tejasā sūryasya varcasā iti
2.1.5.19	paśūnāṃ tvā hiṅkāreṇābhijighrāmy asau / āyuṣe varcase hutam iti mūrdhny abhighrāyāthāsya dakṣiṇena hastena dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ sāṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhṇāti agnir āyuṣmān iti pañcabhiḥ paryāyaiḥ
2.1.5.20	āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhad iti dakṣiṇe karṇe japati yathā purastāt
2.2.1.1	saṃvatsare saṃvatsare ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsu māseṣu caturṣu caturṣu māsi māsi vā janmanakṣatre kriyeta
2.2.1.2	atha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti agnir mūrdhā bhuva iti dvābhyām
2.2.1.3	atha nakṣatradevatābhyām ṛgbhyāṃ juhoti yathāliṅgam anu no 'dyānumatiḥ anv id anumate iti dvābhyām
2.2.1.4	avatte sviṣṭakṛty athājyāhutīr upajuhoti
2.2.1.5	nakṣatradevatābhyo hutvā candramase svāhā / pratīdṛśyāyai svāhā / ahorātrebhyaḥ svāhā / ardhamāsebhyaḥ svāhā
2.2.1.6	māsebhyaḥ svāhā iti māsi māsi vā ṛtubhyaḥ svāhā ity ṛtāvṛtau saṃvatsarāya svāhā iti saṃvatsare
2.2.1.7	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.2.1.8	āyur asi iti prāg annaprāśanād ājyaśeṣaṃ prāśayati
2.2.1.9	ācāmati jaṭharam abhimṛśati yata indra bhayāmahe tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi svastidā viśaspatiḥ iti dvābhyām
2.2.1.10	etad āyuṣyam āyuṣyam
2.2.2.1	ata ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsare saṃvatsare janmanakṣatre kriyeta
2.2.2.2	atha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti agnir mūrdhā bhuva iti dvābhyām
2.2.2.3	atha nakṣatradevatābhyām ṛgbhyāṃ juhoti yathāliṅgaṃ navo navo bhavati jāyamāna ity etenānuvākena
2.2.2.4	pratyṛcaṃ dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām āgneyam apoddhṛtyānumatīṃ juhoti
2.2.2.5	avatte sviṣṭakṛty athājyāhutīr upajuhoti nakṣatradevatābhyo hutvā candramā vā akāmayata ity etenānuvākena svāhākāraiḥ
2.2.2.6	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.2.2.7	āyur asi iti hutaśeṣam annaṃ prāśayati
2.2.2.8	ācāmati jaṭharam abhimṛśati yata indra bhayāmahe svastidā viśaspatiḥ iti dvābhyām
2.2.2.9	etad āyuṣyam āyuṣyam
2.2.3.1	ata ūrdhvaṃ caturthe māsy upaniṣkrāmaṇaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'ṣṭame vā haste tiṣyapunarvasvanūrādhāśvirevatyām ekatamasmin nakṣatre kṛtasvastyayanam apadātiṃ śiśuṃ mātrā chatriṇaṃ catuṣpathe nayet
2.2.3.2	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
2.2.4.1	atha ṣaṣṭhe māsy annaprāśanam
2.2.4.2	āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre 'gnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā juhoti imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
2.2.4.3	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati
2.2.4.4	yathā purastād brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhimiti vācayitvā athainaṃ dadhi madhu ghṛtam iti trivṛt prāśayati bhūs tvayi dadāmi bhuvas tvayi dadāmi svas tvayi dadāmi bhūr bhuvaḥ svas tvayi dadāmi iti
2.2.4.5	athainam annaṃ prāśayati apāṃ tvauṣadhīnāṃ rasaṃ prāśayāmi / śivās ta āpa oṣadhayo bhavantu / anamīvās ta āpa oṣadhayo bhavantu iti
2.2.5.1	tṛtīye varṣe cauḍakarma
2.2.5.2	āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre 'gnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā juhoti imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
2.2.5.3	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati
2.2.5.4	yathā purastād brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhimiti vācayitvā apareṇāgniṃ prāṅmukhaḥ kumāra upaviśati
2.2.5.5	uttarato mātā brahmacārī vā ānaḍuhaṃ śakṛtpiṇḍaṃ dhārayati yenāsya keśān pratigṛhṇāti
2.2.5.6	athoṣṇāḥ śītābhir apaḥ saṃsṛjati
2.2.5.7	śītāsūṣṇā ānīya āpa undantu jīvase dīrghāyutvāya varcase iti dakṣiṇaṃ godānam anakti
2.2.5.8	oṣadhe trāyasvainam ūrdhvāgram oṣadhīr antardadhāti
2.2.5.9	svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīḥ iti kṣureṇābhinidadhāti
2.2.5.10	devaśrūr etāni pravape iti pravapati
2.2.5.11	evam itarān pradakṣiṇam
2.2.5.12	yenāvapat savitā kṣureṇa somasya rājño varuṇasya vidvān / tena brahmāṇo vapatedam asyorjemaṃ rayyā varcasā saṃsṛjātha iti paścāt yena pūṣā bṛhaspater agner indrasya cāyuṣe 'vapat tena te 'haṃ vapāmy asau ity uttarataḥ yathā jyok sumanā asāḥ
2.2.5.13	jyok ca sūryaṃ dṛśe iti purastād uptvā yathoditaṃ cauḍaṃ kārayati
2.2.5.14	yathaṛṣi vā
2.2.5.15	saṃnyasya keśān yatra pūṣā bṛhaspatiḥ savitā somo agniḥ / tebhyo nidhānaṃ bahudhā vyaicchann antarā dyāvāpṛthivī apaḥ suvaḥ iti goṣṭhaudumbare darbhastambe vā nikhanati yo 'sya rātir bhavati
2.2.5.16	yathāśraddhaṃ brāhmaṇāya dadāti
2.2.5.17	sarpiṣmantam odanaṃ nāpitāya prayacchati
2.2.5.18	ity evaṃ vihitaṃ ṣoḍaśe varṣe godānakarma saśikhaṃ vāpayate
2.2.5.19	śikhāmātram atiśinaṣṭi ity ekeṣām
2.2.5.20	agnigodāno vā bhavati
2.2.5.21	gurave gāṃ dadāti
2.3.1.1	atha śucau same deśe 'gnyāyatane śakalena triḥ samuddhatya śakalaṃ nirasyāpa upaspṛśyāgnim adbhir avokṣyoddhanti
2.3.1.2	yad evāsyāmedhyaṃ tad apahanty apo 'vokṣati śāntyā iti brāhmaṇam
2.3.1.3	pañcaprasthaṃ śuci śuklaṃ sikatam anārdraṃ vivicya sthaṇḍilaṃ kṛtvā samacaturaśram aratnimātram udakprākpravaṇaṃ prādeśamātraṃ vrīhibhir dakṣiṇataḥ prācīṃ lekhāṃ likhati evaṃ madhyamam evam uttarataḥ
2.3.1.4	vrīhibhiḥ paścādudīcīṃ lekhāṃ likhati evaṃ madhyamam evaṃ purastāt
2.3.1.5	vrīhīn apohyāpa upaspṛśyādbhir avokṣya oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaroṃ pratiṣṭha ity agnim upasamādhāya barhir aratnimātraṃ ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulaṃ tisraḥ śamyāḥ paridhayo madhyamāṅgulyānāmikayā kaniṣṭhikayeti sthaviṣṭho madhyamo 'ṇīyān dakṣiṇato 'ṇiṣṭho hrasiṣṭha uttarataḥ samiddvādaśāṅguṣṭham aṣṭādaśa yājñikaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ prokṣaṇīm ājyasthālīṃ prājāpatyabhājanaṃ prasthacaturbhāgaṃ pūrṇaprasthadvibhāgaṃ praṇītāpraṇayanaṃ prasthacarusthālīṃ vadānapramāṇam aṅguṣṭhaparvoktam āhutipramāṇaṃ caturaṅgulaṃ darvīpramāṇam ekaviṃśatim aṅguṣṭhaṃ tasyāś caturdaśāṅguṣṭhaṃ pūrvabhāgaṃ tasya dvyaṅguṣṭham unnataṃ pañcāṅguṣṭhaṃ bilam evaṃ sruk prādeśamātraṃ pavitram evam upaveṣaṇam iti homapramāṇanirdeśo vyākhyātaḥ
2.3.2.1	athāto nāndīmukhebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ pūrvedyuḥ karma vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.3.2.2	āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre śvaḥ kariṣyāmīti śvobhūte vānnaṃ saṃskṛtya śucīn śrotriyān brāhmaṇān āmantrayate
2.3.2.3	śuci śuklam anārdram ācchādya yajñopavīty apa ācamya caturvāraṃ śuklān valīn harati dadhitaṇḍulasurabhiśuklāḥ sumanasa iti agnyāyatane prāgagrān darbhān saṃstīrya teṣv aṣṭau balīn dadāti agnaye somāya prajāpataye viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ ṛṣibhyo bhūtebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ sarvābhyo devatābhyo namaḥ iti
2.3.2.4	haviṣyam annaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradāpayati
2.3.2.5	dadhnā māṣamatsyamāṃsabhakṣyāśanam ity aparam
2.3.2.6	atha catuṣṭayam ādāya vrīhiyavapuṣyasarṣapāṇīti saha tair evodakumbham ādāya oṃ manaḥ samādhīyatāṃ prasīdan bhavantaḥ ity uktvā sapraṇavanāndīmukhāḥ pitaraḥ prīyantām ity evaṃ yathārtham itare pratibrūyuḥ
2.3.2.7	asya karmaṇaḥ puṇyāhaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.3.2.8	sthaṇḍilādyupanāndiṃ kṛtvāpādiśikhāntikaṃ karoti
2.3.2.9	punaḥkalpanādyānamaskāraṃ kṛtvānvāhāryādipraṇavādikaṃ karoti
2.3.2.10	anyatra jātakarmanāmakaraṇayoḥ pūrvedyuḥ saṃtiṣṭhate nāndīśrāddhaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate nāndīśrāddhaḥ
2.3.3.1	tatra tatra vinirdiṣṭaṃ puṇyāhādivivācanam / karmāṅgaṃ ca viśuddhyarthaṃ vistareṇa mayocyate
2.3.3.2	puṇyāhaṃ vācayiṣyan hi śuklāmbaradharaḥ śuciḥ / pavitrapāṇir ācāntaḥ tataḥ karma samārabhet
2.3.3.3	śrotriyān kṣālitapadān ācāntāṃś ca dvijottamān / darbhopakḷptāsaneṣu śucīn yugmān praveśayet
2.3.3.4	upaviśya navaṃ kumbham adbhiḥ prakṣālya pūrayet / śubhānanam akalmāṣam āḍhakāpūritaṃ tataḥ
2.3.3.5	arcayed gandhapuṣpādyair akṣataiś ca phalānvitaiḥ / sādayitvātha darbheṣu sakūrcaṃ pihitānanam
2.3.3.6	arcayet tu tataḥ samyagupaviṣṭān dvijottamān / āpo gandhāḥ sumanasa iti dadyāj jalādikam
2.3.3.7	śivā āpaḥ santv iti ca sugandhāḥ pāntv itīti ca / saumanasyam iti brūyur astvantam itare dvijāḥ
2.3.3.8	śivaṃ karmeti cety uktvā brāhmaṇānāṃ dadau jalam / āpaḥ svasti śivaṃ karmety astvantam itare dvijāḥ
2.3.3.9	bhojyaṃ dadyāt tatas tebhyo anvāhārya iti dvijaḥ / odanaṃ taṇḍulaṃ vāpi svanvāhāryo 'stv itītare
2.3.3.10	gṛhṇīyur dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād dakṣiṇā iti ca dvijāḥ / svastyādi dakṣiṇāḥ pāntu bahu deyam itītare
2.3.3.11	astvantaṃ pratigṛhṇīyur dadyād akṣatam akṣatam / ity akṣataṃ cāriṣṭaṃ cety astvantaṃ brūyur arcitāḥ
2.3.3.12	vācayet tu karasthānā nāme bhuktavataḥ śrite / uttiṣṭheyus tataḥ paścān manaḥ samādhīyatām iti
2.3.3.13	samāhitamanasaḥ smaḥ prasīdantu bhavantv iti / prasannāḥ sma iti brūyuḥ śāntipuṣṭīti cocyate
2.3.3.14	tuṣṭiṛddhī avighnam astv iti āyuṣyam iti cocyate / ārogyaṃ śivaṃ karmāstu ity ūcur brāhmaṇā niśam
2.3.3.15	sapraṇavam astu iti brūyuḥ
2.3.3.16	prajāpatiḥ prīyatām
2.3.3.17	prīyatāṃ bhagavān prajāpatiḥ
2.3.3.18	evaṃ tattatkarmaṇi vihitā vācyāḥ
2.3.3.19	puṇyāhaṃ bhavanto bruvantu
2.3.3.20	oṃ puṇyāham iti oṃ paramasvāmināmnaḥ svastiṃ bhavanto bruvantu
2.3.3.21	oṃ svasti
2.3.3.22	oṃ ṛddhiṃ bhavanto bruvantu
2.3.3.23	oṃ ṛddhyatām
2.3.3.24	oṃ triḥ
2.3.3.25	puṇyāhasamṛddhir astu śivaṃ karmāstu
2.3.3.26	evaṃ prativacanam
2.3.3.27	nāndīmukhāḥ pitaraḥ prīyantām
2.3.3.28	bhagavanto nāndīmukhāḥ pitaraḥ iti prativacanam
2.3.3.29	āpohiṣṭhādibhir mantraiḥ praṇītāprokṣaṇavad ātmānaṃ prokṣayet
2.3.3.30	puṇyāhaṃ samāptam
2.3.5.1	atha kautukaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.3.5.2	paramasvāmiśarmaṇaḥ kumārasya kautukabandhaṃ kariṣya iti saṃkalpya taṇḍulam udakumbhaṃ varāhaviṣāṇaṃ ca kaṇṭakinaṃ ca śaṅkham ādarśam añjanaṃ kautukatantuṃ cādāya ekatra nidhāya niśāyāṃ gṛhaṃ sabhācchādanavidhānādyair alaṃkṛtya gomayenopalipya vrīhibhiḥ sthaṇḍilaṃ kṛtvā sthaṇḍilottare kumbhaṃ nidhāya kumbhasya dakṣiṇataḥ saṃbhārān nidhāya suprakṣālitapāṇipādān caturo brāhmaṇān pratidiśam upaveśya darbheṣv āsīnaḥ karmopakramaṃ karoti
2.3.5.3	saṃskāryaṃ kumāram ātmano dakṣiṇata upaveśya āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ svahṛdayaṃ prokṣya brāhmaṇaiḥ sahaitān anuvākān japati kṛṇuṣva pājaḥ prasitiṃ na pṛthvīm indraṃ vo viśvatas pari havāmahe āśuḥ śiśāna iti
2.3.5.4	mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astu agner manve prathamasya pracetasaḥ indro dadhīco asthabhiḥ cakṣuṣo hete manaso hete bhrātṛvyaṃ pātayāmasi ityantam
2.3.5.5	etān anuvākān japitvā mātulaḥ kumārasya samīpa upaviśya trīṇi śalalyādiśaṅkhaparyantāny ādāya kumārasya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anvavahṛtya triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvartayate
2.3.5.6	athāñjanam ādāya dakṣiṇenāṅkte
2.3.5.7	ādarśam ādāya mukhaṃ darśayati
2.3.5.8	tantum ādāya rakṣohaṇaṃ vājinam ājigharmi mitraṃ prathiṣṭham upayāmi śarma / śiśāno agniḥ kratubhiḥ samiddhaḥ sa no divā sa riṣaḥ pātu naktam viśvettāte savaneṣu pravācyā yā cakartha maghavann indra sunvate / pārāvataṃ yat purusaṃbhṛtaṃ vasv apāvṛṇoḥ śarabhāya ṛṣibandhave iti tantuṃ prabadhya bṛhatsāma kṣatrabhṛd vṛddhavṛṣṇiyaṃ triṣṭubhaujaḥ śubhitam ugravīram / indrastomena pañcadaśena madhyam idaṃ vātena sagareṇa rakṣa iti rakṣāṃ karoti
2.3.5.9	atha taṇḍulam ādāya vasavas tvā rudraiḥ purastāt pāntu sarpirgrīvī pīvaryasya jāyā āśiṣam evaitām āśāste pūrṇapātre navo navo bhavati jāyamānaḥ triyambakaṃ yajāmahe viṣṇo tvaṃ no antamaḥ viṣṇor nu kaṃ vīryāṇi pravocam ity evamādiṛgyajurbhiḥ rakṣāṃ karoti
2.3.5.10	evaṃ striyāḥ savyaṃ bāhum anu paryāvṛtya pradakṣiṇam āvartayate
2.3.5.11	yatra nāndīśrāddhaṃ tatra kautukam ity āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.4.1.1	śālāṃ kariṣyann udagayana āpūryamāṇapakṣe rohiṇyāṃ mṛgaśirasi tiṣya uttarayoḥ phalgunyor haste citrāyāṃ viśākhayor eteṣu snāyāt
2.4.1.2	yatrāpas tad gatvāgnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā juhoti imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
2.4.1.3	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati
2.4.1.4	yathā purastād brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvāhataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāyāpa upaspṛśya devasya tvā ity abhrim ādāya parilikhitam iti triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parilikhya yathārtham avaṭān khātvābhyantare pāṃsūn karoti
2.4.1.5	ihaiva dhruvāṃ niminomi śālāṃ kṣeme tiṣṭhatu ghṛtam ukṣamāṇām / tāṃ tvā śāle sarvavīrāḥ suvīrā ariṣṭavīrā anusaṃcarema iti dakṣiṇāṃ dvārasthūṇām ucchrayati
2.4.1.6	ihaiva dhruvā pratitiṣṭha śāle 'śvavatī gomatī sūnṛtāvatī / ūrjasvatī payasā pinvamānocchrayasva mahate saubhagāya ity uttarām
2.4.1.7	ā tvā kumāras taruṇa ā vatso jagatā saha / ā tvā hiraṇmayaḥ kumbha ā dadhnaḥ kalaśīrayan iti saṃmite 'bhimṛśati
2.4.1.8	evam eva sthūṇāv ucchrayati
2.4.1.9	evam abhimṛśati
2.4.1.10	ṛtena sthūṇāv adhiroha vaṃśogro virājann apasedha śatrūn / athāsmabhyaṃ sahavīrāṃ rayiṃ dā iti pṛṣṭhavaṃśam āropayati
2.4.1.11	mā naḥ sapatnī śaraṇā syonā devīr devebhir vimitāsyagre / tṛṇaṃ vasānā sumanās tvaṃ śaṃ na edhi dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade iti channām abhimṛśati
2.4.1.12	tato rurāḍe vāstuśamaṃ niśāyām antarāgāre 'gnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā juhoti vāstoṣpate vāstoṣpate iti dve
2.4.2.1	vāstoṣpate prataraṇo na edhi gayasphāno gobhir aśvebhir indo / ajarāsas te sakhye syāma piteva putrān prati no juṣasva svāhā apaitu mṛtyur amṛtaṃ na āgan vaivasvato no abhayaṃ kṛṇotu / parṇaṃ vanaspater ivābhiḥ naḥ śrīyatāṃ rayiḥ sacatāṃ naḥ śacīpatiḥ svāhā / paraṃ mṛtyo anuparehi panthāṃ yas te sva itaro devayānāt / cakṣuṣmate śṛṇvate te bravīmi mā naḥ prajāṃ rīriṣo mota vīrān svāhā
2.4.2.2	imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
2.4.2.3	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati ity āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.4.3.1	atha taṭākakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.4.3.2	nābhyarcya yūpam upatiṣṭhate
2.4.3.3	tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ / divīva cakṣur ātatam iti
2.4.3.4	atha pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya pratyag adhiśritya jaghanena yūpaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ kṛtvāgnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryāgnimukhāt kṛtvā juhoti imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi iti dvābhyām
2.4.3.5	oṣadhivanaspatibhyāṃ pakvāj juhoti yā jātā oṣadhaya iti dvābhyām
2.4.3.6	atha prāsādāt pakvāj juhoti vāstoṣpate vāstoṣpata iti dvābhyām
2.4.3.7	athājyāhutīr upajuhoti
2.4.3.8	brahmaṇe svāhā / rudrāya svāhā / yamāya svāhā / varuṇāya svāhā / nirṛtyai svāhā / śriyai svāhā / yaśaskarāya svāhā / ahne svāhā / rātryai svāhā / sūryāya svāhā / candramase svāhā / nakṣatrebhyaḥ svāhā iti dvādaśāhutīr juhoti
2.4.3.9	kūpyābhyaḥ svāhā adbhyaḥ svāhā ity etam apy anuvākam
2.4.3.10	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.4.3.11	pāyasatilacūrṇaṃ payomiśraṃ salakṣaṇaṃ sampūrṇaṃ baliṃ kṛtvā balīn saṃprakīrya yamasūktaṃ puruṣasūktaṃ vācayitvormimantam udadhiṃ kṛtvā snātvācamyāhataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
2.4.3.12	hiraṇyaṃ dhānyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo dadāti
2.4.3.13	nṛttagītavādyādīni ghoṣayitvā sarvalokam alaṃkṛtya viṣṇulokaṃ gacchatīty āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.4.4.1	atha kūśmāṇḍair juhuyād yo 'pūta iva manyeta yathā steno yathā bhrūṇahaivam eṣa bhavati yo 'yonau retaḥ siñcati
2.4.4.2	atra svapnāntare retaḥ pated api vā strīkāmo vā
2.4.4.3	amāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā keśaśmaśrulomanakhāni vāpayitvā snātaḥ śuddhavāsā brahmacārikalpena vratam upaiti vatsaraṃ māsaṃ caturviṃśatim ahorātraṃ dvādaśarātraṃ ṣaḍrātraṃ trirātraṃ vā
2.4.4.4	na māṃsam aśnīyān na striyam upeyān nopary āsīta jugupsetānṛtāt
2.4.4.5	payobhakṣa iti prathamaḥ kalpaḥ
2.4.4.6	yāvakaṃ vopayuñjānaḥ kṛcchraṃ dvādaśarāśaṃ caret
2.4.4.7	bhikṣed vā
2.4.4.8	yavāgūṃ rājanyo vaiśya āmikṣām
2.4.4.9	pūrvāhṇe pākayajñidharmeṇāgniṃ praṇīyopasamādhāya yad devā devaheḍanaṃ yad adīvyann ṛṇam ahaṃ babhūva āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhad ity etais tribhir anuvākaiḥ pratyṛcam ājyena hutvā siṃhe vyāghra uta yā pṛdākau iti catasra āhutīḥ agne 'bhyāvartin agne aṅgiraḥ punar ūrjā saha rayyā iti catasra āhutīr hutvā samitpāṇiḥ yajamāna āyatane 'vasthāya vaiśvānarāya prativedayāma iti dvādaśarcena sūktenopasthāya yan me manasā vācā kṛtam enaḥ kadācana / sarvasmāt tasmān meḍito mogdhi tvaṃ hi vettha yathātathaṃ svāhā iti samidham ādhāya varaṃ dadāti
2.4.4.10	jayāprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.4.4.11	ekasminn evāgnau paricarya athāgnyādheye yad devā devaheḍanaṃ yad adīvyann ṛṇam ahaṃ babhūva āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhad iti pūrṇāhutiṃ hutvāgnihotram ārapsyamāno daśahotāraṃ hutvā darśapūrṇamāsāv ārapsyamānaś caturhotāraṃ hutvā cāturmāsyam ārapsyamānaḥ pañcahotāraṃ hutvā paśubandhaṃ ṣaḍḍhotāraṃ some saptahotāram
2.4.4.12	karmādiṣv etair juhuyād iti vijñāyata iti hi brāhmaṇam iti brāhmaṇam
2.4.5.1	athātaḥ pūtakāmo 'gnīn ādhāsyamāno vānyat tu mahat karma samārabhed vā
2.4.5.2	pūrvapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre pūrvakālam upoṣyopavyuṣasi grāmāt prācīm udīcīṃ vā diśam upaniṣkramya kṛtaśaucaḥ kṛtācamano yathoditaṃ snānaṃ kṛtvā nadīṣu vā śuddhajalāśaye vā gṛhaṃ pratyetya śuciḥ śuklam anārdram ācchādyāgnim upasamādhāya darśavat kṛtvā nirvapaṇakāle devasya tvā ity anudrutya gaṇāya juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi iti trīn muṣṭīn yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
2.4.5.3	ājyena śrapayati
2.4.5.4	ā agnimukhāt kṛtvā ghṛtānnena juhuyāt
2.4.5.5	kṣmāpavitraḥ sahasrākṣo mṛgārāṃhomucau gaṇau / pāvamānyaṃ ca kūśmāṇḍyo vaiśvānarya ṛcaś ca yāḥ pratyṛcaṃ juhuyāt
2.4.5.6	imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam ity āhutīr juhuyāt
2.4.5.7	jayāprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
