2.4.5.8	atra gurave gāṃ dattvā patnībhiḥ saha kṛtamaṅgalaś catuṣpathaṃ gatvā gomayena gocaryamātraṃ caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya pātraṃ nidhāya paristīryādbhiḥ pūrayaty avekṣamāṇaḥ pāpmāno vidhatvāyati siṃhe me manyuḥ ity āntād anuvākam
2.4.5.9	atha pātram ādāya prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhan apehi pāpman punar apanāśino bhavā naḥ pāpman sukṛtasya loke pāpman dhehy avihṛto yo naḥ pāpmanna jahāti tam u tvā jahi no vayam / anyatrāsmin niviśatāt sahasrākṣo amartyaḥ / yo no dveṣṭi sa ṛṣyanti yam u dviṣmas tam u jahi iti pṛṣṭhato nidhāyāpa upaspṛśya pradakṣiṇam āvartayet
2.4.5.10	evam eva saptāhaṃ savanatrayam
2.4.5.11	kuryān maunī haviṣyāśī nigṛhītendriyakriyaḥ / mucyate sarvapāpebhyo mahataḥ pātakād api
2.4.5.12	vṛddhatve yauvane bālye vā kṛtaḥ pāpasaṃcayaḥ / pūrvajanmasu vā jātas tasmād api vimucyate
2.4.5.13	bhojānānte dvijātīnāṃ pāyasānnena sarpiṣā / gobhūtilahiraṇyāni bhuktavadbhyaḥ pradāpayet
2.4.5.14	evaṃ kṛtvā sarvān lokān jayatīty āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.4.6.1	atha śatābhiṣekaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.4.6.2	sahasramāsaṃ paryavasitam iti cecchatasaṃvatsara udagayanāpūryamāṇe puṇye nakṣatre brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā atha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty ā praṇītābhyaḥ kṛtvopotthāyāgreṇāgniṃ pratidiśaṃ vrīhitaṇḍulaiḥ sarvāsu dikṣu caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ kṛtvā phalaiḥ puṣpais taṇḍulair akṣatair yavais tilaiḥ saṃprakīrya prādeśamātre same prācīnāgre kūrce kṛtvā prāgagraiḥ kūrcaiḥ sthaṇḍilaṃ nidhāyātha svarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ mṛṇmayaṃ vā pañcaviṃśatiṃ kalaśān sūtreṇa pariveṣṭayitvā sthaṇḍileṣu nidhāya saṃparistīrya jalapavitraṃ nidhāya sarvagandhaiḥ phalaiḥ puṣpais tilaiḥ saṃyukte jalapavitra udakam ānayati
2.4.6.3	kūrcaṃ nidhāyākṣatagandhapuṣpadhūpadīpādyaiḥ kalaśān alaṃkṛtya sarvāsāṃ diśāṃ kalaśeṣv āvāhayati
2.4.6.4	athāsya madhye brahmāṇam āvāhayāmi / prajāpatim āvāhayāmi / parameṣṭhinam āvāhayāmi / hiraṇyagarbham āvāhayāmi / svayaṃbhuvam āvāhayāmi / iti āvāhya purastād anukrameṇa indrādīn kalaśeṣv āvāhayāmīty āvāhya paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā daivatam arcayitvā arghyapādyādibhir ārādhya yathāvidhy athainaṃ snāpayati
2.4.6.5	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjanaḥ ity etenānuvākena mārjayitvaitair eva nāmadheyaiḥ amuṣmai namo 'muṣmai nama iti tarpayati
2.4.6.6	gandhapuṣpākṣatadhūpān dadyād ahatena vāsasā pracchādya
2.4.6.7	dvadaśakalaśaṃ varuṇasūktaṃ śeṣatādantaḥ śāpadhetrikodakena yadivā pareparetītaḥ iti catasṛbhir anucchandasam agnir āyuṣmān iti pañcabhiḥ paryāyaiḥ
2.4.6.8	athaitaiḥ abhiṣecanaṃ karoti
2.4.6.9	atha prakṣālitapāṇipāda ācamya ahatena vāsasā paridhatte
2.4.6.10	evam evordhvaṃ sarvagandhaiḥ candanāgarusaṃyutaṃ sarvān anulepya athādityām udīkṣayati ā satyena iti
2.4.6.11	athainam upatiṣṭhate ud vayaṃ tamasas pari ud u tyaṃ citraṃ tac cakṣur devahitaṃ ya udagāt iti
2.4.6.12	erakām āstīrya tasyāṃ prāṅmukha upaviśyāthājyāhutīr upajuhoti brahma jajñānam iti ṣaḍbhiḥ
2.4.6.13	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.4.6.14	athāgreṇāgniṃ darbhastambe hutaśeṣaṃ nidhāya āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhad ayam agnir vareṇyaḥ āyurdā agne iti dvābhyām athājyaśeṣe hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya indrāya tvā tejasvate tejasvantam iti catasṛbhiḥ anucchandasaiś cārdharcaiḥ ājyaśeṣe praticchāyāṃ darśayati
2.4.6.15	mamāgna āyuṣe varcase kṛdhi ity anena brāhmaṇāya dadāti
2.4.6.16	āyur asi viśvāyur asi / sarvāyur asi sarvam āyur asi / yato vāso manojavāḥ ityantaiś catasṛbhir anucchandasair anubrāhmaṇair āśīrvācanam āha
2.4.6.17	trivṛtānnena brāhmaṇān bhojayitvāśiṣo vācayitvā brāhmaṇena prīyatām iti
2.4.6.18	athāśāmāyuṣa grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ karoti
2.4.6.19	athācchādanaviśeṣair upasarjanaiś cāmarais tālavṛntair vahati
2.4.6.20	atha śaṅkhair geyādinirghoṣayuktaiś ca rathavāhanam āropya svastisūktaṃ japet svasti no 'mimīta ityādi svasti sambādheṣv abhayaṃ no astu iti samānam
2.4.6.21	atha dvārabaliṃ karoti
2.4.6.22	atha gehāntaraṃ gatvā brāhmaṇān sampūjyāśiṣo vācayitvātha bālānāmāhuḥ
2.4.6.23	sahasram āyuḥ sahasramāsas taruṇenduṃ darśayitvātha putrapautraiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ sāyujyaṃ salokatāṃ prāpnoti ity āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.4.7.1	atha brāhmaṇasya mahāpātakādipatitakarmāṇi bhavanti ced atra sapiṇḍaḥ kiṃ kuryād iti
2.4.7.2	nindite 'hni sāyāhne sapiṇḍāḥ saha tiṣṭhanti
2.4.7.3	catuṣpathe tathā kāryaṃ gomayenopalepanam / ninditaṃ caiva śītoṣṇam udakumbhaṃ pratiṣṭhipet
2.4.7.4	asya dāsī tataḥ paścād adbhiḥ kumbhaṃ prapūrayet / uttiṣṭhantaḥ sapiṇḍās tam idaṃ vacanam abruvan
2.4.7.5	sambhāṣaṇaṃ ca saṃyānaṃ sabhāśayanam eva ca / aśanaṃ ca tathā tena na ca kuryād itaḥ param
2.4.7.6	iti vācaṃ visṛjyaiva kuryāt kumbhaṃ pradakṣiṇam / tāḍayed vāmapādasya pārṣṇyā tat tasya saṃnidhau
2.4.7.7	anavekṣamāṇās te sarve gatvā paścād yathoditam / prāyaścittaṃ yathāśāstraṃ vividhaṃ cātha cet kṛtam
2.4.7.8	evaṃ pūtas tataḥ paścāt snātvā śuddhe jalāśaye / puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu praviśec ca catuṣpatham
2.4.7.9	gomayenopalipyātha navakumbhaṃ pratiṣṭhipet / dāserādbhiḥ prapūryātha sapiṇḍān paryupāsayet
2.4.7.10	svastivākyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā kumbhaṃ kuryāt pradakṣiṇam / udaṃ pītvātha kumbhasthaṃ svagehaṃ tu praveśayet
2.4.7.11	brāhmaṇān bhojayitvātha sapiṇḍaiḥ saha bhojayet
2.4.7.12	evaṃ hi śuddhātmānaṃ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahā asya kulavṛddhāś cāśiṣo vācayitvā ata ūrdhvaṃ sarvān kāmān sa hi kuryād iti kuryād iti
2.4.8.1	atha śubhāśubhanimittānāṃ vāyasānāṃ balividhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.4.8.2	grāmāt prācīm udīcīṃ diśam upaniṣkramya gomayena gocarmamātraṃ caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya prokṣya lakṣaṇam ullikhyādbhir avokṣya pradakṣiṇaṃ vāyasānām āsanaṃ kalpayati
2.4.8.3	aṅkatebhyaḥ kalpayāmi / kaṅkatebhyaḥ kalpayāmi / kadruputrebhyaḥ kalpayāmi / vāsebhyaḥ kalpayāmi / brahmaputrebhyaḥ kalpayāmi
2.4.8.4	athaitān āvāhayati
2.4.8.5	na kapilān na kokilān nāriṣṭān na mahāriṣṭān vāyasamātrakān
2.4.8.6	āyāntu śakunāḥ śīghraṃ vāyasā balibhojinaḥ
2.4.8.7	aṅkatān āvāhayāmi / kaṅkatān āvāhayāmi / kadruputrān āvāhayāmi / vāyasān āvāhayāmi / brahmaputrān āvāhayāmi ity āvāhya āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena mārjayitvā amuṣmai namo 'muṣmai nama iti gandhapuṣyadhūpadīpair abhyarcya amuṣmai svāhāmuṣmai svāhā iti pāyasodanena piṇḍaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ dadyāt
2.4.8.8	amuṣmai namo 'muṣmai nama ity upasthāya / satyāḥ stha satyaṃ vadata satye ramata vāyasāḥ / tat satyam iha no brūyān na mithyābalim aśnīyāt / ity āha
2.4.8.9	athainaṃ mātṛghātena pitṛghātena vā punaḥ / tad duṣkṛtaṃ pratigṛhṇīyād yo mithyābalim aśnīyāt
2.4.8.10	kapilānāṃ śataṃ hutvā brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ / duṣkṛtaṃ pratigṛhṇīyād yo mithyābalim aśnīyāt / iti brūyāt
2.4.8.11	bhāvāya pūrvaṃ gṛhṇīyād abhāvāya tu dakṣīṇam / nāstīty aparaṃ caiva bhaviṣyaty api vottaram
2.4.8.12	madhye sarvārthalābhāya ity āha
2.4.8.13	evaṃ jñātvā sarvakarmāṇy ārabhet sarvakarmāṇy ārabhed iti
2.4.9.1	atha yajñopavītavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.4.9.2	āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre brāhmaṇakanyā brāhmaṇavidhavā vā suprakṣālitapāṇipādā śuciḥ śuklam anārdram ācchādya yatra kārpāsas tiṣṭhati tatra gatvā pakvaphalaṃ parigṛhya gomayena gocarmamātraṃ caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya tanmadhye yantraṃ pratiṣṭhāpya prāṅmukhī udaṅmukhī vā upaviśya uparyupari tantuṃ tatya na kadācana nīcaṃ karoti
2.4.9.3	brāhmaṇāya dadāti
2.4.9.4	atha brāhmaṇo hiraṇyena parikrīya vā dhānyena vā dhanena vā suprakṣālitapāṇipāda apa ācamya pavitrapāṇiḥ prāṅmukha udaṅmukho vopaviśya dakṣiṇahastāṅgulībhiḥ śliṣṭābhiḥ ṣaḍadhikena navatyā parigaṇya triguṇīkṛtam athādbhir mārjayati āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena
2.4.9.5	brāhmaṇān āhūya prāg ekaḥ sthitvā pratyag dvau sthitvā dakṣiṇahastaṃ parivrājena bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ iti sūtraṃ kṛtvā triguṇīkṛtya yājñike vṛkṣe visṛjati
2.4.9.6	tṛṇena tāḍayati
2.4.9.7	hastena hastaṃ sūtram ādāya jānubhyāṃ pariveṣṭayati bhūr agniṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca māṃ ca / trīṃś ca lokān saṃvatsaraṃ ca / prajāpatis tvā sādayatu / tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti atha dvitīyaṃ bhuvo vāyuṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca māṃ ca / trīṃś ca lokān saṃvatsaraṃ ca / prajāpatis tvā sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti atha tṛtīyaṃ svar ādityaṃ ca divaṃ ca māṃ ca / trīṃś ca lokān saṃvatsaraṃ ca / prajāpatis tvā sādayatu / tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti atha granthiṃ kṛtvā bhūr bhuvaḥ svaś candramasaṃ ca diśaś ca māṃ ca / trīṃś ca lokān saṃvatsaraṃ ca prajāpatis tvā sādayatu / tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti
2.4.9.8	atha yajñopavītī bhavati yajñasyopavītena upavyayāmi dīrghāyuṣṭvāya suprajāstvāya suvīryāya sarveṣāṃ vedānām ādhipatyāya śriyai yaśase brahmaṇe brahmavarcasāya iti
2.4.9.9	ācāntaḥ sarvakarmārho bhavati sarvakarmārho bhavati
2.4.10.1	atha devatārādhanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.4.10.2	śuci śuklam anārdram ācchādya pavitrapāṇirāc āntaḥ sandhyām upāsyātha kṛtāgnikāryo devam āvāhayet
2.4.10.3	maṇḍale sthaṇḍile vāpsu hṛdi dīpte ca pāvake / tathaiva pratimāyāṃ vā harim āvāhya pūjayet / hṛdayābhyantare padmaṃ manasā cintayed budhaḥ
2.4.10.4	padmasya karṇikāmadhye tasya jyotir vyavasthitam / jyotirmadhye mahāviṣṇuḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
2.4.10.5	evaṃ dvādaśanāmabhir āvāhya keśavāyeti
2.4.10.6	candanādi pradīpāntaiḥ pūjayec ca tataḥ param / maṇḍale ca tathā sarvaṃ sthaṇḍile ca tathaiva ca // tathaiva pāvake dīpte harim āvāhya pūjayet
2.4.10.7	atha cet pratimāṃ kurvan svarṇamayena vā lohamayena vā aśaktau śilāmayena vā śaṅkhacakragadādharaṃ caturbhujaṃ kṛtvā agāre vā vimāne vā pratiṣṭhāpya āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākenābhiṣekaṃ karoti
2.4.10.8	atha devam āvāhayāmi iti keśavādināmabhir āvāhya atha vastraṃ pradāya yuvaṃ vastrāṇi iti atha gandhaṃ pradāya gandhadvārām iti atha puṣpaṃ pradāya yo 'pāṃ puṣpaṃ veda iti atha dhūpaṃ pradāya dhūr asi iti atha dīpaṃ pradāya uddīpyasva iti taccheṣeṇānulepanaṃ karoti
2.4.10.9	arhaṇīyam udakam ity athārghyaṃ pādyam udakam iti pādyaṃ dadyād ācamanīyam udakam ity ācamanīyam
2.4.10.10	atha caruṃ śrapayati
2.4.10.11	āḍhakena āḍhakārdhena vā prasthena vājyena vā payasi śrapayati
2.4.10.12	athānnaṃ bhavati
2.4.10.13	pradāya satyaṃ tvarttena pariṣiñcāmi iti ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmi iti pariṣecanaṃ karoti
2.4.10.14	athānnam abhimṛśya aham asmi prathamajā ṛtasya iti daśarcena sūktena amṛtopastaraṇam asi iti upastaraṇaṃ karoti
2.4.10.15	atha prāṇāhutiḥ
2.4.10.16	prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi / śivo mā viśāpradāhāya / prāṇāya svāhā iti prāṇāya apāne niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi / śivo mā viśāpradāhāya / apānāya svāhā ity apānāya vyāne niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi / śivo mā viśāpradāhāya / vyānāya svāhā iti vyānāya udāne niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi / śivo mā viśāpradāhāya / udānāya svāhā ity udānāya samāne niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi / śivo mā viśāpradāhāya / samānāya svāhā iti samānāya evaṃ pañcavidhāṃ prāṇāhutiṃ karoti
2.4.10.17	atha devam upasthāya keśavādidvādaśanāmabhiḥ viṣṇor nu kaṃ vīryāṇi pravocam iti japati
2.4.10.18	athāvaraṇaṃ karoti amṛtāpidhānam asi ity apa ānīya pidhāya yo 'pām āyatanaṃ veda / āyatanavān bhavati ity ācamanīyaṃ karoti
2.4.10.19	atha tāmbūlaṃ pradāya devam udvāsayati
2.4.10.20	kṣīrārṇave vā merau vā ādityamaṇḍale vā keśavam udvāsya naivedyam apsu nidhāya caturthāṃśaṃ brāhmaṇāya dadāti ity āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.4.11.1	athāto ravikalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.4.11.2	āyuṣkāmasya vā tejaskāmasya vā yaśaskāmasya vā bhūtikāmasya vā putrakāmasya vā rūpakāmasya vā bhavati
2.4.11.3	na naktam aśnīyāt mṛcchayaś ca maithunavarjam
2.4.11.4	śuci śuklam anārdram ācchādya prayataḥ śucir bhavati
2.4.11.5	atha śvobhūte ādityavāre āditye 'bhyuditamātre gomayena gocarmamātraṃ caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya madhye svarṇam athavā rajataṃ vā padmaṃ nidhāya athavā bhūmau vilikhed aṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam
2.4.11.6	pūrvapatre nyaset sūryam āgneyyāṃ ca divākaram / nyasya yāmye vivasvantaṃ nairṛtyāṃ tu bhagaṃ nyaset
2.4.11.7	varuṇaṃ paścime patre vāyavye cendram eva ca / savitāram athaiśānyām ādityaṃ cottare nyaset
2.4.11.8	sakarṇikāpūrvapatre nyased arkaṃ savājinam / sahasrāṃśuṃ dakṣiṇe ca mārtāṇḍaṃ paścime diśi
2.4.11.9	uttare tu raviṃ devaṃ tanmadhye bhāskaraṃ nyaset
2.4.11.10	evaṃ dvādaśādityān yathākramaṃ vinyasya madhye sarvādityarūpaṃ vinyasyāthādbhir mārjayate āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena
2.4.11.11	atha raktacandanena raktapuṣpeṇa raktavarṇa ācāryaḥ amuṣmai namo 'muṣmai namaḥ iti gandhapuṣpadhūpadīpair abhyarcya pādyam udakaṃ namaskāraṃ kṛtvā amuṣmai namo 'muṣmai nama iti atha daivatān udvāsayati
2.4.11.12	dvādaśanāmabhir yathā pūrvam āvāhanaṃ karoti tathodvāsanam
2.4.11.13	gurave yathāśakti dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt
2.4.11.14	evaṃ saṃvatsarasyārkavāreṣu pūjāṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā āyuṣkāmī dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt
2.4.11.15	tejaskāmī tejasvī yaśaskāmī yaśasvī bhūtikāmī bhūtimān bhavati
2.4.11.16	putrakāmī putraṃ labhate
2.4.11.17	sarvakāmī sarvaṃ labhate
2.4.11.18	ity āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.4.12.1	praṇavaṃ cāgnidaivatyaṃ parabrahmasvarūpiṇam / chandas tu devī gāyatrī ṛṣir brahmeti kīrtitaḥ
2.4.12.2	praṇavaṃ namaskaromi sarvadevatāmayaṃ śṛṇu viṣṇum abravīd iti praṇavaṃ tryakṣareṇa
2.4.12.3	akārokāram akārākṣareṇa
2.4.12.4	akāro 'gniḥ ukāraḥ sūryaḥ makāraś candraḥ
2.4.12.5	akāro brahmā ukāro viṣṇuḥ makāra īśvaraḥ
2.4.12.6	akāro napuṃsakaḥ ukāraḥ pulliṅgaḥ makāraḥ strīliṅgaḥ
2.4.12.7	akāro miśravarṇaḥ ukāro raktavarṇaḥ makāraḥ śvetavarṇaḥ
2.4.12.8	upamārahitāḥ aumakārātmakāḥ kālatrayātmakāḥ lokatrayātmakāḥ ṛgyajussāmātmakāḥ avasthātrayātmakāḥ praṇavoccāraṇena mahadaiśvaryadāyakāḥ mūlādhārānāhatabhrūmadhye sthitāḥ akārokāramakārāḥ udāttān udāttasvaritāḥ vakṣyāmy atirahasyam iti
2.4.12.9	ṛgvede praṇavaṃ yajurvede praṇavaṃ sāmavede praṇavaṃ triḥ brūyāt
2.4.12.10	tasyottarā bhūyase nirvacanāya
2.5.1.1	athāto grahātithyabalikarmopahārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.5.1.2	aśraddadhānam ahutam ajapaṃ tyaktamaṅgalam / grahā nayanti suvyaktaṃ puruṣaṃ yamasādanam
2.5.1.3	grahāṇām ugraceṣṭānāṃ nakṣatrapathacāriṇām / upahārān pravakṣyāmi śāntyarthaṃ tu yathāvidhi
2.5.1.4	māsi māsy ṛtāv ṛtāv ayane candragrahe sūryagrahe janmanakṣatre viṣuve śubhāśubhe vā tadgrahāṇām ātithyaṃ saṃvatsarād api prayuñjānaḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnotīti
2.5.1.5	uktam ekāgnividhānaṃ kṛtvā
2.5.1.6	bhāskarāṅgārakau raktau śvetau śukraniśākarau / somaputragurū caiva tāv ubhau pītakau smṛtau
2.5.1.7	kṛṣṇaṃ śanaiścaraṃ vidyād rāhuketū tathaiva ca / grahavarṇāni puṣpāṇi prājñas tatropakalpayet
2.5.1.8	baliṃ caivopahāraṃ ca gandhamālyaṃ tathaiva ca / yathākrameṇopaharet sarveṣām anupūrvaśaḥ
2.5.1.9	iti
2.5.1.10	arkasamidham ādityāya pālāśaṃ somāya khādiram aṅgārakāya apāmārgaṃ budhāya aśvatthaṃ bṛhaspataye audumbaraṃ śukrāya śamīṃ śanaiścarāya rāhoḥ dūrvāṃ ketoḥ kuśam iti
2.5.1.11	madhye vṛttam ādityāya āgneyyāṃ caturaśraṃ somāya dakṣiṇe trikoṇam aṅgārakāya īśānyāṃ vāṇākāraṃ budhāya uttare dīrghacaturaśraṃ bṛhaspataye prāk pañcakoṇaṃ śukrāya paścime dhanurākāraṃ śanaiścarāya nirṛtyāṃ śūrpākāraṃ rāhave vāyavyāṃ dhvajākāraṃ ketubhyaḥ
2.5.1.12	paridhānaprabhṛtyagnimukhāntaṃ kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti
2.5.1.13	ā satyena agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe eṣāmīśe ity ādityāya
2.5.1.14	āpyāyasva apsu me somo abravīt gaurī mimāya iti somāya
2.5.1.15	agnir mūrdhā syonā pṛthivi kṣetrasya patinā ity aṅgārakāya
2.5.1.16	ud budhyasva idaṃ viṣṇuḥ viṣṇo rarāṭam asi iti budhāya
2.5.1.17	bṛhaspate ati indra marutvaḥ brahma jajñānam iti bṛhaspataye
2.5.1.18	pra vaḥ śukrāya indrāṇīm indram vo viśvatas pari iti śukrāya
2.5.1.19	śaṃ no devīḥ prajāpate na tvat imaṃ yama prastaram ā hi sīda iti śanaiścarāya
2.5.1.20	kayā naś citra ābhuvat ā yaṃ gauḥ yat te devī nirṛtir ābabandha iti rāhave
2.5.1.21	ketuṃ kṛṇvan brahmā devānāṃ sacitra citraṃ citayantam asmai iti ketave
2.5.1.22	ghṛtānvaktānāṃ samidhām aṣṭasahasram aṣṭaśatam aṣṭāviṃśatiṃ vā pratyṛcaṃ haviṣā juhuyāt
2.5.1.23	pratyṛcam ājyena juhuyāt
2.5.1.24	haviṣyānnam ādityāya ghṛtapāyasaṃ somāya guḍaudanam aṅgārakāya kṣīraudanaṃ budhāya dadhyodanaṃ bṛhaspataye ghṛtaudanaṃ śukrāya tilamiśrapiṣṭamāṣaudanaṃ śanaiścarāya rāhomārsaudanaṃ ketoś citraudanam ity upahāraḥ sarveṣām alābhe haviṣyam
2.5.1.25	aryamaṇaṃ somaṃ rājānam iti sviṣṭakṛtaṃ juhoti
2.5.1.26	jayāprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.5.1.27	agreṇāgniṃ grahān abhyarcayati
2.5.1.28	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena mārjayitvā svena svena mantreṇa gandhapuṣpadhūpadīpair abhyarcya balim upahṛtya namaskṛtya pravāhya jaghanenāgniṃ prāṅmukha upaviśya adbhir mārjayate āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva ityādibhiḥ
2.5.1.29	atha dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
2.5.1.30	kapilāṃ dhenum ādityāya śaṅkhaṃ somāya raktam anaḍvāham aṅgārakāya kāñcanaṃ budhāya vāso bṛhaspataye rajataṃ śukrāya kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ śanaiścarāya rāhoś chāgaṃ ketoḥ kuñjaram iti
2.5.1.31	sarveṣām alābhe hiraṇyaṃ
2.5.1.32	vā yena vā tuṣyaty ācāryaḥ
2.5.1.33	yathā samutthitaṃ yantraṃ yantreṇa pratihanyate / evaṃ samutthitaṃ ghoraṃ śīghraṃ śāntiṃ nayet sadā
2.5.1.34	yathā śastraprahārāṇāṃ kavacaṃ bhavati vāraṇam / evaṃ daivopaghātānāṃ śāntir bhavati vāraṇam
2.5.1.35	ahiṃsakāsya dāntasya dharmārjitadhanasya ca / nityaṃ ca niyamasthasya sadā sānugrahā grahāḥ
2.5.1.36	grahā gāvo narendrāś ca brāhmaṇāś ca viśeṣataḥ / pūjitāḥ pūjayanty ete nirdahanty avamānitāḥ
2.5.1.37	devatā graharūpeṇa darśayanti śubhāśubham
2.5.1.38	darśayanti śubhāśubhamiti
2.5.2.1	atha yady akāle sthūṇā virohet bakaḥ kapoto vāgāramadhye 'dhipated gaur vā gāṃ dhayet gaur ātmānaṃ pratyaṅ dhayet anaḍvān vā samullikhet anagnau vā dhūmo jāyeta anagnau vā dīpyeta madhu vā jāyeta niryāsaṃ vopajāyeta chatrākaṃ vopajāyeta maṇḍūko vā bhūmau dadṛśe śvānaḥ prasūte vā gṛhapatiṃ jāyāṃ vopatapati anyeṣu cādbhutotpāteṣu
2.5.2.2	atha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā juhoti vāstoṣpate iti dve
2.5.2.3	vāstoṣpate śaṃ naḥ indrāgnī kayā naś citra ā bhuvat ko adya yuṅkte bhavataṃ naḥ samanasau iti
2.5.2.4	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.5.2.5	apareṇāgniṃ śamīparṇeṣu hutaśeṣaṃ nidadhāti śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya iti
2.5.2.6	sthālīsaṃkṣālanam ājyaśeṣam udakaśeṣaṃ ca pātryāṃ samānīyaiteṣūtpāteṣu ninayet
2.5.2.7	prokṣayed vā tac chaṃyor ā vṛṇīmahe iti
2.5.2.8	annaṃ saṃskṛtya brāhmaṇān sampūjyāśiṣo vācayati śivaṃ śivam iti
2.5.2.9	adbhuto vyākhyātaḥ
2.5.3.1	āhutānukṛtir āyuṣyahomacaruḥ saṃvatsare saṃvatsare ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsu māseṣu caturṣu caturṣu māseṣu māsi māsi vā janmanakṣatre kriyeta
2.5.3.2	atha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty ā praṇītābhyaḥ kṛtvā vrīhīn nirvapati agnaya āyuṣmate vo juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi iti
2.5.3.3	tūṣṇīṃ vā
2.5.3.4	atha dhānyān nirvapati prāṇāya vo juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi iti
2.5.3.5	tūṣṇīṃ vā
2.5.3.6	tān abhyukṣyāvahatya triṣphalīkṛtya triḥ prakṣālya nidadhāti
2.5.3.7	atha tiraḥpavitraṃ sthālyām apaḥ payo vānīyādhiśritya tiraḥpavitraṃ taṇḍulān āvapati
2.5.3.8	athājyam adhiśrityobhayaṃ paryagnikṛtvā mekṣaṇaṃ ca sruvaṃ ca saṃmārṣṭi
2.5.3.9	athaitaṃ caruṃ śrapayitvābhighāryodañcam udvāsya pratiṣṭhitam abhighārayati
2.5.3.10	sa eṣa eva sarveṣāṃ sthālīpākānāṃ carukalpaḥ
2.5.3.11	paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhad iti puronuvākyām anūcya āyurdā agne haviṣo juṣāṇaḥ iti yājyayā juhoti
2.5.3.12	ājyāhutīr upajuhoti
2.5.3.13	athāntareṇāgniṃ cājyasthālīṃ carusthālīṃ nidadhāti
2.5.3.14	sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ karoti
2.5.3.15	yo brahmā brahmaṇa ujjahāra prāṇeśvaraḥ kṛttivāsāḥ pinākī / īśāno devaḥ sa na āyur dadhātu tasmai juhomi haviṣā ghṛtena svāhā
2.5.3.16	vibhrājamānaḥ sarirasya madhyād rocamāno gharmarucir ya āgāt / sa mṛtyupāśād apanudya ghorād ihāyuṣe no ghṛtam attu devaḥ svāhā
2.5.3.17	brahmajyotir brahmapatnīṣu garbhaṃ yam ādadhāt pururūpaṃ jayantam / suvarṇarambhagraham arkam arcaṃ tam āyuṣe vardhayāmo ghṛtena svāhā
2.5.3.18	śriyaṃ lakṣmīm aupalāmambikāṃ gāṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ jayām indrasenety udāhuḥ / tāṃ vidyāṃ brahmayoniṃ sarūpām ihāyuṣe tarpayāmo ghṛtena svāhā
2.5.3.19	dākṣāyaṇyaḥ sarvayonyaḥ sayonyaḥ sahasraśo viśvarūpā virūpāḥ / sasūnavaḥ sapatayaḥ sayūthyā āyuṣeṇo ghṛtam idaṃ juṣantāṃ svāhā
2.5.3.20	divyā gaṇā bahurūpāḥ purāṇā āyuśchido naḥ pramanthantu vīrān / tebhyo juhomi bahudhā ghṛtena mā naḥ prajāṃ rīriṣo mota vīrān svāhā
2.5.3.21	ekaḥ purastād ya idaṃ babhūva yato babhūva bhuvanasya gopāḥ / yam apyeti bhuvanaṃ sāṃparāye sa no havir ghṛtam ihāyuṣe 'ttu devaḥ svāhā
2.5.3.22	vasūn rudrān ādityān maruto 'tha sādhyān ṛbhūn yakṣān gandharvāṃś ca pitṝṃś ca viśvān / bhṛgūn sarpāṃś cāṅgiraso 'tha sarvān ghṛtaṃ hutvā svāyuṣyā mahayāma śaśvat svāhā
2.5.3.23	iti ṣaḍviṃśatiśataṃ kṛtvā tadāhutīnām aṣṭasahasraṃ saṃpadyate
2.5.3.24	itarasmāt pakvāt sauviṣṭakṛtaṃ juhoti
2.5.3.25	havyavāham abhimātiṣāham iti puronuvākyām anūcya sviṣṭam agna iti yājyayā juhoti
2.5.3.26	jayāprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.5.3.27	athāgreṇāgniṃ dūrvāstambe hutaśeṣaṃ nidadhāti mā no mahāntaṃ mā nas toka iti dvābhyām
2.5.3.28	apareṇāgniṃ prāṅmukha upaviśya vāgyataḥ sthālīpākaṃ sagaṇaḥ prāśnāti āyur asi viśvāyur asi sarvāyur asi sarvam āyur asi sarvaṃ ma āyur bhūyāt sarvam āyur geṣam iti
2.5.3.29	prāśyācamya jaṭharam abhimṛśati yata indra bhayāmahe svastidā viśaspatiḥ iti dvābhyām
2.5.3.30	kumārāṇāṃ grahagṛhītānām āyuṣyeṇa ghṛtasūktenāharahaḥ svastyayanārthaṃ svādhyāyam adhīyīta
2.5.3.31	etair eva mantrair āhutīr juhuyāt
2.5.3.32	etair eva mantrair baliṃ haret
2.5.3.33	agado haiva bhavati
2.5.3.34	tad etad ṛddham ayanaṃ bhūtopasṛṣṭānāṃ rāṣṭrabhṛtaḥ pañcaśoḍāya sarpāhutir gandharvāhutir iti
2.5.3.35	agado haiva bhavati
2.5.3.36	tad etad ṛddham ayanaṃ hutāhutānukṛtayo 'nye homā āśramānukṛtayaḥ saṃśrayā iti
2.5.4.1	athāto 'pamṛtyuñjayakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.5.4.2	puṇye nakṣatre janmanakṣatre janmavāre vā kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ vā devālaye nadītīre goṣṭhe puṇyatame sthale vā svagṛhe vā gomayenopalipya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhimiti vācayitvā atha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā iti prāyaścittaṃ hutvā śvetadūrvāḥ pālāśasamidho 'ṣṭasahasram aṣṭaśatam aṣṭāviṃśatiṃ vā dadhimadhughṛtapayāṃsi samudāyutya triyambakaṃ yajāmahe iti mantreṇa hutvātha apaitu mṛtyuḥ paraṃ mṛtyo mā no mahāntaṃ mā nas toke triyambakam ye te sahasram iti hutvā sviṣṭakṛtam avadāyāthājyāhutīś copajuhoti nakṣatre rāśau jātasya śarmaṇaḥ mṛtyur naśyatv āyur vardhatāṃ bhūḥ svāhā pūrvavat śarmaṇaḥ mṛtyur naśyatv āyur vardhatāṃ bhuvaḥ svāhā pūrvavat śarmaṇaḥ mṛtyur naśyatv āyur vardhatāṃ svaḥ svāhā pūrvavat śarmaṇaḥ mṛtyur naśyatv āyur vardhatāṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā iti
2.5.4.3	atha sviṣṭakṛtaṃ havyavāham abhimātiṣāham iti puronuvākyām anūcya sviṣṭam agna iti yājyayā juhoti
2.5.4.4	jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛtaḥ iti hutvā tantraśeṣaṃ samāpya darbhastambe hutaśeṣaṃ nidadhāti tac chaṃyor ā vṛṇīmahe iti
2.5.4.5	atha dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt
2.5.4.6	yathācāryas tuṣṭaḥ prasannahṛdayo bhavet tathā dadyāt
2.5.4.7	śeṣebhyo 'pi yathāśakti dattvā brāhmaṇān bhojayet
2.5.5.1	atha jayānām eva homo jayāhe nāṣṭyaṃ tu kalpayate
2.5.5.2	bādhaḥsruvaṃ ca srucaś ca bādhaka evainaṃ vaibhītakam idhmam abhyajyābādhakena sruveṇopasṛjya bādhakāyāṃ sruci caturgṛhītena juhoti
2.5.5.3	catuṣpādaḥ paśavaḥ / paśūn evāvarundhe
2.5.5.4	cittaṃ ca cittiś cākūtaṃ cākūtiś ca vijñānaṃ ca vijñātaṃ ca manaś ca śakvarīś ca darśaś ca pūrṇamāsaś ca bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ ca prajāpatir jayān indrāya vṛṣṇe prāyacchad ugraḥ pṛtanājyeṣu tasmai viśaḥ samanamanta sarvāḥ sa ugraḥ sa hi havyo babhūva svāhā iti
2.5.5.5	atha vaibhītakam idhmam iti
2.5.5.6	devāsurāḥ saṃyattā āsan sa indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvat tasmā etāñ jayān prāyacchat tān ajuhot tato vai devā asurān ajayan yad ajayan tajjayānāṃ jayatvaṃ spardhamānenaite hotavyā jayaty eva tāṃ pṛtanām iti
2.5.5.7	brāhmaṇam ahnaiva bhavati yena karmaṇertset tatra hotavyā iti sa yat karmertsed idaṃ me samṛddhyata iti
2.5.6.1	prajārthihomaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.5.6.2	nadītīre 'śvatthacchāyāyāṃ vā gomayena gocarmamātraṃ caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya prācyāṃ diśi brahmāṇaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya pārśvayor dhātāraṃ vidhātāraṃ ca dakṣiṇato dhātāraṃ vāmato vidhātāraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ dhātāraṃ śvetavarṇaṃ vidhātāraṃ caturmukhaṃ citravarṇaṃ tatas tān arcayet
2.5.6.3	pūrvaṃ brahmāṇam āvāhayet
2.5.6.4	parameṣṭhinam āvāhayet
2.5.6.5	hiraṇyagarbham āvāhayet ity āvāhya pranavena āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena mārjayitvā śuddhānnaṃ brahmaṇe mudgānnaṃ dhātre pītānnaṃ vidhātre
2.5.6.6	yajamānasyāthaināṃ striyam āhūya tat tvam asi jyotir asi viśveśānaṃ gatā nāmadā iti amāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyām ayanadvaye ca vyatīpāte viṣuve tiṣyarohiṇyāṃ śravaṇāyāṃ tasyā janmani ṛtusnātāyām ahataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāpya hiraṇyam ācāryāya dattvākliṣṭāni vāsāṃsi paridhāyācamya gandhaśuklapuṣpair alaṃkṛtya atha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty agnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīrya sapta te agne samidhaḥ sapta jihvā saptaṛṣayaḥ sapta dhāma priyāṇi iti strīṣu dakṣiṇopaviśya paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāt puruṣasūktena juhuyāt
2.5.6.7	juhoti yājyāṃ puronuvākyām iti dvau dvau
2.5.6.8	pratyṛcam athājyāhutīr upajuhoti
2.5.6.9	sāvitryāṣṭottarasahasraṃ juhuyāt
2.5.6.10	apa upaspṛśya sudarśanenāṣṭasahasram agnibījenāṣṭasahasraṃ sapraṇavaṃ juhoti
2.5.6.11	aṣṭasahasraṃ sapraṇavam aṣṭaśatam aṣṭāviṃśatiṃ vā
2.5.6.12	madhyamaṃ juhoty aṣṭaśatam iti kīrtitam
2.5.6.13	sviṣṭakṛtāt prabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.5.6.14	athainaṃ sampātaṃ mūrdhni juhoti
2.5.6.15	praṇavena namaskārāntaṃ yajñavāstu kurvīta
2.5.6.16	tad asya garbhiṇī bhavati
2.5.6.17	evam utpāditaputrā na lupyante kadācana na lupyante kadācaneti
2.5.6.18	atha viṣṇuṃ dvādaśyāṃ bhagavantam arcayitvā sudarśanenāṣṭasahasraṃ japtvā triḥ paryāyam āvaśyakaḥ putro bhavatīty āha putro bhavatīty āha
2.5.6.19	śaivokteṣu kāleṣu nadīṣu vā śuddhajalāśaye vā madhyamena ca palāśaparṇena vāṣṭasahasreṇāṣṭaśatena vāṣṭāviṃśatyā vā āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākenābhiṣecanaṃ kṛtvā gāyatryāṣṭasahasreṇābhiṣecanaṃ karoti
2.5.6.20	puruṣasūktena ca sahasraśīrṣā puruṣa ity etenānuvākena
2.5.6.21	putro bhavatīty āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.5.7.1	atha viṣṇubaliḥ
2.5.7.2	aṣṭame māsi pūrvapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre dvādaśyāṃ saptamyāṃ rohiṇyāṃ śravaṇāyāṃ vā brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā atha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty ā praṇītābhyaḥ kṛtvā upotthāyāgreṇāgniṃ daivatam āvāhayāmi oṃ bhūḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi oṃ bhuvaḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi oṃ svaḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi ity āvāhya paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā daivatam arcayitvā āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena mārjayitvāthādbhis tarpayate keśavaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ mādhavaṃ govindaṃ viṣṇuṃ madhusūdanaṃ trivikramaṃ vāmanaṃ śrīdharaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ padmanābhaṃ dāmodaraṃ tarpayāmi iti
2.5.7.3	etair eva nāmabhiḥ gandhapuṣpadhūpadīpaiḥ amuṣmai namo 'muṣmai nama iti
2.5.7.4	atha vaiṣṇavāhutīr juhoti viṣṇor nu kaṃ tad asya priyaṃ pra tad viṣṇuḥ paro mātrayā vicakrame trir deva iti
2.5.7.5	jayāprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.5.7.6	guḍapāyasaṃ ghṛtamiśram athānnasya balim upaharati amuṣmai svāhāmuṣmai svāhā iti dvādaśabhir yathāliṅgam
2.5.7.7	vaiṣṇavībhiḥ ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvabhiḥ stutibhiḥ stuvanti
2.5.7.8	vyāhṛtībhiḥ puruṣam udvāsayati puruṣam udvāsayāmi iti
2.5.7.9	annaśeṣaṃ patnīṃ prāśayati pumāṃsaṃ janayatīti vijñāyate
2.5.8.1	atha śūlagavaḥ saṃvatsare saṃvatsare mārgaśīrṣapaurṇamāsyāṃ kriyeta
2.5.8.2	api vārdrāyām araṇye 'gnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryā praṇītābhyaḥ kṛtvā barhir ādāya gām upākaroti īśānāya tvā juṣṭam upākaromi iti
2.5.8.3	tūṣṇīm ity eke
2.5.8.4	tām atraiva pratīcīnaśirasīm udīcīnapadīṃ saṃjñapayati
2.5.8.5	tasyai saṃjñaptāyā adbhir abhiṣekam
2.5.8.6	prāṇān āpyāyya tūṣṇīṃ vapām utkhidya hṛdayam uddhārayati
2.5.8.7	prajñātāni cāvadānāni
2.5.8.8	tāny eteṣv eva śūleṣūpanīkṣyaitasminn evāgnau śrapayanti
2.5.8.9	athaitāni śūlebhyo 'parikṣipya punaḥ kumbhyāṃ niśrapayanti
2.5.8.10	athaitāni abhighāritāny udvāsya pratiṣṭhitam abhighārayati
2.5.8.11	paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā daivatam āvāhayati ā tvā vahantu harayaḥ sacetasaḥ śvetair aśvaiḥ saha ketumadbhiḥ / vātājitair maghavadbhir manojavair āyāhi śīdhraṃ mama havyāya śarvom iti
2.5.8.12	atha sruveṇoṣastīrṇābhighāritāṃ juhoti
2.5.8.13	sahasrāṇi sahasraśa iti puronuvākyām anūcya īśānaṃ tvā bhuvanānām abhiśriyam iti yājyayā juhoti
2.5.8.14	athājyāhutīr upajuhoti
2.5.8.15	atraitāny avadānānīḍāsūne pracchidyaudanaṃ māṃsaṃ yūṣam ity ājyena samudāyutya mekṣaṇenopaghātaṃ pūrvārdhe juhoti
2.5.8.16	bhavāya devāya svāhā śarvāya devāya svāhā īśānāya devāya svāhā paśupataye devāya svāhā rudrāya devāya svāhā ugrāya devāya svāhā bhīmāya devāya svāhā mahate devāya svāhā iti
2.5.8.17	atha madhye bhavasya devasya patnyai svāhā śarvasya devasya patnyai svāhā īśānasya devasya patnyai svāhā paśupater devasya patnyai svāhā rudrasya devasya patnyai svāhā ugrasya devasya patnyai svāhā bhīmasya devasya patnyai svāhā mahato devasya patnyai svāhā iti
2.5.8.18	athāparārdhe juhoti
2.5.8.19	bhavasya devasya sutāya svāhā śarvasya devasya sutāya svāhā īśānasya devasya sutāya svāhā paśupater devasya sutāya svāhā rudrasya devasya sutāya svāhā ugrasya devasya sutāya svāhā b hīmasya devasya sutāya svāhā mahato devasya sutāya svāhā iti
2.5.8.20	athājyāhutīr juhoti
2.5.8.21	namas te rudra manyava ity āntād anuvākasya
2.5.8.22	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.5.8.23	athāpareṇāgnim arkaparṇeṣu hutaśeṣaṃ nidadhāti yo rudro agnau yo apsu ya oṣadhīṣu yo rudro viśvā bhuvanā viveśa tasmai rudrāya namo astu iti
2.5.8.24	sthālīsaṃkṣālanam ājyaśeṣam udakaśeṣaṃ ca pātryāṃ samānīya vetasaśākhayāvokṣya triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ gāḥ paryeti ā gāvo agmann uta bhadram akran ity etena sūktena
2.5.8.25	mahat svastyayanam ācakṣate
2.5.8.26	atha yadi gāṃ na labhate meṣam ajaṃ vālabhate
2.5.8.27	īśānasthālīpākaṃ vā śrapayati yad gavā kāryam
2.5.8.28	sa śūlagavo vyākhyātaḥ
2.5.8.29	evam evāṣṭamyāṃ pradoṣe kriyetaitāvad eva nānā
2.5.8.30	nātropākaraṇaṃ paśoḥ
2.5.9.1	athāto gṛhakarmaṇo gṛhavṛddhim icchan māsi māsi ṛtāvṛtau saṃvatsare saṃvatsare pūrvapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre gṛhaśāntim ārabheta
2.5.9.2	apāmārgapālāśaśirīṣaudumbarasadābhadrā amṛtatṛṇam indravallībhir baddhvā gṛhān parisaṃmārṣṭi
2.5.9.3	parisamūhyāpo 'bhyukṣya pañcagavyena darbhamuṣṭinā samprokṣya sarṣapān saṃprakīryāgnimukhāt kṛtvā madhye vāstoṣpate vāstoṣpate iti dve āhutī hutvā sāvitryā sahasraṃ juhuyāt
2.5.9.4	tato dakṣiṇapurastāt tato dakṣiṇapaścāt tata uttarapaścāt madhye vā
2.5.9.5	jayāprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.5.9.6	gāṃ vāso hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā
2.5.9.7	evaṃ prayuñjāna āntaṃ mahāntaṃ poṣaṃ puṣyati
2.5.9.8	bahavaḥ putrā asya bhavanti
2.5.9.9	na ca bālāḥ pramīyante
2.5.9.10	nāgnir dahati
2.5.9.11	na daṃṣṭriṇaḥ khādayeyuḥ
2.5.9.12	na taskarāḥ sapatnā rakṣāṃsi piśācā api bādhante
2.5.9.13	yadi gāvaḥ pratapyeran gavāṃ madhye āhutisahasraṃ juhuyāt
2.5.9.14	etenaiva kalpenāśvoṣṭrakharājāvikamahiṣahastikulam anyatarad dvipadāṃ catuṣpadāṃ ca vyākhyātam
2.5.10.1	vṛṣṭikāmasya sambhārān
2.5.10.2	kṛṣṇaṃ vāsaḥ kṛṣṇāśvaḥ kṛṣṇatūṣaṃ kṛṣṇorabhraḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ ca kṛṣṇavrīhayaś ca kṛṣṇamadhu cāmā ca kumbhī kharjūrasaktavaḥ karīrasaktavaś ca varṣābhūṇāṃ srajas trīṇi ca puṣkaraparṇāni daśasahasraṃ vaitasasamidhām ity ete 'sya saṃbhārā upakḷptā bhavanti
2.5.10.3	agnim upasamādhāya yasmin kāle paścādvāto vāti tasmin kāle kṛṣṇaṃ vāsaḥ kṛṣṇatūṣam paridhatte mārutam asi marutām ojo 'pāṃ dhārāṃ bhindhi ramayata marutaḥ śyenamāyinaṃ manojavasaṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ suvṛktim / yena śardha ugram avasṛṣṭam eti tad aśvinā paridhattaṃ svasti
2.5.10.4	agreṇāgniṃ kṛṣṇam aśvaṃ kṛṣṇam abhraṃ purastāt pratyañcaṃ dhārayanto dakṣiṇata āmāṃ kumbhīṃ nimiñcanti varṣābhūṇāṃ srajaḥ paścāt sthāpayanti
2.5.10.5	saṃparistīrya nirvapān kṛtvā devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ varuṇāya juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi iti trīn muṣṭīn yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
2.5.10.6	patny avahanti
2.5.10.7	triṣphalīkṛtya triḥ prakṣālya tiraḥpavitraṃ sthālyām apa ānīyādhiśritya paryagnikṛtvābhighārya carum udvāsyābhighārayati
2.5.10.8	paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā tasmin kharjūrasaktūṃś ca karīrasaktūṃś ca kṛṣṇamadhuṣā saṃyauti māndā vāśāś śundhyūr ajirā jyotiṣmatīs tamasvarīr undatīḥ suphenāḥ iti
2.5.10.9	trīn piṇḍān kṛtvaiteṣu puṣkaraparṇeṣūpaninahya kṛṣṇam urabhram anulepanaṃ karoti
2.5.10.10	yac ciddhi te yat kiñcedaṃ kitavāsaḥ imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvan no agne sa tvan no agne tvam agne ayāsi ava te heḍa ud uttamaṃ triyambakaṃ yajāmahe ity etair daśabhir mantraiḥ śataśo 'bhyasya pratimantraṃ samidho juhuyāt
2.5.10.11	etair mantrair evam abhyasya haviṣo juhuyāt
2.5.10.12	tathaivābhyasyājyasya juhuyāt
2.5.10.13	jayāprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.5.10.14	gurave gāṃ dadāti
2.5.10.15	kṛṣṇam aśvam adbhir abhyukṣati divā cit tamaḥ kṛṇvanti parjanyenodavāhena / pṛthivīṃ yad vyundanti ā yaṃ naraḥ sudānavo dadāśuṣe divaḥ kośam acucyavuḥ / vi parjanyāḥ sṛjanti rodasī anu dhanvanā yanti vṛṣṭayaḥ iti
2.5.10.16	sayati kṛṣṇo 'śvo 'dbhir abhyukṣya udīrayathā marutaḥ samudrato yūyaṃ vṛṣṭiṃ varṣayathā purīṣiṇaḥ / na vo dasrā upa dasyanti dhenavaḥ śubhaṃ yātām anurathā avṛtsata iti
2.5.10.17	sayeti kṛṣṇorabhrīr adbhir abhyukṣya ādhūnute varṣati yadi śakṛtkaroti vā varṣati yadi palāyate vopaviśati vā na varṣati iti
2.5.10.18	āmāṃ kumbhīm adbhiḥ saṃpūrayati
2.5.10.19	sṛjā vṛṣṭiṃ diva ādbhiḥ samudraṃ pṛṇa / abjā asi prathamajā balam asi samudriyam / unnambhaya pṛthivīṃ bhindhi divyaṃ nabhaḥ / udno divyasya no dehīśāno vi sṛjā dṛtim
2.5.10.20	sa yady āmāṃ kumbhīm adbhiḥ sampūrṇāṃ bhidyate varṣati
2.5.10.21	yadi dhārayate na varṣati
2.5.10.22	apāṃ pūrṇāṃ srucaṃ varṣāhvayā juhoti unnambhaya pṛthivīm iti
2.5.10.23	atha yadi na varṣed eteṣām eva kṛṣṇavrīhīṇāṃ sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā saptāhaṃ savanatrayahomaṃ kuryāt
2.5.10.24	saṃtiṣṭhate vṛṣṭikāmaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate vṛṣṭikāmaḥ
2.5.11.1	atha bhūtabaliṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.5.11.2	vṛṣṭikāmo 'dhikārī kṛṣṇaṃ vāsaḥ kṛṣṇā gauḥ kṛṣṇorabhrī kṛṣṇā vrīhayaś ca kṛṣṇamadhu cāmā ca kumbhī kharjūrasaktavaś ca sarpiś ca trīṇi puṣkaraparṇānīty ete 'sya sambhārā upakḷptā bhavanti
2.5.11.3	yad bhūtebhyo baliṃ harati tad bhūtayajñaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate iti brāhmaṇam
2.5.11.4	saṃvatsare saṃvatsare ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsu māseṣu yadāmāvāsyāṃ śuṣyo bhavati yadā vṛṣṭer udaghātaṃ vinded atha bhūtabaliṃ dadyāt
2.5.11.5	taṭākaṃ gatvā śucau deśe uddhatyamānam ity uddhatya śaṃ no devīḥ ity avokṣya devayajanaṃ parigṛhya parilikhitam iti parilikhati
2.5.11.6	yasmin kāle paścādvāto vāti tasmin kāle brāhmaṇo mārutam asi marutām oja iti kṛṣṇaṃ vāsaḥ paridhāya apa upaspṛśya yajñopavītaṃ dhṛtvāpa ācamya udapātram ādāya paścād bhūtaṃ pratiṣṭhāpyārcayati
2.5.11.7	vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvāṣṭau vātanāmāni juhoti purovāto varṣañjinvarāvṛt svāhā iti
2.5.11.8	atha kṛṣṇavrīhīṇāṃ carūṇāṃ juhoti mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ svāhā agnaye dhāmacchade svāhā marudbhyaḥ svāhā sūryāya svāhā agnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā iti
2.5.11.9	vāruṇyādisviṣṭakṛdantaṃ hutvātha kaṃse vā śarāve vānnaśeṣaṃ kharjūrasaktuṃ samavadāya sarpiṣā madhunā vā saṃyauti
2.5.11.10	māndā vāśā iti dvābhyām
2.5.11.11	apareṇāgniṃ triṣu puṣkaraparṇeṣu nirvaped devā vasavyā iti
2.5.11.12	tisṛbhir annaśeṣasyārdhaṃ nivedayati devasya tvā iti
2.5.11.13	tata udakaṃ gatvāvaśiṣṭasya trīn piṇḍān apsu juhoti
2.5.11.14	udno dattodadhiṃ bhinta iti tribhiḥ svāhākārāntaiḥ
2.5.11.15	athāñjalināpa upahatyotkṣipet udīrayathā maruta iti dvābhyām
2.5.11.16	atha vāstudevaṃ gatvā
2.5.11.17	ye vāstudaivatāḥ krūrarakṣobhūtagaṇāś ca ye / tebhyo baliṃ vṛṣṭikāmo harāmi śāntāḥ śāntiṃ kurvantu / namaḥ sarvebhyo namo bhūtebhyo namo ity āmāṃ kumbhīṃ cādbhiḥ pūrayitvā unnambhaya pṛthivīm iti kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ ca
2.5.11.18	ye devā divi bhāgā ity atha devatā upatiṣṭhate
2.5.11.19	yantu nadayo varṣantu parjanyā iti parjanyān upatiṣṭhate puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā
2.5.11.20	yadi varṣet tāvaty eva hotavyaṃ yadi na varṣet śvobhūte havir nirvapet iti brāhmaṇam
2.5.12.1	atha bījanivāpanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.5.12.2	rohiṇyāṃ tiṣyamūlayoḥ viśākhayor maghāsu śravaṇāyāṃ revatyāṃ mitrāvaruṇayor maruta uttarāsv ekasmin nakṣatre bījān ādāya dattvādhivāsaṃ karoti
2.5.12.3	eṣu nakṣatreṣu ekasmin nakṣatre kṣetraṃ gatvā pūrvāyāṃ diśi gandhādibhir ārādhya śirīṣaparṇair avakīrya gandhaśeṣair ātmānam upalipya karṣakāya gandhādi dattvā bījāni vaped yā jātā oṣadhaya ity etenānuvākena
2.5.12.4	athālahvānāt pūrvaṃ carūrjaṃ śrapayitvātha puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā adbhir mārjayitvā āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākenātha piṇḍaṃ dadāti kṣetrasya pate madhumantam ūrmiṃ dhenur iva payo asmāsu dhukṣva / madhuścutaṃ ghṛtam iva supūtam ṛtasya naḥ patayo mṛḍayantu
2.5.12.5	atha dakṣiṇāpurastāt tato dakṣiṇāpaścāt tataḥ purastāduttarataḥ paścād atha madhye yathoditaṃ lavanaṃ karoti
2.5.12.6	tena dhānyena paścād āgrayaṇaṃ karoti
2.6.1.1	athāta ācamanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.6.1.2	prāṅmukha udaṅmukho vā dvau pāṇī prakṣālya baddhaśikho yajñopavītī jale vātha sthale vāntarjānu navivarāṅgulībhiḥ gokarṇākṛtivat karaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhan na praṇato na hasan na jalpan na vrajan noṣṇābhir na vivarṇābhir na budbudābhiḥ na calo jalaṃ māṣamagnamātraṃ pibet
2.6.1.3	brāhmaṇasya dakṣiṇe haste pañca tīrthāni pañca daivatāni bhavanti
2.6.1.4	aṅgulīmadhye daivaṃ tīrthaṃ aṅgulyagre ārṣaṃ tīrtham aṅguṣṭhatarjanyor madhye paitṛkaṃ tīrtham aṅguṣṭhamūlasyottarato rekhāsu brāhmaṃ tīrtham madhye agnitīrtham
2.6.1.5	aṅguṣṭhe agniḥ pradeśinyāṃ vāyuḥ madhye prajāpatiḥ anāmikāyāṃ brahmā kaniṣṭhikāyām indraḥ
2.6.1.6	atha trir ācāmet praṇavena
2.6.1.7	prathamaṃ yat pibati tena ṛgvedaṃ prīṇāti
2.6.1.8	dvitīyaṃ yat pibati tena yajurvedaṃ prīṇāti
2.6.1.9	tṛtīyaṃ yat pibati tena sāmavedaṃ prīṇāti
2.6.1.10	prathamaṃ yat parimṛjati tenātharvavedaṃ prīṇāti
2.6.1.11	dvitīyaṃ yat parimṛjati tena itihāsaṃ prīṇāti
2.6.1.12	yad upaspṛśati tenāgniṃ yat pādāv abhyukṣate tena viṣṇuṃ sahyaṃ pitṝn cirasyā ṛṣīn yac cakṣuṣī tena candrādityau yan nāsike tena prāṇāpānau yacchrotraṃ tena diśo yad bāhū tena indraṃ yan nābhiṃ tena pṛthivīṃ yad hṛdayaṃ tena rudraṃ yacchiras tena saptarṣīn prīṇāti
2.6.1.13	aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu cakṣuṣī samupaspṛśet pradeśinyaṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ tu nāsike aṅguṣṭhakaniṣṭhikābhyāṃ śrotre madhyamāṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ bāhvoḥ aṅguṣṭhena nābhau aṅgulyagreṇa hṛdi sarveṣām aṅgulītalānāṃ tu śirasi iti sarvān kāmān samardhayantu iti
2.6.1.14	atha ūrdhvaṃ snānavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.6.1.15	snānārthaṃ mṛdam utkhanati
2.6.1.16	mṛttike hana me pāpaṃ yan mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam / tvayā hatena pāpena jivāmi śaradaḥ śatam / mṛttike dehi me puṣṭiṃ tvayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam iti
2.6.1.17	apa ānayati
2.6.1.18	gandhadvārāṃ durādharṣāṃ nityapuṣṭāṃ karīṣiṇīm / īśvarīṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tām ihopahvaye śriyam // iti piṇḍīkaroti
2.6.2.1	atha hastapādau prakṣālya kamaṇḍaluṃ mṛtpiṇḍaṃ ca saṃgṛhya tīrthaṃ ca gatvā triḥ pādau prakṣālayate
2.6.2.2	trir ātmānam
2.6.2.3	atha haike bruvate śmaśānam āpo devagṛhaṃ goṣṭhaṃ yatra ca brāhmaṇāḥ na prakṣālya pādau tatra na praveṣṭavyam iti
2.6.2.4	athāpo 'bhiprapadyate hiraṇyaśṛṅgaṃ varuṇaṃ prapadye tīrthaṃ me dehi yācitaḥ / yan mayā bhuktam asādhūnāṃ pāpebhyaś ca pratigrahaḥ / yan me manasā vācā karmaṇā vā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam / tan na indro varuṇo bṛhaspatiḥ savitā ca punantu punaḥ punaḥ iti
2.6.2.5	athāñjalinā apa upaharati sumitrā na āpa oṣadhayaḥ santu iti
2.6.2.6	tāṃ diśaṃ nirukṣati yasyām asya diśi dveṣyo bhavati durmitrās tasmai bhūyāsur yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ iti
2.6.2.7	athāpa upaspṛśya triḥ pradakṣiṇam udakam āvartate yad apāṃ krūraṃ yad amedhyaṃ yad aśāntaṃ tad apagacchatāt iti
2.6.2.8	apsu nimajjyonmajjya nāpsumataḥ prayamaṇaṃ vidyate
2.6.2.9	na vāsasaḥ patpūlanaṃ nopasparśanaṃ yady avaruddhāḥ syus tena tenopatiṣṭhate
2.6.2.10	namo 'gnaye 'psumate nama indrāya namo varuṇāya namo vāruṇyai namo 'dbhyaḥ ity uttīryācamya ācāntaḥ punar ācāmet āpaḥ punantu pṛthivīṃ pṛthivī pūtā punātu mām / punantu brahmaṇaspatiḥ brahma pūtā punātu mām / yad ucchiṣṭam abhojyaṃ yad vā duścaritaṃ mama / sarvaṃ punantu māmāpo 'satāṃ ca pratigrahaṃ svāhā iti
2.6.2.11	pavitre kṛtvādbhir mārjayate
2.6.2.12	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena mārjayitvāntarjalagato 'ghamarṣaṇena trīn prāṇāyāmān dhārayitvottīrya vāsaḥ pīḍayitvā prakṣālitopavātāny akliṣṭāni vāsāṃsi paridhāyāpa ācamya darbheṣv āsīno darbhān dhārayamāṇaḥ sāvitrīṃ sahasrakṛtva āvartayecchatakṛtvo vā daśāvaram iti
2.6.2.13	athādityam upatiṣṭhate ud v ayaṃ tamasas pari ud u tyaṃ citraṃ tac cakṣur devahitaṃ ya udakāt iti
2.6.2.14	athāpy udāharanti praṇavo vyāhṛtayaḥ sāvitrī cety ete pañca brahmayajñā aharahaḥ brāhmaṇaṃ kilbiṣāt pāvayanti
2.6.2.15	pūtaḥ pañcabhir brahmayajñair athottaraṃ devatās tarpayatīti
2.6.3.1	agniḥ prajāpatiḥ somo rudro 'ditir bṛhaspatiḥ sarpā ityetāni prāgdvārāṇi daivatāni sanakṣatrāṇi sagrahāṇi sāhorātrāṇi samuhūrtāni tarpayāmi
2.6.3.2	vasūn tarpayāmi
2.6.3.3	pitaro 'ryamā bhagaḥ savitā tvaṣṭā vāyur indrāgnī ity etāni dakṣiṇadvārāṇi daivatāni sanakṣatrāṇi sagrahāṇi sāhorātrāṇi samuhūrtāni tarpayāmi
