2.6.3.136	pitṛsaṃyuktāni cety ekeṣām ekeṣām
2.6.4.1	athātaḥ svādhyāyavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.6.4.2	prāṅmukho vā udaṅmukho vā grāmān niṣkramya apa āplutya yajñopavīty ācānto 'klinnavāsā darbhāṇāṃ mahad upastīrya prākkūlānāṃ teṣu prāṅmukha upaviśyopasthānaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇottarau pāṇī saṃdhāya pavitravantau vijñāyate 'pāṃ vā eṣa oṣadhīnāṃ raso yad darbhāḥ sarasam eva brahma karoti dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ sandhim īkṣamāṇaḥ sammīlya vā yathā vā yuktam ātmānaṃ manyeta tathā yukto 'dhīyīta svādhyāyam
2.6.4.3	oṃpūrvā vyāhṛtayaḥ
2.6.4.4	sāvitrīm anvāha paccho 'rdharcaśaḥ sarvām iti tṛtīyam
2.6.4.5	atha svādhyāyam adhīyīta ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāny atharvāṅgiraso brāhmaṇāni kalpān gāthā nārāśaṃsīr itihāsapurāṇānīti
2.6.4.6	yad ṛco 'dhīte payasaḥ kūlyā asya pitṝn svadhā upakṣaranti yad yajūṃṣi ghṛtasya kūlyā yat sāmāni madhvaḥ kūlyā yad atharvāṅgirasaḥ somasya kūlyā yad brāhmaṇāni kalpān gāthā nārāśaṃsīr itihāsapurāṇānīty amṛtasya kūlyāḥ
2.6.4.7	sa yāvan manyeta tāvad adhītyaitayā paridadhāti namo brahmaṇe namo astv agnaye namaḥ pṛthivyai nama oṣadhībhyo namo vāce namo vācaspataye namo viṣṇave bṛhate karomi iti
2.6.4.8	ata ūrdhvaṃ devayajñaḥ sarveṣām upadiśyate
2.6.4.9	yatrātmāvirodhena pratiniyatānām oṣadhīnāṃ kodravacīnarājamāṣamamūrakulatthavarakavarjaṃ nirvapāṇi yavānāṃ taṇḍulānāṃ prātaḥ patnīṃ dadyāt
2.6.4.10	svayaṃ vātha śrapayet
2.6.4.11	susaṃmṛṣṭagṛhadvāropalepanaḥ pratiniyataḥ sāyaṃprātaḥ anyadāvaśyakān kuryāt agnaye jātavedase svāhā ity agnau tūṣṇīṃ dvitīyam
2.6.4.12	ud u tyaṃ jātavedasam ity ādityam upatiṣṭhate
2.6.4.13	brahmaṇe nama iti brahmasthale baliṃ haret
2.6.4.14	somāya ity udakumbhe vāyava iti vāstugṛhe gṛhapataya iti gṛhadvāri prajāpataya iti garbhagṛhe viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ iti devagṛhe śaṃ no devīḥ ity abhriṇyādikṣu tat puruṣebhya iti pratidiśaṃ gṛhebhya ity antarikṣe sarvataḥ paśūnāṃ pataye namo devebhya iti prāgudīcyāṃ brahmasthale vā svadhā pitṛbhya iti dakṣiṇe nidadhāti
2.6.4.15	anena vā pūrvoktena vāsabaliharaṇena vā balim
2.6.5.1	vaiśvadevaṃ hutvā ā gordohamātrakṣaṇam ākāṅkṣed atithīn
2.6.5.2	śrotriyo vedavratī yatir dharmanaiṣṭhikaḥ samānavṛttiḥ
2.6.5.3	manasvatyāhutis tasya prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate / dvyahaṃ tryahaṃ vā vicchinne pramādād akṛteṣu ca
2.6.5.4	tisras tantumatīr hutvā catasro vāruṇīr yajet / daśāhaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ vā vicchinneṣu tu sarvaśaḥ
2.6.5.5	catasro 'bhyāvartanīr hutvā kāryas tāntumataś caruḥ / yasya strī vānupeto vā gṛheṣv agnibaliṃ haret
2.6.5.6	kūśmāṇḍyas tatra hotavyo hutvā yajñasamṛddhaye / pravāsaṃ gacchato yasya gṛhe kartā na vidyate
2.6.5.7	pañcānāṃ mahatām eṣāṃ sa yajñaiḥ saha gacchati / pravāse kurute cainān yad annam upapadyate
2.6.5.8	na ced utpadyate cānnam adbhir enā samāviśet / adbhir eva vrataṃ kuryād yathālābham anuvratam
2.6.5.9	devānāṃ devayajñena dvijo gacchati sāmyatām / pitṝṇāṃ pitṛyajñena bhūtānāṃ yajñabhūtikaiḥ
2.6.5.10	manor manuṣyayajñena brahmaṇo brahmayajñataḥ / eteṣāṃ sāmyatāṃ gatvā daivatānāṃ śataṃ samāḥ ānandaṃ brahma gacchanti dhruvaṃ śāśvatam avyayam iti
2.6.5.11	athāsyātithir bhavati guroḥ samānavṛttir vaikhānaso yadi snātako vā rājā vā dharmayuktaḥ
2.6.5.12	teṣām abhyutthāyāsanaṃ pādyam arhaṇam arghyaṃ prayacchati
2.6.5.13	yās tatra oṣadhayaḥ santi tā deyāḥ
2.6.5.14	anyāṃ vā prakriyāṃ prakurvīta
2.6.5.15	oṣadhivibhāgas tu vibhavavatā kāryaḥ
2.6.5.16	abhāve bhūmir udakaṃ tṛṇāni kalyā vāg iti etāni vai sato 'gāre na kṣīyante kadācana iti
2.6.5.17	tān etān paraṃ brahmety ācakṣate
2.6.5.18	teṣāṃ grahaṇe dvādaśarātraṃ vrataṃ cared akṣāralavaṇabhojanam adhaśśayanaṃ brahmacaryam
2.6.5.19	trirātropoṣitaḥ utkṣepaṇau parau gṛhṇīyāt
2.6.5.20	baliharaṇaṃ vyākhyātam
2.6.6.1	atha madhuparkaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.6.6.2	catvāri pātrāṇi kāṃsyaturyāṇi dadhi madhu ghṛtaṃ kūrcatrayaṃ ca vāsasī kuṇḍalayugmaṃ ca darbheṣu sādayitvā darbhair apidadhāti
2.6.6.3	tiraḥpavitraṃ prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtyemāni prokṣya pavitrāntarhite pātre 'pa ānīyotpūya arhaṇīyārthān nidhāyaivam eva pādyam evam evācamanīyakaṃ kaṃse tiraḥpavitraṃ dadhi madhu ghṛtam ānīya punarāhāraṃ trir utpūya madhuparkārthān nidhāyācāryaśvaśurapitṛvyamātulasnātakātithirājabhyo dadyāt
2.6.6.4	vivāhe varāya
2.6.6.5	athādbhyaḥ karmaṇi ca dadyād ayaṃ kūrca iti kūrcam
2.6.6.6	tasmin prāṅmukha upaviśati rāṣṭrabhṛd asy ācāryāsandī mā tvad yoṣam iti
2.6.6.7	athāsmai kūrcābhyāṃ parigṛhyārhaṇīyaṃ dadyād arhaṇīyam udakam iti
2.6.6.8	tad abhimantrayate ā mā gāt tejasā varcasā yaśasā saṃsṛja payasā ca iti
2.6.6.9	tad añjalinopasaṃgṛhya prāk sektavā ity uktvā prāñcaṃ visṛjati
2.6.6.10	evam eva pādyaṃ dadyāt pādyam udakam iti
2.6.6.11	tad abhimantrayate yaśo 'si yaśo mayi dhehi rāṣṭram asi rāṣṭraṃ mayi dhehi iti
2.6.6.12	tenāsya pādāv anyaḥ prakṣālayati
2.6.6.13	avanektuḥ pāṇiṃ saṃmṛśati mayi maho mayi bhargo mayi yaśaḥ iti
2.6.6.14	upaspṛśya mayīndriyaṃ vīryam ity ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati
2.6.6.15	ācamanīyam udakam iti
2.6.6.16	tenācāmati amṛtopastaraṇam asi iti
2.6.6.17	ācamya athāsmai madhuparkaṃ dadyād ayaṃ madhuparka iti
2.6.6.18	tad abhimantrayate sa māvatu sa mā pātu sa mā juṣatām iti
2.6.6.19	vāsasī kuṇḍale ca dadyāt
2.6.6.20	svāmā tanūr āviśa ity ahataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāyaivamāsaṃgyaṃ kuṇḍale ca gṛhya yajñopavītaṃ kṛtvāpa ācamya madhuparkaṃ gṛhṇāti śrīr asy ehi mayi śrayasva iti
2.6.6.21	tad aṅguṣṭhena mahānāmyā copasaṃgṛhyāvajighrati prāṇemaṃ te baliṃ harāmi śraiṣṭhyaṃ ma ādhipatyaṃ gamaya iti
2.6.6.22	apa upaspṛśya aṅgulībhiḥ samudāyutyācāmati priyatamo nāmāsi devayādur mahyaṃ tvā śriyai yaśase gṛhṇāmi iti
2.6.6.23	somo 'si somapaṃ mā kuru iti dvitīyam
2.6.6.24	annam asy annādaṃ mā kuru iti tṛtīyam
2.6.6.25	pītvocchiṣṭaṃ nidhāya amṛtāpidhānam asi ity ācamanīyenācamya upavītaṃ gām abhimantrayate jahi me pāpmānam upavettuś ca iti
2.6.6.26	tāmudvā sṛjata kuruteti vā brūyāt
2.6.6.27	yady utsṛjati tām abhimantrayate gaur dhenur bhavyā iti dvābhyām
2.6.6.28	tasyām utsṛṣṭāyāṃ meṣam ajaṃ vālabhate
2.6.6.29	āraṇyena vā māṃsena
2.6.6.30	na tv evāmāṃso 'rghyaḥ syāt
2.6.6.31	aśaktau vā yavasaktumiśram odanaṃ yathālābhaṃ dadyāt
2.6.7.1	pañca yajñān tataḥ kṛtvā brahmayajñādyanukramāt / devayajñaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pitṛyajñaṃ tataḥ param
2.6.7.2	bhūtayajñaṃ ca kṛtvā tu yajñaṃ mānuṣyam eva ca / kṛtvaivaṃ pañcadhā yajñān yathāśāstrānusārataḥ
2.6.7.3	gomayaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā gṛhadvāre tu deśataḥ / patitāya śunādibhyaḥ piṇḍān samyaṅ nivedayet
2.6.7.4	devavihitāṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā gomayena gocarmamātraṃ caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya
2.6.7.5	kṣatriyasya trikoṇam upalipya vaiśyasya vṛttam upalipya bhojanaṃ kurute
2.6.7.6	brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca śrīrhutāśana eva ca / maṇḍalenopajīvanti tasmāt kurvīta maṇḍalam
2.6.7.7	yātudhānāḥ piśācāśca yakṣarākṣasakinnarāḥ / ghnanti vai balam annasya maṇḍalena vivarjitam iti
2.6.7.8	vacanāt prayatnato maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvārdrapādaḥ prāṅmukha upaviśya bhūmau savyaṃ pādaṃ pratiṣṭhāpyādhomukho vāgyataḥ parṇamayaṃ vā kāṃsyamayaṃ vā pātraṃ savyena hastena saṃspṛṣṭvā snehalavaṇavyañjanādyannenājyenākūro dātavyaḥ
2.6.7.9	tato bhoktavyam ity āhuḥ
2.6.7.10	udakyādibhir na darśitam annam
2.6.7.11	darśanamātre ā mastakād ā hṛdayād vā dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim uddharet
2.6.7.12	ājyenābhighārayati
2.6.7.13	athodakena pradakṣiṇaṃ pariṣiñcati
2.6.7.14	ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmi iti sāyam
2.6.7.15	satyaṃ tvartena pariṣiñcāmi iti prātaḥ
2.6.7.16	pāṇiṃ prakṣālyānnasūktenānnam abhimṛśati aham asmi prathamajā ṛtasya iti daśarcena sūktena
2.6.7.17	atha apa ācāmayati amṛtopastaraṇam asi iti
2.6.7.18	atha prāṇāhutīr juhoti prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo mā viśāpradāhāya prāṇāya svāhā iti prāṇāya
2.6.7.19	apāne niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo mā viśāpradāhāya apānāya svāhā ity apānāya
2.6.7.20	vyāne niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo mā viśāpradāhāya vyānāya svāhā iti vyānāya
2.6.7.21	udāne niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo mā viśāpradāhāya udānāya svāhā ity udānāya
2.6.7.22	samāne niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo mā viśāpradāhāya samānāya svāhā iti samānāya
2.6.7.23	prāṇāya svāhā apānāya svāhā vyānāya svāhā udānāya svāhā samānāya svāhā iti vā
2.6.7.24	etā āhutīr hutvā yathākāmaṃ bhuṅkte mūlaphalādivyañjanāni na dantena khādet
2.6.7.25	pādoddhṛtāni sarvāṇi snehadravyāṇi vyañjanāni
2.6.7.26	punaḥ punaḥ pānenāsti doṣaḥ
2.6.7.27	dadhnā havirmiśrena trivṛtānnena yathākarma hutvāthāpa ācamya amṛtāpidhānam asi ity ācāntaḥ punar ācamya prāṇānāṃ granthir asi sa mā visrasa iti nābhideśam abhimṛśati
2.6.7.28	evaṃ bhojane bhojane kurvan ahorātropavāsaphalam aśnute
2.6.7.29	yadi śayanam icchen nodakchirā na vaṃśavaśo na dvārāya pādābhyāṃ na parvaṇe notsaveṣu na bhasi ca na grahāyatanabhūtāyatanāgnyāyataneṣu na nagno nāśuciḥ na sandhyayor na viśīrnakhaṭvāyāṃ na śmaśānāyatanamahāvṛkṣacchāyāsu nānyat pramādam astīti manyate
2.6.7.30	prākchirā dakṣiṇaśirā vā saṃviśed iti
2.6.8.1	athāparāhṇe tāmramayaṃ vā mṛṇmayaṃ vā kamaṇḍalum ādāya grāmāt prācīm udicīṃ vā diśam upaniṣkramya tīrthe gatvodakaṃ gṛhītvā śucau deśe śaucārthe mṛdaṃ parigṛhya nasiktaṃ napurīṣaṃ noṣaraṃ navalmīkaṃ naśarkarāmiśraṃ naśāḍvalamiśraṃ karṇasthabrahmasūtraḥ pavitram asi iti tṛṇair avakīrya teṣu mūtrapurīṣaṃ visṛjati
2.6.8.2	na cityāṃ na nadyāṃ na śāḍvalopavanadivyacchāyāsu na pathi na bhasmani na kṣetramadhye kṛṣṇe na gomaye na śmaśānamahāvṛkṣavalmīkacchāyāsu
2.6.8.3	divāsandhyayor udaṅmukhaḥ rātrau ced dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ
2.6.8.4	śiśnaṃ gṛhītvotthāya yathā gandhalepakṣayakaraṃ tathātandritaḥ śaucaṃ kuryāt
2.6.8.5	ekayā ca kamaṇḍalum upaspṛśya prakṣālya pāṇipādau cācamya oṃkāraṃ manasā dhyātvā śucir bhavet
2.6.8.6	athāstaṃgate 'rke adbhir mārjayate dadhikrāviṇṇo 'kāriṣam iti
2.6.8.7	athāpo 'śnāti agniś ca mā manyuś ca ity etenānuvākena
2.6.8.8	apa ācamyādbhir mārjayate āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ
2.6.8.9	tūṣṇīṃ pradakṣiṇam udakena pravartayet
2.6.8.10	athāñjalinodakamādāyotthāyādityābhimukhas tiṣṭhan praṇavena vyāhṛtībhiḥ saha gāyatryābhimantrya trir ūrdhvaṃ prakṣipet
2.6.8.11	tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt
2.6.8.12	athopaviśyādbhis tarpayate dhātāraṃ tarpayāmi / aryamṇaṃ tarpayāmi / mitraṃ tarpayāmi / varuṇaṃ tarpayāmi / aṃśumantaṃ tarpayāmi / bhagaṃ tarpayāmi / indraṃ tarpayāmi / vivasvantaṃ tarpayāmi / pūṣaṇaṃ tarpayāmi / parjanyaṃ tarpayāmi / tvaṣṭāraṃ tarpayāmi / viṣṇuṃ tarpayāmi iti
2.6.8.13	athodakasamīpe darbhair avakīryopaviśya pavitrapāṇiḥ pratyaṅmukha upaviśya gāyatrīṃ manasāvāhayet
2.6.8.14	āyātu varadā devy akṣaraṃ brahmasammitam / gāyatrī chandasāṃ mātedaṃ brahma juṣasva naḥ / ojo 'si saho 'si balam asi bhrājo 'si devānāṃ dhāma nāmāsi viśvam asi viśvāyuḥ sarvam asi sarvāyuḥ abhibhūr oṃ gāyatrīm āvāhayāmi / sāvitrīm āvāhayāmi / sarasvatīm āvāhayāmi / ity āvāhya oṃ bhūḥ oṃ bhuvaḥ oṃ suvaḥ oṃ mahaḥ oṃ janaḥ oṃ tapaḥ oṃ satyaṃ oṃ tat savitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt ity etam anuvākaṃ trir abhyasya trīn prāṇāyāmān dhārayitvā nakṣatrāṇām udayāt pūrvaṃ praṇavena vyāhṛtībhiḥ saha sāvitrīṃ sahasrakṛtva āvartayet śatakṛtvo vā daśāvaraṃ vā
2.6.8.15	atha devīm udvāsayet uttame śikhare iti
2.6.8.16	athotthāya vāruṇīṃ diśam upatiṣṭhate yac ciddhi te viśo yathā iti tisṛbhiḥ imaṃ me varuṇa śrudhī havam iti dvābhyām
2.6.8.17	dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anuparyāvṛtya dakṣiṇāṃ diśam upatiṣṭhate yamāya dharmarājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca / vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhūtakṣayāya ca / audumbarāya dadhnāya nīlāya parameṣṭhine / vṛkodarāya citrāya citraguptāya vai namaḥ / iti
2.6.8.18	evam eva uttarāṃ diśam upatiṣṭhate ṛtaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ brahma puruṣaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam / ūrdhvaretaṃ virūpākṣaṃ viśvarūpāya vai namaḥ / iti
2.6.8.19	evam eva paryāvṛtya pratyaṅmukhaḥ sthitvā yad apsu te sarasvati goṣv aśveṣu yan madhu / tena me vājinīvati mukham aṅgdhi sarasvati iti mukham abhimṛśati
2.6.8.20	piśaṅgabhṛṣṭim aṃbhṛṇaṃ piśācam indra saṃvṛṇu / sarvaṃ rakṣo nibarhaya iti skandham abhimṛśati
2.6.8.21	trīṇi pradakṣiṇāni kṛtvābhivādanaṃ karoti
2.6.8.22	evaṃ prātaḥsandhyām upāsyāpośanakāle sūryaś ca māmanyuś ca ity etenānuvākenābhimantrya prāśnāti
2.6.8.23	prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhan sāvitrīṃ japet
2.6.8.24	prācīṃ diśam upatiṣṭhate mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛta iti tisṛbhiḥ
2.6.8.25	prasiddhaṃ snānaṃ kṛtvā madhyāhne sandhyām upāsya āpaḥ punantu pṛthivīm ity apo 'śnāti
2.6.8.26	athodakam ādāya ā satyena ity abhimantryordhvaṃ prakṣipyādityam upatiṣṭhate ud v ayaṃ tamasas pari ud u tyaṃ citram iti tisṛbhiḥ tac cakṣur devahitaṃ ya udagāt iti dvābhyāṃ ca
2.6.8.27	diśopasthānam eva
2.6.8.28	snānavidhiyuktena vā saṃtiṣṭhate sandhyopāsanaḥ santiṣṭhate iti
2.7.1.1	punarupanayanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.7.1.2	agurorucchiṣṭabhakṣī madhumāṃsabhakṣī bhavati
2.7.1.3	sandhyākārya udakumbhe 'gnikārye ciralopī bhavati
2.7.1.4	aguroḥ pretam anugacched dahed vā
2.7.1.5	ubhayatra daśāhāni kulānyannavejañca brahmacaryakṣatir bhavati
2.7.1.6	etaiś cānyaiś ca nimittāni bhavanti cet pūrvapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre gomayena gocarmamātraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya yamaniyamayantraiḥ vratopavāsaiś ca prāyaścittaṃ kṛtvā agnim upasamādhāya samparistīryā daṇḍapradānāt pūrvavadupanayanaṃ kṛtvā sāvitrīṃ vācayati
2.7.1.7	bhikṣāṃ na kurvann aśnāti na ca śmaśrūṇi vāpanam / śiromuṇḍaṃ na kurvan na vāsasaḥ paridhāpanam
2.7.1.8	nālaṅkāraṃ tataḥ kurvan brahmasūtrasya dhāraṇam / mekhalādhāraṇaṃ caiva na caivāmbaradhāraṇam
2.7.1.9	na cābhimantraṇaṃ kurvan nājinasya ca dhāraṇam / na pradānaṃ ca daṇḍasya na bhaikṣācaraṇaṃ tathā
2.7.1.10	vāsaso grahaṇaṃ nāsti vratopanayanaṃ tathā / evaṃ hi vidhivat kṛtvā pūto bhavati mānavaḥ
2.7.1.11	punaḥsaṃskāraṃ kṛtvā pūto bhavati
2.7.1.12	tad ahar eva sāvitrīvrataṃ kṛtvā tad ahar eva visṛjed ity āha
2.7.2.1	yaḥ pāṇigrahādir agnis tam aupāsana ity ācakṣate
2.7.2.2	tasmin gṛhyāṇi karmāṇi kriyante
2.7.2.3	tasyaupāsanenāgnihotritvaṃ yathā pārvaṇena carūṇāṃ darśapūrṇamāsayājitvam
2.7.2.4	tasmān nityo dhāryo 'nugato manthyaḥ śrotriyāgārād vāhāryaḥ
2.7.2.5	upavāsaś cānugate bhāryāyāḥ patyur vā
2.7.2.6	etāś cāhutīr juhuyāt mitrāya svāhā varuṇāya svāhā somāya svāhā sūryāya svāhā agnaye svāhā agnaye tapasvate janadvate pāvakavate svāhā agnaye śucaye svāhā agnaye jyotiṣmate svāhā agnaye vratapataye svāhā iti vyāhṛtībhir vihṛtābhiḥ samastābhiś ca
2.7.2.7	atha yadi dvyahaṃ tryahaṃ vā sāyaṃprātarvicchinno bhavati agnaye tantumate juhuyāt
2.7.2.8	yadi sthālīpākasyātipātanaṃ bhavati agnaye pathikṛte agnaye vaiśvānarāya vā juhuyāt
2.7.2.9	asyāpi vyākhyātāv āgrayaṇapiṇḍapitṛyajñau
2.7.2.10	dvādaśāhāni vicchinnaḥ punarādheyaḥ pratisaṃkhyāya vā homān juhuyāt
2.7.2.11	punarādhānaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.7.2.12	pariśrite uddhatyāvokṣya sikatopopta udumbaraśākhābhiḥ plakṣaśākhābhiḥ pālāśaśākhābhir vā pracchādya yājñikāt kāṣṭhād agniṃ mathitvā śrotriyāgārād vāhṛtya sate kṛtvā prajvalayitvā śākhām apohya oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaroṃ pratiṣṭha iti nyupyopasamādadhāti
2.7.2.13	vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā tisras tantumatīr juhoti tantuṃ tanvan udbudhyasvāgne trayastriṃśat tantavaḥ iti
2.7.2.14	atha catasro 'bhyāvartanīr juhoti agne 'bhyāvartin agne aṅgiraḥ punar ūrjā saha rayyā iti
2.7.2.15	etāṃ prājāpatyāṃ manasvatīṃ sāptapatīṃ ca hutvā dve mindāhutī juhoti yan ma ātmano mindābhūt punar agniś cakṣur adāt iti
2.7.2.16	prāyaścittīyāṃ juhoti ayāś cāgner anabhiśastīś ca satyamitvamayā asi / ayasā manasā dhṛto 'yasā havyam ūhiṣe ayāno dhehi bheṣajaṃ svāhā iti
2.7.2.17	daśahotāraṃ manasānudrutya sagṛhaṃ hutvā imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti ca
2.7.2.18	atraike jayābhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛta ity upajuhvati
2.7.2.19	yathā purastād brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svastyayanam ṛddhim iti vācayitvā prasiddha āgneyaḥ sthālīpākaḥ
2.7.2.20	atra gurave varaṃ dadāti vāsasī dhenum anaḍvāhaṃ vā
2.7.2.21	yadi pravased oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ iti upasthāya pravaset
2.7.2.22	yadi prayāyād vyākhyātam ātmany araṇyoḥ samāropaṇam upāvarohaṇaṃ ca
2.7.2.23	samidhi vā samāropanam upāvarohaṇaṃ ca
2.7.2.24	samidhi vā samāropayed araṇīkalpena
2.7.2.25	yatra vāsas tasmin śrotriyāgārād agnim āhṛtya ājuhvānaḥ udbudhyasva iti dvābhyām avadhāya paristīrya yasyāṃ samārūḍhatām ādadhāti
2.7.2.26	vyākhyāto homakalpaḥ
2.7.3.1	atha gṛhasthasya dve bhārye
2.7.3.2	agnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryājyaṃ vilāpya utpūya sruksruvau niṣṭapya sammṛjya sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvānvārabdhāyāṃ patnyāṃ yajamāno juhoti namastarṣe gada / avyavāyai tvā svadhāyai tvā / mā na indrābhitastvadṛṣvāriṣṭāsaḥ / evā brahman tavedastu svāhā iti
2.7.3.3	athainam agniṃ samāropayate ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti
2.7.3.4	samāropya pūrvāgnau samidham ādhāya ājuhvānaḥ udbudhyasva iti dvābhyāṃ saṃparistīryājyaṃ vilāpyotpūya sruksruvau niṣṭapya saṃmṛjya sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvānvārabdhayoḥ patnyoḥ yajamāno juhoti yo brahmā brahmaṇa ujjahāra ity etena sūktenaikaikaśaś caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā
2.7.3.5	ā praṇītābhyaḥ kṛtvā catuśśarāvam odanaṃ śrapayitvābhighāryodañcam udvāsya pratiṣṭhitam abhighārayati
2.7.3.6	paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti
2.7.3.7	samitaṃ saṃkalpethām iti puronuvākyām anūcya agne purīṣyādhipā bhavā tvaṃ na iti yājyayā juhoti
2.7.3.8	adhājyāhutīr upajuhoti purīṣyas tvam agne ity āntād anuvākasya
2.7.3.9	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.7.3.10	saṃtiṣṭhate aupāsanatantraḥ saṃtiṣṭhate aupāsanatantraḥ
2.7.4.1	atha gṛhyaprāyaścittāni juhoti anugate 'gnau kālātikrame homayoḥ darśapūrṇamāsayoś ca āgrayaṇam akṛtvā navānnaprāśane 'kṛtasīmantāyāṃ prasūtāyāṃ bhāryāyāṃ strīṣu goṣu ca yamalajanane parāgamane rajasvalāgamane divāmaithune kumārasyājātasaṃskāre mantraviparyāse karmaviparyāse brahmacāriṇo vrataviparyāse mekhalācchedane daṇḍabhinne yajñopavītasyādhāraṇe sandhyālope agnikāryalope udakumbhalope ity etaiś cānyaiś ca kalpadṛṣṭam agnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīrya ghṛtaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā pāhi no agna enase svāhā iti
2.7.4.2	purastāc copariṣṭāc ca mahāvyāhṛtībhir hutvā etad evāsya prāyaścittam avicchinnakaraṇaṃ saṃtataṃ bhavatīti
2.7.4.3	upanayanāgnir vivāhāgniḥ sūtakāgniḥ śmaśānāgnir ā caturahād ā daśāhād ā saṃcayanād udvātaḥ syāt apahatā asurā rakṣāṃsi piśācā ye kṣayanti pṛthivīm anu / anyatreto gacchantu yatraiṣāṃ gataṃ manaḥ ity adbhir avokṣya kṣipraṃ bhasmasamāropaṇam
2.7.4.4	ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti śrotriyāgārād agnim āhṛtya ājuhvānaḥ udbudhyasva iti dvābhyām avadhāya paristīrya pariṣicya prāyaścittaṃ juhoti ayāś cāgneḥ pañcahotāraṃ brāhmaṇa ekahotāraṃ manasvatīmindāhutīvyāhṛtībhiḥ
2.7.4.5	athāpivā caturahaḥsadyaskālaṃ brahmacaryaṃ vicchinatti sārasvatena homena manasvatīmindāhutīmahāvyāhṛtīnāṃ sapraṇavaṃ juhuyāt
2.7.5.1	atha brahmacāryavakīrṇī bhavati yo 'yonau retaḥpātena vā sandhyālopena vodakumbhalopenāgnikāryalopena vā
2.7.5.2	anyāni nimittāni bhavanti cecchuklam anārdram ācchādya kṛtopavāsaḥ kṛtaniyamayantro 'māvāsyāyāṃ rātryām agnim upasamādhāya vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā dvirājyasyopaghātaṃ juhoti kāmāvakīrṇo 'smy avakīrṇo 'smi kāmakāmāya svāhā kāmābhidrugdho 'smy abhidrugdho 'smi kāmakāmāya svāhā iti
2.7.5.3	punar māmaitv indriyam ity etam anuvākam aṣṭaśatam ājyasya juhuyāt
2.7.5.4	yad devā devahelanam ity etam anuvākaṃ pratyṛcam ājyasya juhuyāt
2.7.5.5	vāruṇyādijayāprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
2.7.5.6	gurave gāṃ dadāti
2.7.5.7	atha svapne śuklaṃ pated vāsāṃsi visṛjyānyat paridadhāti
2.7.5.8	upavyuṣasi grāmāt prācīm udīcīṃ diśam upaniṣkramya nadīṣu snāyāt
2.7.5.9	samudragānadīsnānāt trirātraṃ phalam aśnute / samudragānadīsnānāt pakṣopoṣaṇameva ca
2.7.5.10	saritpates tvam āvāsyāmanantamayane viṣau
2.7.5.11	ity evaṃ snānaṃ yathāvidhi tathā karoti
2.7.5.12	punar māmaitv indriyam ity etenānuvākena japtvā pūto bhavatīty āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.7.6.1	athartusnānād bhartur mukhe nānvīkṣamāṇā prayatnād vāharmukhaṃ darśayet na tad ahaḥ saṃveśanaṃ kuryāt
2.7.6.2	yadi saṃveśayet
2.7.6.3	tad ahar jāyate putraḥ so 'lpāyur dhanavarjitaḥ / pañcamyāṃ tu śramed yā vā vandhyāṃ nārīṃ prasūyate
2.7.6.4	ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tu yā śramet sādhvī putrapautravatī bhavet / saptamyāṃ tu tathā nārī aṣṭamyāṃ ṣaṇmukhopamaḥ
2.7.6.5	paripriyā navamyāṃ tu daśamyāmuttamaḥ sutaḥ / ekādaśyāṃ tu duṣṭātmā dvādaśyāṃ tu dhaneśvaraḥ
2.7.6.6	trayodaśyāṃ tu daurbhāgyā caturdaśyaghavān sutaḥ / labhet pativratāṃ nārīṃ pañcadaśyāṃ tathaiva ca
2.7.6.7	ṣoḍaśyāṃ labhate putraṃ brahmakīrtiṃ natādṛśam / tadūrdhvopayamaṃ nāsti kāmabhogaiva kevalam
2.7.6.8	tasmāt sarvaprayatnena ṣoḍaśyantaṃ pratiśramet / śuklotkarṣe labhet putraṃ śoṇitasya sriyaṃ labhet
2.7.6.9	nindite'hani saṃveśaṃ na kuryāttu prayatnataḥ / yadi pramādāt kuryāccejjapet tāṃ vaiṣṇavīmṛcam
2.7.6.10	keśavādīni nāmāni japettu vividhāni ca / agnyagāre tato gatvā hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ
2.7.6.11	evaṃ janmatrayaṃ vāpi śravaṇaṃ ca na saṃviśet / parvadvaye ca tatkuryāt śrāddhaṃ dattvā na vāhani
2.7.6.12	somavāre'rkavāre ca bhaumavāre śanaiścare / viṣuve ayane caiva vyatīpāte ca saṅkrame
2.7.6.13	etānyanyāni nindyāni divasāni na saṃviśet / viṣṭiraṣṭamyathānye ca pakṣacchidrāstathaiva ca
2.7.6.14	ṣoḍaśe dvādaśe vāpi pañcadaśyāṃ tathaiva ca / caturdaśyāṃ navamyāṃ ca ṣaṣṭhyāmaṣṭama eva ca
2.7.6.15	etānyanyatamaṃ vīkṣya śaucaṃ kuryādyathoditam / abhivīkṣya sunakṣatraṃ puṇyaṃ caiva grahodayam
2.7.6.16	prakṣālya pāṇipādau dvāvācamya manasā harim / dhyātvā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam
2.7.6.17	asyā dakṣiṇahastena bhagaṃ caiva pradarśayet / śivena tvābhimṛśāmīti śiśnaṃ yonau praveśayet
2.7.6.18	ekayā ṛṣabheṇeti ṛcā samyaganīkṣaṇaḥ
2.7.6.19	yathā ratyantaṃ kṛtvā tathā śaucaṃ kṛtvā paścājjaped ṛcaḥ samyak ā te yonim iti
2.7.6.20	ya evaṃ jñātvābhimṛśati sa satputraṃ labhate budhaḥ
2.7.6.21	evam eva māsi māsi ṛtuvelāyāṃ kṛtvā putraṃ cārubuddhimantaṃ baliṣṭhaṃ labhate baliṣṭhaṃ labhata ity āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.7.7.1	brahmakūrcaṃ pravakṣyāmi kāyaśodhanamuttamam / vedādijayahomaṃ ca mantrahīnamasaṃskṛtam
2.7.7.2	śudrānnabhojane caiva vedānāṃ vikrayeṣu ca / kākaśvānāvalīḍhe cotkaṇṭhake mṛgapakṣiṇām
2.7.7.3	pañcamamlecchasaṃsparśe pañcagavyaṃ viśodhanam / nīlavarṇyāstu gomūtraṃ kṛṣṇāgomayamuddharet
2.7.7.4	tāmravarṇīpayaścaiva śvetāyā dadhireva ca / kapilāyā ghṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam
2.7.7.5	alābhe sarvavarṇānāṃ kapilādekāttu grāhyakam / gomūtraikapalaṃ dadyādaṅguṣṭhārdhaṃ tu gomayam
2.7.7.6	kṣīraṃ saptapalaṃ dadyād dadhi tripalameva ca / ghṛtamekapalaṃ dadyāt tathaiva ca kuśodakam
2.7.7.7	sāvitryā grāhya gomūtraṃ gandhadvāreti gomayam / āpyāyasveti ca kṣīraṃ dadhikrāvṇṇa iti vai dadhi
2.7.7.8	ājyaṃ śukramasītyevaṃ devasya tvā kuśodakam
2.7.7.9	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva ity āloḍya mā nastoke ity abhimantrya praṇavenoddhṛtya praṇavena nirmathya praṇavenaiva pibet
2.7.7.10	agnaye somāya irāvatī idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrame mā nas toke prajāpate gāyatrīṃ ca hutvā madhyamena palāśaparṇena padmapatreṇa tat pibet
2.7.7.11	yat tvagasthigataṃ pāpaṃ dehe tiṣṭhati māmake / brahmakūrcodakāt sarve dahatyagnirivendhanam iti
2.7.8.1	athāto naimittikāni prāyaścittāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.7.8.2	sarvatra vaiṣṇavarcaṃ japet viṣṇor nu kaṃ vīryāṇi pravocam iti
2.7.8.3	atha karmāntare yadi kṣudhed vā niṣṭhīved vā sahasraśīrṣā puruṣa iti japati
2.7.8.4	apa upaspṛśyāṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ dakṣiṇakarṇam upaspṛśet
2.7.8.5	yadi mūtraṃ kuryāt pādau prakṣālyācamya oṃkāraṃ manasā dhyātvā śucir bhūtvā puruṣa evedaṃ sarvam iti dve ṛcau japet
2.7.8.6	yadi mehet pūrvavacchaucaṃ kṛtvā tripād ūrdhva udait puruṣa iti tisra ṛco japet
2.7.8.7	yady aśucisparśe śuddhajalāśaye snātvāpa ācamya tasmād yajñāt sarvahuta iti catasra ṛco japet
2.7.8.8	yadi caṇḍālapatitādidarśe apa ācamya ādityam abhivīkṣya brāhmaṇo 'sya mukham āsīt / bāhū rājanyaḥ kṛtaḥ / ūrū tad asya yad vaiśyaḥ / padbhyāṃ śūdro ajāyata / candramā manaso jātaḥ / cakṣoḥ sūryo ajāyata iti tisra ṛco japet
2.7.8.9	yadi homo madhye vicchinnaḥ syād vedāham etaṃ puruṣaṃ mahāntam iti tisra ṛco japet
2.7.8.10	dve mindāhutī hutvā punaḥ śeṣaṃ samāpayet
2.7.8.11	yadi pātrāṇi śunādyavalīḍhe dārumayāny agnau prakṣipet mṛṇmayāni cāpsu prakṣipet lohamayāni bhasmanā śudhyanti
2.7.8.12	anyāni navāni pātrāṇi saṃgṛhya viṣṇo tvaṃ no antamaḥ viṣṇor nu kaṃ vīryāṇi pravocam iti dve ṛcau japet
2.7.8.13	yan ma ātmano mindābhūt punar agniś cakṣur adāt imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi tvaṃ no agne iti ṣaḍ āhutīr juhuyāt
2.7.8.14	yady agnim udakyādyavalīḍhe agnim udvāsya pūrvavat śaucaṃ kṛtvā agniṃ mathitvā laukikaṃ vāhṛtya srauksruvau niṣṭapya saṃmṛjya sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā pūrṇāhutiṃ hutvā pūrvavat saṃskāraṃ karoti
2.7.8.15	yady araṇy aśucir bhaved anyām āhṛtyaiva caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā puruṣasūktena manasānudrutya juhoti
2.7.8.16	yadi sūtako mṛtako bhavet tanmadhye homaṃ na karoti sthālīpākaṃ ca tāny ahāni
2.7.8.17	vyatīpāte tad dravyaṃ brāhmaṇāya dadātīty āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.7.9.1	athāto gṛhyāṇi prāyaścittāni smaryante tāni vakṣyāmaḥ
2.7.9.2	śeṣāṇi vaitānikāni
2.7.9.3	ya āhitāgner dharmas sa dharmo ya āhitāgneḥ lokas sa aupāsanikasya iti śāṭyāyanīyaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ bhavati
2.7.9.4	tatra ye puroḍāśās ta iha caravaḥ
2.7.9.5	payodadhipṛṣadājyānām ājyavat saṃskāro na dadhno 'dhiśrayaṇaṃ pratyasanaṃ prativeṣaṇam adbhī raudrarākṣasapaitṛkanairṛtacchedanabhedananirasanātmābhimarśanāni ca kṛtvā apa upaspṛśet
2.7.9.6	sarvatra skanne bhinne kṣāme dagdhe viparyāse 'ntarite ca dve mindāhutī juhuyāt yan ma ātmano mindābhūt punar agniś cakṣur adād iti
2.7.9.7	skanne santvā siñcāmi iti skannam abhimantryāpohyāvasicya bhūḥ ity upasthāya askān dyauḥ pṛthivīm iti dve āhutī juhuyāt
2.7.9.8	ājyaṃ ced devāñjanavanaspatim aṃhasa iti cānumantrya kiñcic ca dadyāt
2.7.9.9	atha bhinne bhūmir bhūmnā iti bhinnam abhimantrya unnambhaya pṛthivīm ity apohyāvasicya trayastriṃśat tantava ity etayā juhuyāt
2.7.9.10	agnau prakṣiped dārumayāṇi
2.7.9.11	atha kṣāme nirṛtyai tvā iti dagdham abhimantrya kiñcit tvaṃ parācī tvam avācī tvaṃ rakṣāṃsi gaccha iti dakṣiṇāparam uttarāparaṃ vā diśaṃ pratinirasya agnī rakṣāṃsi sedhati iti tisra ājyāhutīr juhuyāt
2.7.9.12	haviṣām abhigamanasyaikadeśaṃ ced uddhṛtya tat kṛtvaitayā juhuyāt
2.7.9.13	etenāśṛtaduḥśṛtau vyākhyātau
2.7.9.14	apo 'bhyavaharet
2.7.9.15	rudrāya tvā ity aśṛtam abhimantrya yamāya tvā iti duḥśṛtam atha paristaraṇadāhe agnaye kṣāmavate namo namaḥ kṣāmavan mā mā hiṃsīḥ mā me gṛhaṃ mā me dhanaṃ mā me paśūn ity abhimantrya agnaye kṣāmavate svāhā iti juhuyāt
2.7.9.16	indraṃ vo viśvatas pari iti punaḥ paristirya indrāya svāhā iti juhuyāt
2.7.9.17	atha paridhidāhe pradāvyāyāgnaye namo namaḥ pradāvyāya iti
2.7.9.18	samānam ata ūrdhvam agneḥ samid asi iti paścārdhaṃ yamasya samid asi iti dakṣiṇārdham somasya samid asi ity uttarārdham
2.7.9.19	indhānās tvā śataṃ hi mā iti dve āhutī juhuyāt
2.7.9.20	juṣṭe 'nyaṃ paridadhyāt gandharvo 'si iti pratimantram
2.7.9.21	atha viparyāse tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agne tvam agne ayāsi prajāpate iti catasra āhutīr juhuyāt
2.7.9.22	etā evāntarite mano jyotiḥ iti pañcamīm antaritaṃ ca kuryāt
2.7.9.23	saṃsthite cet kiñcic ca dadyāt
2.7.9.24	uttarasmin kāla āgate homaś ced anivṛttaḥ pūrvasya seyaṃ kālātipattis tasyāṃ prāyaścittaṃ mano jyotiḥ iti pūrvasya juhuyāt
2.7.9.25	tathāparasya juhuyāt
2.7.9.26	evaṃ pratihomam ā daśarātrāt prāṇāyāmaḥ
2.7.9.27	ekādaśīprabhṛtyā viṃśatirātrād upavāsas triṃśadrātrād ata ūrdhvaṃ prājāpatyaṃ vihitam
2.7.9.28	ekādaśīprabhṛti tisras tantumatīr dvādaśāhāni vicchinnaḥ punarādheya ity uktam evaṃ vā
2.7.9.29	atha parvaṇy atīte mano jyotiḥ ayāś cāgne yad asmin svasti na indra iti catasra āhutīr hutvāgnaye pathikṛte sthālīpākaṃ kuryāt prāg aṣṭamāt
2.7.9.30	ata ūrdhvaṃ sopavāsaḥ kāryaḥ
2.7.9.31	dve triṣu ca tisra ity evam atīteṣu prāyaścittaṃ pārvaṇavaddhomaḥ pitṛyajñe 'tīte pakṣadvaye copavāsaḥ kārya iti siddham
2.7.9.32	atha mahāyajñānām ekasminn ahani mano jyotiḥ iti dvayos triṣu caturṣu pañcasu vā ṣaṭsu prabhṛtīti tisras tantumatīr hutvā catasro vāruṇīr japet imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmi yat kiñca ava te heḍa ity ā navarātrāt
2.7.9.33	ata ūrdhvam ā daśarātrāc catasro 'bhyāvartinīr juhuyāt
2.7.9.34	sarveṣām antato vyāhṛtībhir iti siddham
2.7.10.1	ata ūrdhvaṃ vānaprasthavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.7.10.2	anavadyaṃ gṛhadharmaṃ caritvā yajñān yajati
2.7.10.3	putram utpādya saṃskṛtya vedam adhyāpya vṛttiṃ vidhāya guṇavati putre kuḍumbabhāraṃ niyojya uttarāyaṇe pūrvapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre kuśacīracarmavalkalavāsā jaṭī kṛṣṇājinottarīyaḥ kṛtaprasthānaliṅgo 'gnim ātmasamāropaṇaṃ kṛtvā sapatnīko vāpyapatnīko vā vanam āśrayet
2.7.10.4	śramaṇam agnim ādhāya veṇuśyāmākanīvārādibhir āraṇyamūlaphalair oṣadhībhiḥ sāyaṃprātar agniṃ paricaret
2.7.10.5	phālākṛṣṭābhiḥ devabrāhmaṇapitṛbhūtamanuṣyayajñān ahar ahar hutvāraṇyor vā kāle śaktitaḥ śarīraṃ pariśoṣayed yamaniyamamantropavāsādibhiḥ
2.7.10.6	jīrṇaparṇāhāraḥ dantolūkhalikaḥ śailakuṭṭo ye kāla āgaccheyus tebhyo 'pi dadyāt
2.7.10.7	sthaṇḍilaśāyī ūrdhvaretāḥ atithipriyaḥ amatsarī vivādapaiśunyamṛṣāvādavarjī sadāśuciḥ grāmasya chadiṃ na darśed araṇyavāsapriyo 'bhayadāyī sarvabhūtānāṃ parair abhimṛṣṭāny āśramāntarahitāni nābhyavahared ekāgniparāyaṇaḥ apramādī sabījāṃ proṣitāṃ bhūmiṃ nākramet
2.7.10.8	tapo'dhikāya yajñādhikāya vayo'dhikāya phalodakaṃ dadyāt
2.7.10.9	evaṃ mṛgaiḥ saha caritvāparispandyasahavāsī svakālaṃ vyapohya svargalokaṃ gamiṣyatīti
2.7.10.10	athavā tṛtīyam āyurbhāgaṃ vānaprasthavrataṃ caritvā caturtham āyurbhāgaṃ parivrajed vā
2.7.11.1	athātaḥ saṃnyāsavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
2.7.11.2	udagayana āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre pūrvakālam upoṣya saṃbhārān upakalpayate
2.7.11.3	kāṣāyavāsasī plakṣapavitrapādukāsanavaiṇavadaṇḍaśikyakamaṇḍalvalābupātraṃ kuśabandham ity evamādisaṃbhārān upakalpayate
2.7.11.4	agnim āropya vanād grāmaṃ praviśya keśaśmaśrūṇi vāpayitvā nadīṣu snāyāt śuddhe jalāśaye vā
2.7.11.5	apa ācamya nadītīre devagṛhe vā brāhmaṇān abhigamyākrodhano 'dveṣaṇaḥ sarvakarmāṇi saṃnyaset
2.7.11.6	na vedaṃ saṃnyaset
2.7.11.7	vedasaṃnyāsācchūdro bhavati
2.7.11.8	tasmād vedaṃ na saṃnyaset
2.7.11.9	brāhmaṇasannidhau mantram uktvāpaḥ pibet saṃnyastaṃ mayā iti
2.7.11.10	gṛhasthenopanītān vaiṇavāntān saṃbhārān parigṛhya savitṛmaṇḍalam udvīkṣamāṇaḥ saṃnyastaṃ mayā iti trir uccaiḥ prabrūyāt
2.7.11.11	atha brāhmaṇaṃ nivītaṃ bahuyājinam abhigamya daṇḍān dātavā ity uktvā daṇḍān parigṛhya kṛtanāmānikṛto 'nujñāto yater dharmān samyak paricaret nityaśikhī nityayajñopavītī nityasandhyopāsī nityaprātaḥsnāyī nityaṃ bhaikṣāśī nityaṃ yamaniyamayantravratopavāsī nityam īśvaropāsī nityaṃ godevagṛhavāsī apagatabhayakāmakrodhalobhamohamadamātsaryaḥ iti
2.7.11.12	evamādidharmaṃ caritvā svargalokaṃ gamiṣyati
2.7.11.13	athavā brāhmaṇeṣu kṣīyamāṇeṣu pūrvavacchaucaṃ kṛtvā sarvakarmāṇi saṃnyasya praiṣaṇam apo 'śnāti
2.7.11.14	īśvaram evopāsya pūto bhavatīty āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
2.7.11.15	### 3 ###
3.1.1.1	amāvāsyāyām aparāhṇe māsikam aparapakṣasya vāyukṣv ahassu pitṛbhyo 'nnaṃ saṃskṛtya dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān āsanāni kalpayitvā brāhmaṇān śucīn mantravataḥ samāṅgān ayugmān āmantrayate
3.1.1.2	yonigotramantrasambandhān arthāpekṣo na bhojayet
3.1.1.3	agnim upasamādhāya dakṣiṇāprāgagrair darbhaiḥ paristīrya ekapavitrāntarhitāyām ājyasthālyām ājyaṃ nirupya saṃskṛtya tataḥ apasavyaṃ pariṣiñcati
3.1.1.4	audumbaram idhmam abhyādhāya audumbaryā darvyā juhoti
3.1.1.5	ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā prācīnāvītī pitṝn āvāhayati āyāta pitaraḥ saumyā gambhīraiḥ pathibhiḥ pūrvyaiḥ prajām asmabhyaṃ dadato rayiṃ ca dīrghāyutvaṃ ca śataśāradaṃ ca iti
3.1.1.6	etām eva diśam abhy apaḥ prasiñcati āpo devīḥ prahiṇutāgnim ete yajñaṃ pitaro no juṣantām / āsīnām ūrjam uta ye bhajante te no rayiṃ sarvavīrān niyacchatāt iti
3.1.1.7	vyāhṛtiparyantaṃ kṛtvā prācīnāvītī juhoti somāya pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ svāhā / yamāyāṅgirasvate pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ svāhā / yāḥ prācīḥ saṃbhavanty āpa uttarataś ca yāḥ / adbhir viśvasya bhuvanasya bhartrībhir antaranyaṃ pitur dadhe svadhā namaḥ svāhā / antardadhe parvatair antar mahyā pṛthivyā / divā digbhir anantābhir ūtibhir antaranyaṃ pitāmahād dadhe svadhā namaḥ svāhā / antardadha ṛtubhiḥ sarvair ahorātraiḥ sasandhibhiḥ / ardhamāsaiś ca māsaiś cāntaranyaṃ prapitāmahād dadhe svadhā namaḥ svāhā
3.1.1.8	atha nāmadheyair juhoti amuṣmai svadhā namo 'muṣmai svadhā nama iti
3.1.1.9	yan me mātā pralulobha caraty ananuvratā tan me retaḥ pitā vṛṅktām ābhur anyo 'vapadyatāṃ svadhā namaḥ svāhā
3.1.1.10	evaṃ dvitīyam
3.1.1.11	tathā tṛtīyam
3.1.1.12	yan me pitāmahī yan me prapitāmahī iti mantraṃ saṃnamati
3.1.2.1	ye ceha pitaro ye ca neha yāṃś ca vidma yāṁ u ca na pravidma / agne tān vettha yadi te jātavedas tayā prattaṃ svadhayā madanti kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā / yad vaḥ kravyād aṅgam adahal lokānanayan praṇayan jātavedāḥ / tad vo 'haṃ punar āvedayāmy ariṣṭāḥ sarvair aṅgaiḥ saṃbhavantu pitaraḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā / vahājyaṃ jātavedaḥ pitṛbhyo yatraitān vettha nihitān parāke / ājyam asya kūlyā upa tāṃ kṣarantu satyā eṣām āśiṣaḥ santu kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā
3.1.2.2	evaṃ dvitīyaṃ tathā tṛtīyam
3.1.2.3	pitāmahebhyaḥ prapitāmahebhya iti mantraṃ saṃnamati
3.1.2.4	evam annasya juhoti
3.1.2.5	vahānnam iti mantraṃ saṃnamati
3.1.2.6	atha sauviṣṭakṛtīṃ juhoti agnaye kavyavāhanāya sviṣṭakṛte svadhā nama iti
3.1.2.7	dakṣiṇārdhapūrvārdhe hutvānuprahṛtya darvīm athānnam abhimṛśati pṛthivī te pātraṃ dyaur apidhānaṃ brahmaṇas tvā mukhe juhomi brāhmaṇānāṃ tvā vidyāvatāṃ prāṇāpānayor juhomy akṣitam asi mā pitṝṇāṃ kṣeṣṭhā amutrāmuṣmin loke pṛthivīṃ samantas same 'gnir upadraṣṭā dattasyāpramādāya ṛcas te mahimā / pṛthivī te pātraṃ dyaur apidhānaṃ brahmaṇas tvā mukhe juhomi brāhmaṇānāṃ tvā vidyāvatāṃ prāṇāpānayor juhomy akṣitam asi mā pitāmahānāṃ kṣeṣṭhā amutrāmuṣmin loke 'ntarikṣaṃ samantas same vāyur upaśrotā dattasyāpramādāya yajūṃṣi te mahimā / pṛthivī te pātraṃ dyaur apidhānaṃ brahmaṇas tvā mukhe juhomi brāhmaṇānāṃ tvā vidyāvatāṃ prāṇāpānayor juhomy akṣitam asi mā prapitāmahānāṃ kṣeṣṭhā amutrāmuṣmin loke dyauḥ samantas same ādityo 'nukhyātā dattasyāpramādāya sāmāni te mahimā iti
3.1.2.8	brāhmaṇān upasparśayati
3.1.2.9	bhuktavato 'nuvṛttyā śeṣam anujñāpya
3.1.3.1	udakumbhaṃ darbhamuṣṭiṃ cādāya dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān paristīrya teṣv avācīnapāṇir dakṣiṇāpavargāṃs trīn udapātrān upari ninayati mārjayantāṃ pitaraḥ saumyāsaḥ mārjayantāṃ pitāmahāḥ saumyāsaḥ mārjayantāṃ prapitāmahāḥ saumyāsaḥ iti
3.1.3.2	asāv avaneniṅkṣva asāv avaneniṅkṣva iti vā teṣv avācīnapāṇir dakṣiṇāpavargān trīn piṇḍān dadāti
3.1.3.3	etat te tata asau iti pitre piṇḍaṃ dadāti etat te pitāmaha asau iti pitāmahāya etatte prapitāmaha asau iti prapitāmahāya
3.1.3.4	tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
3.1.3.5	sa kṛtākṛto vā
3.1.3.6	yadi nāmadheyāni na vidyāt svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pṛthivīṣadbhya iti pitre piṇḍaṃ dadāti
3.1.3.7	svadhā pitāmahebhyo 'ntarikṣasadbhya iti pitāmahāya
3.1.3.8	svadhā prapitāmahebhyo diviṣadbhya iti prapitāmahāya
3.1.3.9	atrāñjanābhyañjane vāsaś cānupiṇḍaṃ dadāti
3.1.3.10	āṅkṣvāsāv āṅkṣvāsau iti trir āñjanam
3.1.3.11	abhyaṅkṣvāsāv abhyaṅkṣvāsau iti trir abhyañjanam
3.1.3.12	etāni vaḥ pitaro vāsāṃsy ato no 'nyat pitaro mā yoḍhum etāni vaḥ pitāmahā vāsāṃsy ato no 'nyat pitāmahā mā yoḍhum etāni vaḥ prapitāmahā vāsāṃsy ato no 'nyat prapitāmahā mā yoḍhum iti daśām ūrṇāstukāṃ vā chittvā nyasyati pūrve vayasi svaṃ loma chittvā uttare
3.1.3.13	atha pātraṃ saṃkṣipya ninayati putrān pautrān abhitarpayantīr āpo madhumatīr imāḥ
3.1.3.14	svadhāṃ pitṛbhyo 'mṛtaṃ duhānā āpo devīr ubhayāṃs tarpayantu iti
3.1.3.15	nyubjapātraṃ pāṇī vyatyasya namo vaḥ pitaro rasāya iti ṣaḍbhir namaskārair upatiṣṭhate
3.1.3.16	udakāntaṃ gatvā trir udakāñjalidānenodakāñjalīn dadāti eṣa te tata pitur madhumāṁ ūrmiḥ sarasvān yāvān agniś ca pṛthivī ca tāvaty asya mātrā tāvān asya mahimā tāvantam enaṃ bhūtaṃ dadāmi yathāgnir akṣito 'nupadasta evaṃ me tatāya pitre 'kṣito 'nupadastaḥ svadhā bhavatāṃ tvaṃ svadhām akṣitaṃ taiḥ sahopajīvāsau ṛcas te mahimā eṣa te pitāmaha pitur madhumāṁ ūrmiḥ sarasvān yāvān vāyuś cāntarikṣaṃ ca tāvaty asya mātrā tāvān asya mahimā tāvantam enaṃ bhūtaṃ dadāmi yathā vāyur akṣito 'nupadasta evaṃ me pitāmahāya pitre 'kṣito 'nupadastaḥ svadhā bhavatāṃ tvaṃ svadhām akṣitaṃ taiḥ sahopajīvāsau yajūṃṣi te mahimā
3.1.3.17	eṣa te prapitāmaha pitur madhumāṁ ūrmiḥ sarasvān yāvān ādityaś ca dyauś ca tāvaty asya mātrā tāvān asya mahimā tāvantam enaṃ bhūtaṃ dadāmi yathādityo 'kṣito 'nupadastaḥ evaṃ me prapitāmahāya pitre 'kṣito 'nupadastaḥ svadhā bhavatāṃ tyaṃ svadhām akṣitaṃ taiḥ sahopajīvāsau sāmāni te mahimā iti
3.1.3.18	pratyetya pratiṣṭhitam udapātreṇāpa upapravartayati parāyāta pitaraḥ saumyā gambhīraiḥ pathibhiḥ pūrvyaiḥ prajām asmabhyaṃ dadato rayim
3.1.3.19	atha māsi punar āyāta no gṛhān havir attuṃ suprajasaḥ suvīrāḥ iti
3.1.3.20	etena arghyāvarṣaṃ vyākhyātatantram
3.1.3.21	māṃsaṃ niyataṃ māṃsābhāve śākam
3.2.1.1	aṣṭakāṃ kariṣyamāṇa upakalpayate ukṣāṇaṃ vā vehataṃ vrīhīn annaṃ madhuś ca sarpiś ca
3.2.1.2	prasiddhaṃ śaucam
3.2.1.3	anūrādhāyām agnim upasamādhāya paristīryāpareṇāgniṃ vrīhīn ekapavitro 'tha nirvapati imam apūpaṃ catuśśarāvaṃ nirvapāmi kleśāpahaṃ pitṝṇāṃ saṃparāye / devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ pitṛbhyas tvā juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi iti pitṛbhyas tvā pitṛbhyas tvā ity evaṃ catuśśarāvaṃ nirvapati
3.2.1.4	prokṣya tūṣṇīṃ haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjya yathā puroḍāśam evam evaitam apūpaṃ padakapālam adhiśrayati
3.2.1.5	ekakapālaṃ vā
3.2.1.6	śṛte tasminn ājyaṃ dadhi vilāpyotpūyātha pariṣiñcati adite 'numanyasva iti dakṣiṇataḥ prācīnam anumate 'numanyasva iti paścād udīcīnaṃ sarasvate 'numanyasva iti uttarataḥ prācīnaṃ deva savitaḥ prasuva iti sarvataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ pariṣicyāghārāv āghārya ājyabhāgau juhoti
3.2.1.7	ājyena prāyaścittaṃ juhoti yā tiraścī nipadyase 'haṃ maryādā vidharaṇī iti / tāṃ tvā ghṛtasya dhārayā juhomi vaiśvakarmaṇīṃ kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.1.8	athaitasyāpūpasya madhyād avadāyopastīrṇābhighāritam audumbaryā darvyā juhoti
3.2.1.9	apūpaṃ juhoti ghṛtavantam adya svadhāvantaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇāya vaha havyaṃ pitṛbhya āhutīr juhomi kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.2.1	atha purastād dakṣiṇato 'vadāya paścād varṣīyo juhoti iyam eva sā yā prathamā vyaucchad antarasyāṃ carati praviṣṭā / vadhūr jajāna navagarjjanitrī traya enāṃ mahimānaḥ sacante kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.2.2	tṛtīyāṃ juhoti aulūkhalā grāvāṇo ghoṣam akrata apaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ kṛṇvantaḥ parivatsarīṇām / ekāṣṭake suprajā vīravanto vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.2.3	caturthīṃ juhoti yāṃ janāḥ pratinandanti rātriṃ dhenum ivāyatī / saṃvatsarasya yā nī patnī sā no astu sumaṅgalā kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.2.4	pañcamīṃ juhoti prajāpate na tvad etāny anyo viśvā jātāni paritā babhūva / yatkāmās te juhumas tan no astu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇāṃ kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.2.5	ṣaṣṭhīṃ juhoti yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricaṃ yad vā nyūnam ihākaram / agniṣ ṭat sviṣṭakṛd vidvān sarvaṃ sviṣṭaṃ suhutaṃ karotu me agnaye sviṣṭakṛta suhutahute sarvahute sarvaprāyaścittāhutīnāṃ kāmānāṃ samardhayitre kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.2.6	darvīṃ prakṣālya nidhāya tathaiva parimṛjya pariṣicya piṇḍāvṛtaitān piṇḍān dattvātraitam apūpaṃ ghṛtavantaṃ madhumantaṃ śraddhābhimarśanenābhimṛśati
3.2.3.1	pṛthivī te pātraṃ dyaur apidhānaṃ brahmaṇas tvā mukhe juhomi brāhmaṇānāṃ tvā vidyāvatāṃ prāṇāpānayor juhomy akṣitam asi mā pitṝṇāṃ kṣeṣṭhā amutrāmuṣmin loke pṛthivī samantas same 'gnir upadraṣṭā dattasyāpramādāya ṛcas te mahimā / pṛthivī te pātraṃ dyaur apidhānaṃ brahmaṇas tvā mukhe juhomi brāhmaṇānāṃ tvā vidyāvatāṃ prāṇāpānayor juhomy akṣitam asi mā pitāmahānāṃ kṣeṣṭhā amutrāmuṣmin loke 'ntarikṣaṃ samantas same vāyur upaśrotā dattasyāpramādāya yajūṃṣi te mahimā / pṛthivī te pātraṃ dyaur apidhānaṃ brahmaṇas tvā mukhe juhomi brāhmaṇānāṃ tvā vidyāvatāṃ prāṇāpānayor juhomy akṣitam asi mā prapitāmahānāṃ kṣeṣṭhā amutrāmuṣmin loke dyauḥ samantas same ādityo 'nukhyātā dattasyāpramādāya sāmāni te mahimā ity etena
3.2.3.2	brāhmaṇān vidyāvataḥ pariviśati
3.2.3.3	pariviśyodakāya gatvodakāñjalidānenodakāñjalīn dadāti eṣa te tata pitur madhumāṁ ūrmis sarasvān yāvān agniś ca pṛthivī ca tāvaty asya mātrā tāvān asya mahimā tāvantam enaṃ bhūtaṃ dadāmi yathāgnir akṣito 'nupadastaḥ evaṃ me tatāya pitre 'kṣito 'nupadastaḥ svadhā bhavatāṃ tvaṃ svadhām akṣitaṃ taiḥ sahopajīvāsāv ṛcas te mahimā
3.2.4.1	eṣa te pitāmaha pitur madhumāṁ ūrmis sarasvān yāvān vāyuś cāntarikṣaṃ ca tāvaty asya mātrā tāvān asya mahimā tāvantam enaṃ bhūtaṃ dadāmi yayā vāyur akṣito 'nupadasta evaṃ me pitāmahāya pitre 'kṣito 'nupadastaḥ svadhā bhavatāṃ tvaṃ svadhām akṣitaṃ taiḥ sahopajīvāsau yajūṃṣi te mahimā / eṣa te prapitāmaha pitur madhumāṁ ūrmis sarasvān yāvān ādityaś ca dyauś ca tāvaty asya mātrā tāvān asya mahimā tāvantam enaṃ bhūtaṃ dadāmi yathādityo 'kṣito 'nupadasta evaṃ me prapitāmahāya pitre 'kṣito 'nupadastaḥ svadhā bhavatāṃ tvaṃ svadhām akṣitaṃ taiḥ sahopajīvāsau sāmāni te mahimā iti
3.2.4.2	etāvad etat tadahaḥkarma bhavati
3.2.4.3	etaddhasma vai tadvidvāṃsaḥ pūrva ṛṣaya evam aṣṭakyam apūpaṃ catuśśarāvam evam akalpayaṃs tena vai te pitṝn atarpayaṃs ta enāṃs tṛptāḥ prajayā paśubhir atarpayaṃs tato ha pitṛbhir mitram akurvata mitraṃ hy eṣāṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny āsan
3.2.4.4	sa yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān etam aṣṭakyam apūpaṃ catuśśarāvam evaṃ kalpayati
3.2.4.5	tena vai sa pitṝṃs tarpayati yena tṛptāḥ prajayā paśubhis tarpayanti
3.2.4.6	ato ha pitṛbhir mitraṃ kurute
3.2.4.7	mitraṃ hy asya sarvāṇi bhūtāni bhavanti
3.2.4.8	ya evaṃ vidvān etam aṣṭakyam apūpaṃ catuśśarāvam evaṃ kalpayati
3.2.5.1	śvo jyeṣṭhāyām agnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīrya tathaiva pariṣicyāghārāv āghāryājyabhāgau juhoti
3.2.5.2	prāyaścittīyāṃ hutvopākaraṇīyāṃ juhoti imāṃ pitṛbhyo gām upākaroty ūrjasvatīṃ svadhāvatīṃ tan me juṣantāṃ pitaraḥ paretāḥ / sā me pitṝn saṃparāye dhinotu kāmaiḥ svāhā iti
3.2.5.3	athaibhyo gām upākaroti pitṛbhyas tvā juṣṭām upākaromi iti
3.2.5.4	athaināṃ prokṣati pitṛbhyas tvā juṣṭāṃ prokṣāmi iti
3.2.5.5	tām atraiva pratīcīnaśirasaṃ dakṣiṇāpadīṃ saṃjñapayanti
3.2.5.6	tasyai saṃjñaptāyā adbhiḥ prāṇān āpyāyayati tūṣṇīm
3.2.5.7	athāsyai vapām uddhṛtya viśālayopatṛṇatti tūṣṇīm eva
3.2.5.8	athāsyai hṛdayam uddhārayanti prajñāte ca matasne
3.2.5.9	tāny eteṣv eva śūleṣu saṃpraṇīkṣyaitasminn evāgnau śrapayanti
3.2.5.10	śṛteṣu tredhā vapāṃ vicchidyodumbaradarvyā upastīrṇābhighāritāṃ juhoti vaha vapāṃ jātavedaḥ pitṛbhyo yatraitān vettha nihitān parāke / medasaḥ kūlyā upa tān kṣarantu satyā eṣām āśiṣaḥ santu kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.5.11	athaitasya māṃsasyopastaraṇābhighāritaudumbaryā darvyopaghātaṃ juhoti
3.2.6.1	ekāṣṭakāṃ paśyata dohamānām annaṃ māṃsavad ghṛtavat svadhāvat / tad brāhmaṇair atipūtam anantam akṣayyaṃ sphītiṃ gacchatu kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.6.2	dvitīyāṃ juhoti ekāṣṭakā tapasā tapyamānā saṃvatsarasya patnī duduhe prapīnā / tāṃ doham upajīvātha pitaraḥ sahasradhā mucyamānāṃ kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.6.3	tṛtīyāṃ juhoti ekāṣṭakā tapasā tapyamānā jajāna garbhaṃ mahimānam indram / tena dasyūn vyasahanta devā hantāsurāṇām abhavacchacībhiḥ kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.6.4	caturthīṃ juhoti aulūkhalā grāvāṇa iti
3.2.6.5	pañcamīṃ juhoti yāṃ janāḥ pratinandanti iti
3.2.6.6	ṣaṣṭhīṃ juhoti prajāpate iti
3.2.6.7	saptamīṃ juhoti yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti
3.2.6.8	darvīṃ prakṣālya nidhāya tathaiva pariṣicya piṇḍāvṛtaitān piṇḍān dattvā śraddhābhimarśanenābhimṛśati pṛthivī te pātram ity etena
3.2.6.9	brāhmaṇān vidyāvataḥ pariviśati
3.2.6.10	pariviśyodakāya gatvodakāñjalidānenodakāñjaliṃ dadāti eṣa te tata pituḥ iti
3.2.6.11	etāvad evaitadahaḥkarma bhavati
3.2.6.12	etaddhasma vaitadvidvāṃsaḥ pūrva ācāryā evam aṣṭakyāṃ gām evam akalpayaṃs tayā vaite pitṝn atarpayaṃs ta enāṃs tṛptāḥ prajayā paśubhir atarpayan tato ha pitṛbhir mitram akurvata mitraṃ hy eṣāṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny āsan
3.2.6.13	sa yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān etām aṣṭakyāṃ gām evaṃ kalpayati
3.2.6.14	tena vai sa pitṝṃs tarpayati
3.2.6.15	te yena tṛptāḥ prajayā paśubhis tarpayanti
3.2.6.16	ato ha pitṛbhir mitraṃ kurute mitraṃ hy asya sarvāṇi bhūtāni bhavanti
3.2.6.17	ya evaṃ vidvān etām aṣṭakyāṃ gām evaṃ kalpayati
3.2.7.1	tṛtīye 'hni bhūyo 'tha śrāddham annaṃ ca dhanaṃ ca kalpayitvāgnim upasamādhāya paristīrya tathaiva pariṣicyāghārāv āghāryājyabhāgau hutvājyena prāyaścittīyāṃ hutvāthaitasyānnasyopastīrṇābhighāritaudumbaryā darvyā juhoti vahānnaṃ jātavedaḥ pitṛbhyo yatraitān vettha nihitān parāke / annasya kūlyā upa tān kṣarantu satyā eṣām āśiṣaḥ santu kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.7.2	dvitīyāṃ juhoti saṃvatsarasya pratimāṃ yāṃ tvā rātry upāsate / prajāṃ suvīrāṃ kṛtvā viśvam āyur vyaśnuvat kāmaiḥ svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti
3.2.7.3	tṛtīyāṃ juhoti yāṃ janāḥ pratinandanti iti
3.2.7.4	caturthīṃ juhoti prajāpate iti
3.2.7.5	pañcamīṃ juhoti yad asya karmaṇo 'tyarīricam iti
3.2.7.6	anuprahṛtya darvīṃ tathaiva pariṣicya piṇḍāvṛtaitān piṇḍān dattvā śraddhābhimarśanenābhimṛśati pṛthivī te pātram ity etena
3.2.7.7	brāhmaṇān vidyāvataḥ pariviśati
3.2.7.8	pariviśyodakāya gatvodakāñjalidānenodakāñjaliṃ dadāti
3.2.7.9	eṣa te tata iti
3.2.7.10	etāvad evaitadahaḥkarma bhavati
3.2.7.11	etaddhasma vaitad vidvāṃsaḥ pūrve śrotriyā evam aṣṭakyam annam evam akalpayaṃs tena vaite pitṝn atarpayaṃs ta enāṃs tṛptāḥ prajayā paśubhir atarpayan tato ha pitṛbhir mitram akurvata mitraṃ hy eṣāṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny āsan sa yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān etam aṣṭakyam annam evaṃ kalpayati
3.2.7.12	tena vai sa pitṝṃs tarpayati
3.2.7.13	te yena tṛptāḥ prajayā paśubhis tarpayanti
3.2.7.14	ato ha pitṛbhir mitraṃ kurute mitraṃ hy asya sarvāṇi bhūtāni bhavanti
3.2.7.15	ya evaṃ vidvān tṛtīye 'hni yathāśraddham annaṃ ca dhanaṃ ca dadāti tato vai tasyāparimitānnadhanāḥ paśavo bhavanti
3.2.7.16	ya evaṃ vidvān tṛtīye 'hni yathāśraddham annaṃ dhanaṃ ca na dadāti tasyāparimitānnadhanā na vai paśavo bhavanti
3.3.1.1	athātaḥ śrāddhaśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
3.3.1.2	pūrvedyuḥ sāyam aupāsanaṃ hutvā prāṇān āyamya saṃkalpya śvaḥ pitṛbhyo māsiśrāddhaṃ kariṣya iti vā śvo yajñaśarmaṇaḥ nakṣatraśrāddhaṃ kariṣya iti vā śvo yajñaśarmaṇaḥ tripakṣaśrāddhaṃ kariṣya iti vā śvo yajñaśarmaṇaḥ ṣaṇmāsaśrāddhaṃ kariṣya iti vā śvo yajñaśarmaṇaḥ saṃvatsaraśrāddhaṃ kariṣya iti vā śvo yajñaśarmaṇaḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaśrāddhaṃ kariṣya iti vā saṃkalpya brāhmaṇān śucīn śrotriyān daridrān vedajñān samāṅgān agotrān asamānārṣeyān kṣaṇaṃ karoti
3.3.1.3	dvau viśvedevebhyaḥ trayaḥ pitṝṇām
3.3.1.4	sapiṇḍīśrāddhaṃ ced eko 'dhikam
3.3.1.5	pretaśrāddheṣv ekam eva varayet
3.3.1.6	śvaḥ pitṛbhyo māsiśrāddhaṃ bhavitavyaṃ tasya bhavatā prasādaḥ karaṇīya iti evam eva śvaḥ pitṛbhyo 'ṣṭakāśrāddhaṃ bhavitavyaṃ tasya bhavatā prasādaḥ karaṇīya iti śvaḥ pitṛbhyo nityaśrāddham ekoddiṣṭaṃ nakṣatraśrāddham iti sarvatroktvā gandhādibhir ārādhya tilapiṣṭādibhir bhakṣyadravyair yathāvakāśo 'sti tathārādhya tāmbūlādi dadyāt
3.3.1.7	śvobhūte prātaraupāsanaṃ hutvāvaṭau khanati
3.3.1.8	pretaśrāddheṣv ekam eva khanati
3.3.1.9	sapiṇḍīkaraṇe trīn khātvā avaṭe tiladarbhān prakīrya brāhmaṇān āhūya kṣaṇaṃ karoti
3.3.1.10	uttare 'vaṭe viśvedevayoḥ pādān prakṣālya madhyame pitṝṇāṃ dakṣiṇe pretasya pādau prakṣālya tān ārādhya tāmbūlaṃ dadyāt
3.3.1.11	pādaprakṣālanakrameṇa sarvaṃ kuryāt prācīnāvītī
3.3.1.12	aparāhṇe brāhmaṇabhojanārtham aupāsane sthālīpākaṃ kuryāt
3.3.1.13	pitṝṇām āvāhanakāle prācīnāvītī dakṣiṇābhimukhaḥ sthitvā āvāhya brāhmaṇān āhūya yathoktaṃ diṅmukham upaveśayati
3.3.1.14	yathāvidhi hutvā yatra yatrokteṣu piṇḍāvṛtaitān piṇḍān dadāti
3.3.1.15	pātrasādanakāle ekasmin pātre ā ma āgantu pitaro devayānān samudrān salilān savarṇān / asmin yajñe sarvakāmān labhante 'kṣīyamāṇam upaduhyantām imāṃ pitṛbhyo vo 'rghyaṃ gṛhṇāmi iti pitṛbhyaḥ pitāmahebhyo vo 'rghyaṃ gṛhṇāmi iti pitāmahebhyaḥ prapitāmahebhyo vo 'rghyaṃ gṛhṇāmi iti prapitāmahebhyaḥ athānyasmin pātre pretāya te gṛhṇāmi iti pretāya apa ānayati
3.3.1.16	tilo 'si somadevatyo gosave devanirmitaḥ / pratnavadbhiḥ prattaḥ svadha ehi pitṝn imān lokān prīṇayāhi naḥ svadhā namaḥ iti tilān āvapati
3.3.1.17	pitāmahān prapitāmahān imān lokān prīṇayāhi naḥ svadhā namaḥ iti ca
3.3.1.18	pretāya imān lokān iti ca
3.3.2.1	madhu vātā ṛtāyate madhu kṣaranti sindhavaḥ / mādhvīr naḥ santv oṣadhīḥ / madhu naktam utoṣasi madhumat pārthivaṃ rajaḥ / madhu dyaur astu naḥ pitā / madhumān no vanaspatir madhumāṁ astu sūryaḥ / mādhvīr gāvo bhavantu na iti madhv ānayati
3.3.2.2	kuśalavam ādāya somāsya tviṣir asi taveva me tviṣir bhūyād amṛtam asi mṛtyor mā pāhi didyon mā pāhy aveṣṭā dantaśūkā iti mathitvā nirastaṃ namuceḥ śiraḥ iti phenaṃ nirasya darbheṣu sādayitvā darbhaiḥ pracchādya śaṃ no devīḥ ity avokṣya gandhādibhir alaṅkṛtya svadhāṃ yatra guptaṃ manyate tatra nidadhāti
3.3.2.3	pūrvavat pādaprakṣālanaṃ kṛtvā yathodaṅmukhān upaveśya viśvedevān kṣaṇaṃ karoti viśvedevāḥ kṣaṇaḥ kartavya iti
3.3.2.4	prativacanam oṃ tathā ity uktvā prāpnotu bhavān ity āha prāpnavāni itītare pratyāhuḥ
3.3.2.5	māsiśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya iti māsi aṣṭakāśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya ity aṣṭakāsu nityaśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya iti nityaśrāddhe ekoddiṣṭaśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya ity ekoddiṣṭe nakṣatraśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya iti nakṣatre tripakṣaśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya iti tripakṣe ṣaṇmāsaśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya iti ṣaṇmāse saṃvatsaraśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya iti saṃvatsare sapiṇḍīkaraṇaśrāddhe kṣaṇaḥ kartavya iti sapiṇḍīkaraṇe prativacanam oṃ tathā ity uktvā prāpnotu bhavān ity āha prāpnavāni itītare pratyāhuḥ
3.3.2.6	tebhyo gandhādibhir ārādhya svadhāpātram ārādhya vastrayugmaṃ kuṇḍalam aṅgulīyakaṃ ca dattvāthānnam abhimṛśati pṛthivī te pātram iti
3.3.2.7	bhuñjānān samīkṣate prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi iti
3.3.2.8	brahmaṇi ma ātmāmṛtatvāya iti
3.3.2.9	pitṛliṅgaiḥ ṛgyajurbhiḥ śrāvayet
3.3.2.10	ācāntebhyas tilodakaṃ pradāya pavitraṃ pitṛhaste nidhāya svadhām ānayati pitṛbhyo haste svadhāstu iti
3.3.2.11	astu svadhā iti prativacanam
3.3.2.12	evaṃ pitāmahāyaivam prapitāmahāyaivaṃ pretāya
3.3.2.13	tathaiva śuddhodakaṃ pradāya astu śuddhodakam iti prativacanam
3.3.2.14	yathāśakti dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā annaśeṣaiḥ kiṃ kriyatām iti iṣṭaiḥ sahopabhujyatām iti prativacanam
3.3.2.15	pratyetya śeṣaṃ sagaṇaḥ prāśnāti
3.3.2.16	yadi nityaśrāddhaṃ kurvan śaśaṃ vā mṛgaṃ vā kūrmaṃ vopākaroti śrapayitvā hiraṇyena parikrīya vā yathāṣṭakāsu dvitīye 'hni tathā karoti
3.3.2.17	ekoddiṣṭavat tripakṣaśrāddhaṃ kurvanti
3.3.2.18	tripakṣavat ṣaṇmāsaśrāddhaṃ kurvanti
3.3.2.19	ṣaṇmāsavat saṃvatsaraśrāddhaṃ kurvanti
3.3.2.20	evam ā saṃvatsarāt pretasya dahananakṣatreṣv evam evaṃ kurvanti
3.4.1.1	athāto dahanavidhiḥ
3.4.1.2	āhitāgner anāhitāgneḥ striyāś caiva maraṇasaṃśaye śucau same deśe gomayenopalipya avokṣya sikatābhir avakīrya tāsu dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān saṃstīrya teṣu dakṣiṇāśirasam enaṃ nidhāyāsvadhāyuktāni brahmāṇy abhiśrāvayet āyuṣaḥ prāṇaṃ santanu iti
3.4.1.3	atha prāṇeṣūtkrānteṣu prācīnāvīty avācīnapāṇiḥ hiraṇyaśakalam āsye pratyasyāṅguṣṭhabandhaṃ prabadhya grāmyeṇālaṅkāreṇālaṅkṛtya pattodaśenāhatena vāsasā pracchādya sāyamāhutiṃ hutvā prātarāhutiṃ hutvā paurṇamāsyeneṣṭvāmāvāsyeneṣṭvātha gārhapatya ājyaṃ vilāpyotpūya sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā prāg udetya samidvaty āhavanīye juhoti mṛtyor adhiṣṭhānāya svāhā iti
3.4.1.4	caturo brāhmaṇān vāhayitvā grāmābhimukhena catuṣpathe nidhāya mukhaṃ darśayitvā śmaśānābhimukhena vāhayitvā śmaśānaṃ nirhṛtya sahāgnibhiḥ pretaṃ tatrainaṃ nidhāya dahanaṃ joṣayet dakṣiṇāpratyakpravaṇam abhaṅguram aniriṇam asuṣiraṃ samaṃ vā
3.4.1.5	apeta vīta vi ca sarpatāto ye 'tra stha purāṇā ye ca nūtanāḥ / ahobhir adbhir aktubhir vyaktair yamo dadātv avasānam asmai iti hariṇyā palāśaśākhayaudumbaraśākhayā vā sataṃ sammṛjya dakṣiṇataḥ śākhāṃ nirasya apa upaspṛśyādbhir avokṣya hiraṇyaśakalam avadhāya apasarpata pretā ye ke ceha pūrvajāḥ svasti naḥ kuruta māśrupātaḥ punar āgamat iti dakṣiṇāpavargāḥ sphyena paraśunā vā tisraḥ karṣūḥ khātvādbhir avokṣya tilataṇḍulānāṃ muṣṭiṃ pūrayitvā yamāya pitṛpataye pitṛbhyaḥ svadhā nama iti prathamāyāṃ nivapati
3.4.1.6	evaṃ dvitīyāyāṃ tathā tṛtīyāyām
3.4.1.7	śeṣāṃs tilataṇḍulān yady āhitāgnir bhavati tasya kṛṣṇājinaṃ chittvā dakṣiṇāgrīvam adharalomāstṛṇāti
3.4.1.8	etasmin kāle snātvodakenauṣadhībhiś ca kumbhaṃ pūrayitvā tena daśahotrā pattogrāt snāpayet
3.4.1.9	athāhataṃ vāsaḥ paridhāpyālaṅkṛtya tataś citām āropyātha saptaprāṇāyataneṣu sapta hiraṇyaśakalān pratyasyālābha ājyabindūn vā mukhe prathamam āsye dadhitaṇḍulāṃś ca tilāṃś ca juhoti idaṃ ta ātmanaḥ śarīramayaṃ ta ātmanas ta ātmānaṃ śarīrād brahma nirbhinadmi bhūr bhuvaḥ svar asau svargāya lokāya svāhā iti
3.4.1.10	daśahotāraṃ cittiḥ srug ityādi grahavarjam evam evāgre nāsikācchidrayor dvir japet
3.4.1.11	āsīd iti sarveṣu hotṛpadeṣv anuṣajaty anyatra ṣaḍḍhotṛpadebhyaḥ
3.4.1.12	āstām iti dvivacanādiṣu
3.4.1.13	caturhotāraṃ pṛthivī hotā iti mukhe sṛkkikaṭayor dviḥ pañcahotāram agnir hotā iti karṇayor dviṣ ṣaḍḍhotāraṃ sūryam ta iti kīkasāsu dvis saptahotāraṃ mahāhavir hotā iti
3.4.2.1	athājyāni gṛhṇīte darśapūrṇamāsavat tūṣṇīṃ juhvāṃ ghṛtaṃ dadhyupabhṛti dadhi madhu ghṛtam iti dhruvāyāṃ payo 'gnihotrahavaṇyām
3.4.2.2	api vājyam eva sarvāsu
3.4.2.3	atra pātrāṇy upacinoti
3.4.2.4	yāni pātrāṇy āsecanavanti tāni sampūrayitvābhyukṣatītarāṇy ariktatāyā iti vijñāyate
3.4.2.5	tasya dakṣiṇahaste juhūṃ sphyaṃ cādadhāti
3.4.2.6	savya upabhṛtam urasi dhruvām upaveṣam araṇīṃ ca mukhe 'gnihotrahavaṇīṃ nāsikayoḥ sruvāv ājyasruvau vā karṇayoḥ prāśitraharaṇaṃ bhittvaikaikam
3.4.2.7	hanvor ulūkhalamusale datsu grāvāṇo bhavanti
3.4.2.8	śirasi kapālāni
3.4.2.9	lalāṭa ekakapālam udare piṣṭasaṃyavanīṃ pātrīṃ nābhyām ājyasthālīṃ patta upāvaharaṇīyaṃ kūrcaṃ śirasta upasādanīyaṃ kūrcaṃ pārśvayoḥ śūrpaṃ chittvaikaikaṃ vā ghrāṇayoḥ sāṃnāyyakumbhyau yadi saṃnayan bhavati aṇḍayor dṛṣadupale śiśne vṛṣaravaṃ śamyāṃ ca pṛṣṭhayor agnihotrasthālīm anvāhāryasthālīm iḍāpātraṃ vedaṃ śikhāyām
3.4.2.10	athavāvaśiṣṭāny antareṇa sakthinī nivapati
3.4.2.11	tasya kṛṣṇājinaśeṣeṇa dakṣiṇāgrīvam uttaralomnā pracchādya bāndhavāḥ sigvātenopavījayanti
3.4.2.12	trayaḥ sigvātā bhavanti grāme pathi citāyāṃ ca
3.4.2.13	vātās te vāntu pathi puṇyagandhā manaḥśubhā gātraśubhā anulomāḥ / tvacassukhā māṃsasukhā asthisaukhyā vahantu tvā marutaḥ sukṛtāṃ yatra lokāḥ iti
3.4.3.1	yady āhitāgnir bhavati apa naḥ śośucad agham ity aṅguṣṭhabandhaṃ visṛjya patny udakumbham ādāyādhvaryur vā śīrṣann adhinidhāya trir apasalaiḥ pariṣiñcan paryeti
3.4.3.2	kiñcit paraśunā praharati
3.4.3.3	atha dhārām anumantrayate imā āpo madhumatyo 'smiṃs te loka upaduhyantām iti
3.4.3.4	dvitīyaṃ parigatāyāṃ paścāt praharati imā āpo madhumatyo 'ntarikṣe te loka upaduhyantām iti
3.4.3.5	tṛtīyaṃ parigatāyāṃ paścāt praharati imā āpo madhumatyaḥ svarge te loka upaduhyantām iti
3.4.3.6	bhinatti kumbham
3.4.3.7	yadi purastāt patati pāpīyān bhavati yadi paścāt patati vasīyān bhavati iti
3.4.3.8	atha kapālaśeṣā apaḥ pretasya prāṇasthāneṣu ninayati divi jātā apsu jātā iti
3.4.3.9	ārdrā oṣadhīr ālabhyottiṣṭhati
3.4.3.10	gāṃ paśyati
3.4.3.11	brāhmaṇān paśyati
3.4.3.12	hiraṇyam ālabhate
3.4.3.13	atra gurave varaṃ dadāti
3.4.4.1	athāsmā adhvaryur dakṣiṇapūrvasyāṃ diśy āhavanīyam ādīpayati nairṛtyām anvāhāryapacanaṃ vāyavyāṃ gārhapatyam uttarataḥ sabhyāvasakthyau
3.4.4.2	saṃbhāraiḥ agnir yajurbhiḥ patnībhiḥ senendrasya ity etaiḥ upoṣayet
3.4.4.3	grahaiḥ vācaspate vidhe nāman vācaspate vāco vīryeṇa somaḥ somasya vācaspate 'cchidrayā vācā vācaspate hṛdidhe nāman ity etaiḥ ṛtumukhīyena vāgghotā ity etena brāhmaṇa ekahotā iti copasthānam
3.4.4.4	āhavanīya ekeṣāṃ kapālaḥ
3.4.4.5	saṃtapanāgninā vājasaneyinaḥ samāmananti
3.4.4.6	tam abhinivartate yaṃ gharmo 'gnir abhijihartti yāṃ gatiṃ yānti yudhi yuddhaśūrā vidhṛtapāpā virajā viśokās tāṃ gatiṃ yāhi surabhir nākapṛṣṭhaḥ svadhā nama iti
3.4.4.7	yady anāhitāgnir bhavati yāṃ gatiṃ yānti yudhi yuddhaśurās tanutyajo mokṣavido manīṣinaḥ sukṛtino 'gnihotrahaviṣṭhās tāṃ gatiṃ yāhi surabhir nākapṛṣṭhaḥ svadhā nama iti
3.4.4.8	tato yajñopavītī saṃ tvā siñcāmi yajuṣā iti śāntiṃ kṛtvā jyotiṣmatyā ādityam upatiṣṭhate ud vayaṃ tamasas pari ud u tyaṃ citram iti
3.4.4.9	putrabhrātṛsapiṇḍāḥ saṃviśanti
3.4.4.10	anavekṣamāṇās tīrtham āyānti
3.4.4.11	rājapuruṣo vā tānasagotro vā parṇaśākhayā śamīśākhayaudumbaraśākhayā vārayati mā tarata iti
3.4.4.12	na punar āgamiṣyāmaha ity uktvāturavyañjanāni kṛtvā keśān saṃprakīrya pāṃsūn opyaikavāsaso 'hatavāsaso vā dakṣiṇāmukhāḥ sakṛd unmajjyottīrya savyaṃ jānuṃ bhūmau nidhāya vāsaḥ pīḍayitvotthāyāñjalinodakam ādāya tilamiśrā apastaṃ prati asāv etat ta udakam iti evaṃ dvitīyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ ca kṛtvā athāpratīkṣā grāmam āyānti
3.4.4.13	kaniṣṭhaprathamāḥ pipīlikā yānti
3.4.4.14	niveśanadvāre nimbapatraṃ prāśyāpa ācamya gomayaṃ hiraṇyam apo 'gniṃ sarṣapāṃs tailam ity upaspṛśya śiraḥ prāṇān saṃmṛśyāśmānam ākramya gṛhaṃ praviśya yat striya āhus tat kurvanti
3.4.4.15	yatra prāṇā utkrāntā bhavanti tasmin gomayenopalipya vatsaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya tilataṇḍulāny udakamiśrāṇi saṃprakīrya svasty astu gṛhāṇāṃ śeṣe śivam āstām iti pavanaṃ kṛtvāpakvāśī striyā ata ūrdhvaṃ brahmacaryam ā daśarātrāt
3.4.4.16	sāyaṃ prātaḥ sakṛd udakam utsicya daśame 'hani trir udakam utsicya daśamyāṃ vikṛtāhāram
3.4.5.1	athāto 'sthisaṃcayanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.4.5.2	anivṛtte 'gnaukaraṇe dvyahe tryahe caturahe pañcāhe saptāhe vā navakumbham ādāya śmaśānaṃ nītvā pālāśaśaṅkunā śamīśaṅkunaudumbaraśaṅkunā vāṅguṣṭhopakaniṣṭhikābhyāṃ vā sarvābhir aṅgulībhir vāsthīni samudāyutya kṣīreṇa plāvayitvā ghṛtaṃ ninayed idaṃ ta ātmanaḥ śarīram ayaṃ ta ātmā ātmanas ta ātmānaṃ śarīrād brahma nirbhinadmi bhūr bhuvaḥ svar asau svargāya lokāya svāhā iti
3.4.5.3	atha yadi na daheyur ulmukam ādāya punar dahed asmāt tvam adhijāto 'sy ayaṃ tvad adhijāyatām / agnaye vaiśvānarāya svargāya lokāya svāhā iti
3.4.5.4	athāsthy ādāya nadītīreṣu vā samudratīreṣu vāpāhareyuḥ
3.4.5.5	api vā gajasammitaṃ puruṣasammitaṃ vā gartaṃ khātvāsthikumbham avadhāya punar abhyajya purīṣeṇa pūrayet yāvad eva tad bhavati tāvat svarge loke mahīyate iti
3.5.1.1	atha yady āhitāgnir nirmāraṃ gacchati upatapatā vā jarayā vā agniṣṭha evāsya yajamānāyatane śayanaṃ kalpayeyur jaghanena vā gārhapatyam
3.5.1.2	tad asmai bhakṣān āharanti yāvad alaṃ bhakṣāya manyate
3.5.1.3	sa yady u hāgado bhavati punar eti
3.5.1.4	yady u vai praiti na payaḥ samāsiñcati
3.5.1.5	athedam agnihotraṃ sāyam upakramaṃ prātar apavargam ācāryā bruvate
3.5.1.6	tatrodāharanti
3.5.1.7	sa yadi sāyaṃ hute 'gnihotre preyāt pratikṛṣya prātar agnihotraṃ juhuyāt
3.5.1.8	atha yadi prātar agnihotre hute kuśalam
3.5.1.9	athemau darśapūrṇamāsau paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāsaṃsthāv ācāryā bruvate
3.5.1.10	tatrodāharanti
3.5.1.11	sa yadi paurṇamāsyāṃ vṛttāyāṃ preyāt pratikṛṣyāmāvāsyāṃ yajeteti
3.5.1.12	atha yady amāvāsyāyāṃ vṛttāyāṃ kuśalam
3.5.1.13	atha yasyobhe parvaṇī atipanne syātām atipannaprāyaścittaṃ kurvīta
3.5.1.14	atha yady ārtasyāgnihotraṃ vicchidyeta yady asya putro vāntevāsī vālaṃ karmaṇyaḥ syāt so 'raṇyor agniṃ samāropyodavasāya mathitvāgnīn vihṛtyāgnaye tantumate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati
3.5.1.15	śarāvaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
3.5.1.16	sā prasiddheṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
3.5.1.17	divi prakrānte preyāt tūṣṇīm etat tantram saṃsthāpyāpo bhakṣān abhyavahareyuḥ
3.5.1.18	apo bhakṣān abhyavaharanti iti vijñāyate
3.5.1.19	athainam ādāyāntareṇa vedyutkarāv udaṅmukham upanirhṛtyāthainaṃ pariśrayanti
3.5.1.20	tasya dakṣiṇā dvāraṃ kurvanti
3.5.1.21	athāsya keśaśmaśrūṇi vāpayitvā lomāni saṃhṛtya nakhāni nikṛntayīta
3.5.1.22	athāsya dakṣiṇaṃ kukṣim upākṛṣya niṣpurīṣaṃ kṛtvādbhiḥ prakṣālya sarpiṣāntrāṇi pūrayitvā darbhaiḥ saṃsīvyati
3.5.1.23	tad u tathā na kuryāt kṣodhukā asya prajā bhavanti iti vijñāyate
3.5.1.24	api vā sapurīṣam evāplāvyācchādyālaṅkṛtyāthainam ādāyāntareṇa vedyutkarau prapādya jaghanena gārhapatyam upasādayanty atra havir nirupyata iti
3.5.1.25	athainam ādāyāntarvedi prākcchirasam āsādayanty atra havir āsādyata iti
3.5.1.26	atha gārhapatya ājyaṃ vilāpyotpūya sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā prāg udetya samidvaty āhavanīye 'thāsya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anvārabhya juhoti
3.5.2.1	pareyuvāṃsaṃ pravato mahīr anu bahubhyaḥ panthām anapaspaśānam / vaivasvataṃ saṃgamanaṃ janānāṃ yamaṃ rājānaṃ haviṣā duvasyata svāhā iti
3.5.2.2	etenaiva gārhapatye juhoti
3.5.2.3	tūṣṇīm anvāhāryapacane hutvāthainam ādāyāntareṇa vedyutkarau prapādya jaghanena gārhapatyam āsandyāṃ kṛṣṇājine dakṣiṇāśirasaṃ saṃveśya śirasto naladamālāṃ pratimucya pattodaśenāhatena vāsasā prorṇoti idaṃ tvā vastraṃ prathamaṃ nv āgan iti athaitad apohati apaitad ūha yad ihābibhaḥ purā / iṣṭāpūrtam anusaṃpaśya dakṣiṇāṃ yathā te dattaṃ bahudhā vibandhuṣu iti
3.5.2.4	tad asya putro vāntevāsī vā patnī vā paridadhīta
3.5.2.5	tad u hājarasam eva vasītāhaśśeṣaṃ vā
3.5.2.6	atha trīñchakalān upakalpayate
3.5.2.7	atha yadi na śakalā bhavanti antarvedi parāg avahatānāṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ vrīhīṇām anvāhāryapacane trīn carūn śrapayaty ekaṃ vā
3.5.2.8	gārhapatya āmikṣāṃ śrapayati
3.5.2.9	athainān saṃbhārān upakalpayate dadhi ca sarpirmiśram ājyaṃ codakumbhaṃ ca darbhāś ca paristaraṇīyān hiraṇyaṃ cājaṃ ca śāsaṃ ceḍasūnaṃ ca kumbhīṃ ca pracyāvanīṃ sikatāś ca śulbe ca tisraḥ parṇaśākhāś ca
3.5.2.10	katham u khalv enaṃ daheyuḥ iti
3.5.2.11	yo bahuyājī syāt taṃ pūrvāgninā daheyur ity etad ekam
3.5.2.12	ajasrair enaṃ daheyur ity etad ekam
3.5.2.13	nirmanthyair enaṃ daheyur ity etad ekam
3.5.2.14	api vā tisra ulaparājīr ādīpya yatrāgnayaḥ saṃgaccheran tatrolmukam ādāya tenainaṃ daheyur ity etad ekam aparam
3.5.3.1	athāto 'nustaraṇīkalpaḥ
3.5.3.2	ānayanty etāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ kūṭāṃ jaratīṃ mūrkhāṃ tajjaghanyām anustaraṇīṃ pratibaddhām
3.5.3.3	savyapratibaddhā bhavati iti vijñāyate
3.5.3.4	etasmin kāle 'syāmātyāḥ prakīrṇakeśās tisṛbhir aṅgulībhiḥ upahatya pāṃsūn aṃseṣv āvapante khalv aghaṃ nāsya khalvo evāgham iti
3.5.3.5	athāsya bhāryāḥ kaniṣṭhaprathamāḥ prakīrṇakeśyo vrajeyuḥ pāṃsūn aṃseṣv āvapamānāḥ khalv aghaṃ nāsya khalvo evāgham iti
