3.5.3.10	anaś ced yuñjyād imau yunajmi te vahnī asunīthāya voḍhave / yābhyāṃ yamasya sādanaṃ saukṛtāṃ cāpi gacchatāt iti samāropyāgnīn haranti
3.5.3.11	samāropya vāntareṇa vā kṛtvāgnīn haranti
3.5.4.1	athainam ādadate
3.5.4.2	ādīyamānam anumantrayate pūṣā tvetaś cyāvayatu pravidvān anaṣṭapaśur bhuvanasya gopāḥ / sa tvaitebhyaḥ paridadāt pitṛbhyo 'gnir devebhyaḥ suvidatrebhyaḥ iti
3.5.4.3	tṛtīyam etasyādhvano gatvā nidadhati
3.5.4.4	athaiteṣāṃ śakalānām ekam aśastreṇa plakṣṇoti
3.5.4.5	atha yadi na śakalā bhavanti caruṃ mekṣaṇena prayauti
3.5.4.6	athavā eka eva sa bhavati caros tṛtīyaṃ mekṣaṇena prayauti
3.5.4.7	loṣṭān upasaṃhṛtya teṣūpamṛjya kaniṣṭhaprathamāḥ prakīrṇakeśās trir apasalaiḥ pariyanti sigbhir upavātayantaḥ
3.5.4.8	evam amātyā evaṃ striyaḥ saṃyamya keśān yathetaṃ triḥ punaḥ pariyanti
3.5.4.9	athainam ādadate
3.5.4.10	ādīyamānam anumantrayate pūṣemā āśā anuveda sarvāḥ so asmāṁ abhayatamena neṣat / svastidā aghṛṇiḥ sarvavīro 'prayucchan pura etu pravidvān iti
3.5.4.11	ardham etasyādhvano gatvā nidadhati
3.5.4.12	athaiteṣāṃ śakalānām ekam aśastreṇa plakṣṇoti
3.5.4.13	atha yadi na śakalā bhavanti caruṃ mekṣaṇena prayauti
3.5.4.14	loṣṭān upasaṃhṛtya teṣūpamṛjya kaniṣṭhaprathamāḥ prakīrṇakeśās trir apasalaiḥ pariyanti sigbhir upavātayantaḥ
3.5.4.15	evam amātyā evaṃ striyaḥ saṃyamya keśān yathetaṃ triḥ punaḥ pariyanti
3.5.4.16	athainam ādadate
3.5.4.17	ādīyamānam anumantrayate āyur viśvāyuḥ paripāsati tvā pūṣā tvā pātu prapathe purastāt / yatrāsate sukṛto yatra te yayus tatra tvā devaḥ savitā dadhātu iti
3.5.4.18	samastam etasyādhvano gatvā nidadhati
3.5.4.19	athaiteṣāṃ śakalānām ekam aśastreṇa plakṣṇoti
3.5.4.20	atha yadi śakalā na bhavanti caruṃ mekṣaṇena prayauti
3.5.4.21	yady u vā eka eva bhavati caror avaśiṣṭaṃ mekṣaṇena prayauti
3.5.4.22	loṣṭān upasaṃhṛtya teṣūpamṛjya kaniṣṭhaprathamāḥ prakīrṇakeśāḥ trir apasalaiḥ pariyanti sigbhir upavātayantaḥ
3.5.4.23	evam amātyā evaṃ striyaḥ saṃyamya keśān yathetaṃ triḥ punaḥ pariyanti
3.5.4.24	athaitāṃ carusthālīṃ subhinnāṃ bhinatti yathāsyai kapāleṣūdakaṃ na tiṣṭhed iti
3.5.4.25	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
3.5.5.1	athāsyāvakāśaṃ joṣayate
3.5.5.2	paścād udakam anūṣaram anupahatam asrutahāryam aniriṇam abhaṅguram avalmīkam ajāgarti bahulauṣadhi yatra kṣīriṇo vṛkṣā oṣadhayo vyatiṣaktāḥ syuḥ yasmād dakṣiṇāpratīcya āpaḥ śanaiḥ pratiṣṭheran tāḥ pradakṣiṇam abhiparyāvṛtya mahānadīm abhyupetya prācyaḥ saṃpadyeran
3.5.5.3	dakṣiṇāpratyakpravaṇam ity ekeṣām
3.5.5.4	api vā yā samā subhūmiḥ
3.5.5.5	tasmād vīrudha uddhārayanti
3.5.5.6	kālāṃ ca pṛśnīparṇīṃ ca tilvakāṃ cāpāghāṃ cāpāmārgaṃ ca śuṇṭhīṃ ca bahuputrīṃ ca visraṃsinīkāṃ ca rājakṣapaṇīṃ ca yāś cānyā kṣīriṇya oṣadhayo bhavanti
3.5.5.7	athainam uddhatyāvokṣya hiraṇyena parikrīya parṇaśākhayāpohati apeta vīta vi ca sarpatāta iti
3.5.5.8	dārucitāṃ kurvanti dakṣiṇāprācīm eṣā hi pitṝṇāṃ prācī dig iti vijñāyate
3.5.5.9	jaghanena citāṃ dakṣiṇāprācīṃ vihāraṃ kalpayitvā darbhair agniṃ pretaṃ citāṃ ca paristīrya dakṣiṇena vihāraṃ dakṣiṇāgnān darbhān saṃstīrya teṣv ekaikaśo nyañci pātrāṇi sādayati
3.5.5.10	ekapavitreṇa prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya pātrāṇi prokṣya pretaṃ citāṃ cājyaṃ nirupyādhiśritya paryagnikṛtvodvāsyotpūya tūṣṇīṃ darbhaiḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛjya tūṣṇīṃ tūṣṇīṃ dārśapūrṇamāsikājyāni gṛhītvā
3.5.6.1	athāsya rājagavīm upākaroti bhuvanasya pate iti
3.5.6.2	tasyāṃ nipadyamānāyāṃ savyāni jānūny upanighnate puruṣasya sayāvaryapedaghāni mṛjmahe / yathā no atra nāparaḥ purā jarasa āyati iti
3.5.6.3	tām atraiva śastrād ghnanti
3.5.6.4	athaitasyai prāṇān visrasyamānān anumantrayate puruṣasya sayāvari vi te prāṇam asisrasam / śarīreṇa mahīmihi svadha ehi pitṝn upa prajayāsmān ihāvaha iti
3.5.6.5	upotthāya pāṃsūnamavamṛśante maivaṃ māṃstā priye 'haṃ devī satī pitṛlokaṃ yadaiṣi / viśvavārā nabhasā saṃ vyayanty ubhau no lokau payasābhyāvavṛtsva iti
3.5.6.6	athainaṃ saṃśāsti aṅgād aṅgād anasthikāni piśitāni pracchidyāsaṃśrāvayanto 'pracyāvayanta ekolmukena śrapayantaḥ prajñātāṃ vapāṃ nidhatta prajñātaṃ hṛdayaṃ prajñātāṃ jihvāṃ prajñātaṃ carma saśīrṣavālapādaṃ prajñāte ca matasre prajñātaṃ meda iti
3.5.6.7	athāsya bhāryām upasaṃveśayati iyaṃ nārī patilokaṃ vṛṇānā nipadyata upa tvā martyapretam / viśvaṃ purāṇam anu pālayantī tasyai prajāṃ draviṇaṃ ceha dhehi iti
3.5.6.8	tāṃ patihitaḥ savye pāṇau gṛhītvotthāpayati udīrṣva nāry abhi jīvalokam itāsum etam upaśeṣa ehi / hastagrābhasya didhiṣos tvam etat patyur janitvam abhi saṃbabhūva iti
3.5.6.9	athāsya svarṇena hastau nimṛjate svarṇe hastād ādadānā mṛtasya śriyai brahmaṇe tejase balāya / atraiva tvam iha vayaṃ suśevā viśvā spṛdho abhimātīr jayema iti brāhmaṇasya dhanur hastād ādadānā mṛtasya śriyai kṣatrāyaujase balāya / atraiva tvam iha vayaṃ suśevā viśvā spṛdho abhimātīr jayema iti rājanyasya maṇiṃ hastād ādadānā mṛtasya śriyai viśe puṣṭyai balāya / atraiva tvam iha vayaṃ suśevā viśvā spṛdho abhimātīr jayema iti vaiśyasya
3.5.6.10	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
3.5.6.11	athainam etayāsandyā saha citāv ādadhāti
3.5.6.12	apakṛṣya rajjūr āsandīm apavidhyanti
3.5.6.13	kṛṣṇājine caiva rajjuṣu cottānaḥ śete
3.5.6.14	tasya prāṇeṣu hiraṇyaśakalān pratyasyati
3.5.6.15	nānā caturgṛhītābhyām akṣṇor juhoti citraṃ devānām udagād anīkam ity ardharcābhyāṃ juhotīti vijñāyate
3.5.7.1	katham u khalv asya pātrāṇi yuñjyād iti
3.5.7.2	dadhnā sarpirmiśreṇa pūrayitvā mukhe 'gnihotrahavaṇīṃ nāsikayoḥ sruvau akṣṇoḥ hiraṇyaśakalau ājyasruvau vā karṇayoḥ prāśitraharaṇaṃ bhittvaikaikaṃ hanvor ulūkhalamusale śirasi kapālāni lalāṭe ekakapālaṃ śirastaḥ praṇītāpraṇayanaṃ camasaṃ nidadhāti imam agne camasaṃ mā vijīhvaraḥ priyo devānām uta saumyānām / eṣa yaś camaso devapānas tasmin devā amṛtā mādayantām iti
3.5.7.3	dakṣiṇe haste juhūṃ savye upabhṛtam urasi dhruvām upaveṣam araṇīṃ ca dakṣiṇe aṃse mekṣaṇaṃ savye piṣṭodvapanīṃ pṛṣṭhe sphyam udare dārupātrīṃ kukṣau camasau sāṃnāyyapidhānaṃ ceḍopavahanaṃ ca vaṅkṣṇayoḥ sāṃnāyyakumbhyau pādayor agnihotrasthālīm anvāhāryasthālīṃ corvorulūkhalamusale aṇḍayor dṛṣadupale śiśne vṛṣāravaṃ śamyāṃ ca pārśvayoḥ śūrpaṃ chittvaikaikaṃ śirasta upasādanīyaṃ kūrcaṃ nidadhāti
3.5.7.4	patta upāvaharaṇīyaṃ kūrcam
3.5.7.5	athāvaśiṣṭāny antareṇa sakthinī nivapeyuḥ
3.5.7.6	apo mṛṇmayāny abhyavahareyuḥ
3.5.7.7	apo mṛṇmayāny abhyavaharanti iti vijñāyate
3.5.7.8	atraivopanidadhyuḥ
3.5.7.9	brāhmaṇebhyo 'yasmayāni lohamayāni ca dadyuḥ
3.5.7.10	teṣāṃ yāny āsecanavanti tāni dadhnā sarpirmiśreṇa pūrayet
3.5.7.11	saṃspṛśed itarāṇi
3.5.7.12	ariktāni bhavanti iti vijñāyate
3.5.7.13	atraivādhyasyanty upavājinaṃ khārīṃ nalvam
3.5.7.14	athāsyāmikṣām uddhṛtya pāṇyor ādadhyāt mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ tvā iti
3.5.7.15	athāsya matasnām ullikhya pāṇyor ādadhyāt śyāmaśabalābhyāṃ tvā iti
3.5.7.16	dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇaṃ savye savyaṃ hṛdaye hṛdayam āsye jihvāṃ yathāṅgam aṅgair itarāṇi saṃpracchādya vapayāsya mukhaṃ pracchādayati
3.5.7.17	medasā srucau prorṇoti iti vijñāyate
3.5.7.18	athainaṃ carmaṇā saśīrṣavālapādenottaralomnā prarṇoti agner varma pari gobhir vyayasva saṃprorṇuṣva medasā pīvasā ca / netvā dhṛṣṇur harasā jarhṛṣāṇo dadhad vidhakṣyan paryaṅkhayātai iti
3.5.8.1	atha yady anustaraṇīṃ nānustariṣyanto bhavanty utsṛjed vainām
3.5.8.2	brāhmaṇebhyo vā dadyāt
3.5.8.3	dattvātraiva śreyase bhavanti iti vijñāyate
3.5.8.4	atha yady utsrakṣyan bhavati tām apasalaiḥ paryāṇayati apaśyāma yuvatim ācarantīm iti tisṛbhistriḥ paryāṇīyottarataḥ pratiṣṭhitām anumantrayate ye jīvā ye ca mṛtā ity etayā
3.5.8.5	athāsyāḥ karṇalomāny utpāṭya pāṇyor evādadhyāt śyāmaśavalābhyāṃ tvā iti
3.5.8.6	dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇaṃ savye savyam
3.5.8.7	athainām utsṛjati mātā rudrāṇāṃ duhitā vasūnāṃ svasādityānām amṛtasya nābhiḥ / pra ṇu vocaṃ cikituṣe janāya māgāmanāgām aditiṃ vadhiṣṭa / pibatūdakaṃ tṛṇāny attu / om utsṛjata iti
3.5.8.8	athainam upoṣayati purastād āhavanīyena dakṣiṇato' nvāhāryapacanena paścād gārhapatyenottarataḥ sabhyāvasakthyābhyām
3.5.8.9	atrāpyutprekṣā bhavanti
3.5.8.10	taṃ yady āhavanīyaḥ prathamam abhyujjvaled devalokam abhyajaiṣīd ity enaṃ jānīyāt
3.5.8.11	atha yady anvāhāryapacanaḥ pitṛlokam
3.5.8.12	atha yadi gārhapatyaḥ svargalokam
3.5.8.13	atha yadi sabhyāvasakthau saptarṣīṇāṃ lokam
3.5.8.14	atha yadi sarva eva sahābhyujjvaled brahmalokam abhyajaiṣīd ity enaṃ jānīyāt
3.5.8.15	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
3.6.1.1	athainam ādīpayate
3.6.1.2	ādīpyamānam anumantrayate mainam agne vidaho mābhiśoco māsya tvacaṃ cikṣipo mā śarīram / yadā śṛtaṃ karavo jātavedo 'them enaṃ prahiṇutāt pitṛbhyaḥ iti
3.6.1.3	prajvalitam anumantrayate śṛtaṃ yadā karasi jātavedo 'them enaṃ paridattāt pitṛbhyaḥ / yadā gacchāty asunītim etām athā devānāṃ vaśanīr bhavāti iti
3.6.1.4	atra ṣaḍḍhotāraṃ vyācaṣṭe sūryaṃ te cakṣur gacchatu vātam ātmā dyāṃ ca gaccha pṛthivīṃ ca dharmaṇā / apo vā gaccha yadi tatra te hitam oṣadhīṣu pratitiṣṭhā śarīraiḥ iti
3.6.1.5	atrainam ajaṃ cityante 'balena śulbena badhnāti ajo bhāgas tapasā taṃ tapasva taṃ te śocis tapatu taṃ te arciḥ / yās te śivās tanuvo jātavedas tābhir vahemaṃ sukṛtāṃ yatra lokāḥ iti
3.6.1.6	sa yady aho dravati nainam āvartayati
3.6.1.7	prāg u haika upoṣaṇāt
3.6.1.8	udakumbhena trir apasalaiḥ pariyanti vāruṇībhiḥ
3.6.1.9	tat pracchādyena parṇamayena sruveṇopaghātaṃ juhoti ya etasya patho goptāras tebhyaḥ svāhā iti nava sruvāhutīḥ
3.6.1.10	athānyāṃ juhoti ayaṃ vai tvam asmād adhi tvam etad ayaṃ vai tad asya yonir asi / vaiśvānaraḥ putraḥ pitre lokakṛj jātavedo vahemaṃ sukṛtāṃ yatra lokāḥ svāhā iti
3.6.1.11	atraiva sruvam anu praharati
3.6.1.12	atraitāny avadānānīḍasūne pracchādyaudumbaryā darvyopaghātaṃ juhoti agnaye rayimate svāhā iti
3.6.1.13	atraiva darvīm anupraharati jaghanena citām
3.6.1.14	athainaṃ navarcena yāmyena sūktenopatiṣṭhate praketunā bṛhatā bhāty agniḥ iti
3.6.1.15	āsīnaḥ parācānuśaṃsati
3.6.1.16	jaghanena dahanaṃ tisro dakṣiṇāḥ karṣūḥ kurvanti
3.6.1.17	athainā adbhir anuplāvya sikatābhir avakīrya saṃgāhante yavīyān yavīyān pūrvaḥ saṃgāhante
3.6.1.18	aśmanvatī revatīḥ saṃrabhadhvam uttiṣṭhata prataratā sakhāyaḥ / atrā jahāma ye asannaśevāḥ śivān vayam abhi vājān uttarema iti
3.6.1.19	jaghanena karṣūḥ parṇaśākhe nihatyābalena śulbena baddhvā vinisarpanti yad vai devasya savituḥ pavitraṃ sahasradhāraṃ vitatam antarikṣe / yenāpunād indram anārtamārtyai tenāhaṃ māṃ sarvatanuṃ punāmi iti
3.6.1.20	jaghanyo vyudasyati yā rāṣṭrāt pannād apayanti śākhā abhimṛtā nṛpatim icchamānāḥ / dhātus tāḥ sarvāḥ pavanena pūtāḥ prajayāsmān rayyā varcasā saṃsṛjātha iti
3.6.1.21	yatrāpas tad yanty anavekṣamāṇāḥ
3.6.1.22	apaḥ sacelā dakṣiṇāmukhāḥ samṛttikāḥ plavante dhātā punātu savitā punātu iti
3.6.1.23	nāmagrāhaṃ trir udakam utsicyottīryācamyādityam upatiṣṭhate ud vayaṃ tamasas pari iti
3.6.1.24	atha gṛhān āyānti
3.6.1.25	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
3.6.2.1	etasmin kāle 'syāmātyāḥ prakīrṇakeśāḥ keśaśmaśrūṇi vāpayante ye sannidhāne bhavanti
3.6.2.2	vikalpa itareṣu
3.6.2.3	vāpayeran nivartayeran vā
3.6.2.4	śrutavatā tu vaptavyam evāsannidhāne 'pīti mataṃ bodhāyanasya kalpe
3.6.2.5	na samāvṛttā vaperann anyatra vihārād ity eke
3.6.2.6	mātari pitary ācārya iti trirātraṃ kṣāralavaṇavarjitabhojanam adhaḥśayanaṃ brahmacaryaṃ tryahaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ yāvadgrahaṇaṃ dvādaśāhāparārdham paramaguruṣv evam aghodakam itareṣu trirātram yāvajjīvaṃ pretapatnī
3.6.2.7	atha yady āhitāgnir anyatra preyād ādīpyamānair āhūyamānair vasīran yāvad asya śarīram agnibhiḥ samāgamayeran
3.6.2.8	athaitad abhivānyāyai payo dohayitvā gārhapatye 'bhiviṣyandayitvāhavanīye 'bhiviṣyandayet
3.6.2.9	adhastāt samidham āharanty upariṣṭāddhi devebhyo haranti iti vijñāyate
3.6.2.10	athainam ādāyāntareṇa vedyutkarāv udag upanirhṛtya prasiddham upoṣeyuḥ
3.6.2.11	atha yady āhitāgnir anyatra preyād udakānte trīn agnyagārān ālikhya sakṛt praviśya nimīlya nigṛhya skandakṣiṇāntān ādityam udīkṣet
3.6.2.12	parikurvīta ca
3.6.2.13	anenaiva trir videśasthe
3.6.2.14	atha yadi dagdhaḥ syād asthīny āhṛtyāntarvedi śarīrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇājine puruṣākṛtiṃ kṛtvā teṣūpari pātrāṇi citvā kuśataruṇakaiḥ praticchādya prasiddham upoṣeyuḥ
3.6.2.15	atha yady asthīni na vindeta trayāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭiśatānāṃ parṇatsarūṇām eva kṛṣṇājine puruṣākṛtiṃ kṛtvā teṣūpari pātrāṇi citvā kuśataruṇakaiḥ praticchādya prasiddham upoṣeyuḥ
3.6.2.16	āhitāgnim agnibhir dahanti yajñapātraiś ca iti vijñāyate
3.6.2.17	puruṣāhutir hy asya priyatamā ity etām anukhyātāṃ dahanasya bruvate
3.6.2.18	athāpy udāharanti śarīradāyādā ha vāgnayo bhavanti iti
3.6.2.19	tad api dāśataye vijñāyate śatam in nu śarado anti devā yatrā naś cakrā jarasaṃ tanūnām / putrāso yatra pitaro bhavanti mā no madhyā rīriṣatāyur gantoḥ iti
3.6.3.1	athātaḥ saṃcayanam
3.6.3.2	ekasyāṃ vyuṣṭāyāṃ tisṛṣu vā pañcasu vā saptasu vā navasv ekādaśasu vāyugmeṣv ahassu ardhamāseṣu māseṣu ṛtuṣu saṃvatsareṣu vā sampādya saṃcinuyur iti
3.6.3.3	sa upakalpayate sataṃ ca kṣīraṃ cājyaṃ ca udakumbhaṃ ca darbhāṃś ca paristaraṇīyān nīlalohite sūtre bṛhatīphalaṃ cāśmānaṃ cāpāmārgaṃ ca vaitasaśākhāṃ ca sikatāś ca śulbe ca tisraś ca parṇaśākhāś ca
3.6.3.4	ata eva dahanād aṅgārān nirvartya tisro avasarjanīyā juhoti avasṛja punar agne pitṛbhyaḥ saṃgacchasva pitṛbhiḥ yat te kṛṣṇaḥ śakuna ātutoda iti
3.6.3.5	etasmin sate kṣīraṃ codakumbhaṃ ca nikṣipya vaitasaśākhayāvokṣya sampādayaty aprakāthayan śarīrāṇi yaṃ te agnim amanthāma iti ṣaḍbhiḥ
3.6.3.6	prathamāṃ vottamāṃ dvir abhyāvartayeyuḥ
3.6.3.7	athaitad ādahanam udakumbhaiḥ svavokṣitam avokṣya yā asya strīṇāṃ mukhyā sā savye pāṇau bṛhatīphalaṃ nīlalohitābhyāṃ mūtrābhyāṃ viśrathyāśmānam anvāsthāyāpāmārgeṇa sakṛd upamṛjyānanvīkṣamāṇā pattaḥ śirasto vāsthīni gṛhṇāti uttiṣṭhātas tanuvaṃ saṃbharasva meha gātram avahā mā śarīram / yatra bhūmyai vṛṇase tatra gaccha tatra tvā devaḥ savitā dadhātu iti
3.6.3.8	idaṃ ta ekam iti dvitīyam
3.6.3.9	para ūta ekam iti tṛtīyam
3.6.3.10	tṛtīyena jyotiṣā saṃviśasva iti caturtham
3.6.3.11	saṃveśanas tanuvai cārur edhi iti pañcamam
3.6.3.12	priyo devānāṃ parame sadhasthe iti ṣaṣṭham
3.6.3.13	athainaṃ susaṃcitaṃ saṃcitya piṇḍīkaroti
3.6.3.14	taṃ tathā karoti yathāsya kapotaḥ chāyāyāṃ nopaviśed iti
3.6.3.15	athainam aparimitaiḥ kṣudramiśrair aśmabhiḥ paricinoti na tena paricinuyād yathāsya kapotaḥ chāyāyām upaviśet
3.6.3.16	athaitāny asthīny adbhiḥ prakṣālya kumbhe vā sate vā kṛtvopottiṣṭhati uttiṣṭha prehi pradravaukaḥ kṛṇuṣva parame vyoman / yamena tvaṃ yamyā saṃvidānottamaṃ nākam adhirohemam iti
3.6.3.17	saṃpraveśaṃ kumbhaṃ nidhāya athāto haviryajñiyaṃ nivapanam yaṃ kāmayetānantalokaḥ syāt iti
3.6.3.18	tam asyā uddhate sikatopopte pariśrite nidadhāti pṛthivyās tvā akṣityā apām oṣadhīnāṃ rase svarge loke nākasya tvā pṛṣṭhe bradhnasya tvā viṣṭape sādayāmy amum asau iti
3.6.3.19	anantaloko ha vai bhavati iti vijñāyate
3.6.3.20	jaghanena kumbhaṃ tisro dakṣiṇāḥ karṣūḥ kurvanti
3.6.3.21	tat purastād vyākhyātam
3.6.3.22	jaghanena karṣūḥ parṇaśākhe nihatyābalena śulbena baddhvā vinisarpanti
3.6.3.23	tat purastāt vyākhyātam
3.6.3.24	yatrāpas tad yanty anavekṣamāṇāḥ
3.6.3.25	apaḥ sacelā dakṣiṇāmukhāḥ samṛttikāḥ plavante dhātā punātu savitā punātu iti
3.6.3.26	nāmagrāhaṃ trir udakam utsicyottīryācamyāthādityam upatiṣṭhate ud vayaṃ tamasas pari iti
3.6.3.27	atha gṛhān āyānti
3.6.3.28	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
3.6.4.1	atha yadi punar dhakṣyanto bhavanti purastād evāvaśeṣayeyur juhūṃ cāraṇīṃ ca kṛṣṇājinaṃ dṛṣadupale śamyām iti
3.6.4.2	atha yady anuhṛtāḥ syur yasya kasyacid aśvatthasyāraṇī gṛhītvā mathitvāgnim upasamādhāya paristīrya kṛṣṇājine śamyāyāṃ dṛṣadupale yuktvāsthīny evāñjanaṃ piṣṭvā purāṇena sarpiṣā samudāyutya juhvā prasekaṃ juhoti asmāt tvam adhijāto 'sy ayaṃ tvad adhijāyatām / agnaye vaiśvānarāya svargāya lokāya svāhā iti
3.6.4.3	atraivānupraharati juhūṃ cāraṇīṃ ca kṛṣṇājinaṃ dṛṣadupale śamyām iti
3.6.4.4	atrāpy utprekṣā bhavanti
3.6.4.5	taṃ yadi jvālordhvam abhyujjvaled devalokam abhyajaiṣīd ity enaṃ jānīyād atha yadi muhūrtam udetya vā bhramed antarikṣam abhyajaiṣīd ity enaṃ jānīyād atha yadīmām anuvinamed ihaivety enaṃ jānīyāt
3.6.4.6	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
3.6.4.7	na cāsyāta ūrdhvaṃ śmaśānaṃ kartum ādriyeta
3.6.4.8	kṛtīrvāsya dahane vaped apasyābhir vā paricinuyāt
3.6.4.9	tam abhy evādityas tapati abhi vā vātaḥ pavate sa nādityasya sakāśān na vāyor nāpāṃ sparśāc chidyate
3.6.4.10	yam evaṃ nidadhyur ya u cainam evaṃ vidur evam u hāhīnā hāyanā vāśvatthaṃ nidadhyus taṃ ho evaṃ cakre tasyo heme 'hīnā hāyanā śreyasī śreyasī hy asmai vasyasī vasyasī prajā bhavati
3.6.4.11	yam evaṃ nidadhyur ya u cainam evaṃ vidur etāṃ ha kauṣītakir vidāṃcakāra
3.6.4.12	tasyo heme kauṣītakinaḥ śreyasī śreyasī hyasmai vyucchantī vyucchanty asmai vasyasī vasyasī prajā bhavati yam evaṃ nidadhyur ya u cainam evaṃ vidur ya u cainam evaṃ viduḥ
3.7.1.1	atha gṛhān eṣyann upakalpayate vāraṇaṃ srucaṃ ca sruvaṃ ca vāraṇān paridhīn kuśamayaṃ barhiḥ parṇamayam idhmaṃ rohitaṃ carmānaḍuhaṃ navaṃ ca sarpir āñjanaṃ cāśmānaṃ cānaḍvāhaṃ ca śamīśākhāṃ ca kuśataruṇakāni ca darbhastambhaṃ cājaṃ ca yavāṃś ca iti
3.7.1.2	athāntareṇa grāmaṃ ca śmaśānaṃ ca tadvṛdhāgnim upasamādhāya kṛśamayaṃ barhis tīrtvā vāraṇān paridhīn paridhāya parṇamayam idhmam abhyajya svāhākāreṇābhyādhāyāthaitad rohitaṃ carmānaḍuhaṃ jaghanenāgniṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti
3.7.1.3	tad ārohanti yāvanto 'sya jñātayo bhavanti ārohatāyur jarasaṃ gṛṇānā anupūrvaṃ yatamānāya tiṣṭa / iha tvaṣṭā sujanimā suratno dirgham āyuḥ karatu jīvase va iti
3.7.1.4	athainān anupūrvaṃ kalpayanti yathāhāny anupūrvaṃ bhavanti yathartava ṛtubhir yanti kḷptāḥ / yathā na pūrvam aparo jahāty evā dhātar āyūṃṣi kalpayaiṣām iti
3.7.1.5	atha vāraṇena sruveṇa vāraṇyāṃ sruci catur gṛhītvā juhoti na hi te agne tanuvai krūraṃ cakāra martyaḥ / kapir babhasti te janaṃ punar jarāyu gaur iva / apa naḥ śośucad agham agne śuśudhyā rayim / apa naḥ śośucad aghaṃ mṛtyave svāhā iti
3.7.1.6	atha vāraṇena sruveṇopaghātaṃ juhoti apa naḥ śośucad agham iti dvādaśa sruvāhutīḥ
3.7.1.7	athopotthāya anuḍvāham anvārabhante anaḍvāham anvārabhāmahe svastaye / sa na indra iva devebhyo vahniḥ saṃpāraṇo bhava iti
3.7.1.8	prāñco yānti ime jīvā vimṛtair āvavartinn abhūd bhadrā devahūtiṃ no adya / prāñco gām ānṛtaye hasāya drāghīya āyuḥ pratarāṃ dadhānāḥ / mṛtyoḥ padaṃ yopayanto yadaima drāghīya āyuḥ pratarāṃ dadhānāḥ / āpyāyamānāḥ prajayā dhanena śuddhāḥ pūtā bhavatha yajñiyāsaḥ iti
3.7.2.1	athāntarenāgniṃ ca grāmaṃ cāśmānam avadadhāti imaṃ jīvebhyaḥ paridhiṃ dadhāmi mā no 'nugād aparo ardham etam / śataṃ jīvantu śaradaḥ purūcīs tiro mṛtyuṃ dadmahe parvatena iti
3.7.2.2	athaitāḥ patnayo navena sarpiṣā saṃmṛśante imā nārīr avidhavāḥ supatnīr āñjanena sarpiṣā saṃmṛśantām iti
3.7.2.3	kuśataruṇakaiḥ traikakudenāñjanenāṅkte yad āñjanaṃ traikakudaṃ jātaṃ himavatas pari / tenāmṛtasya mūlenārātīr jambhayāmasi iti
3.7.2.4	athaitāni kuśataruṇakāni samuccitya darbhastambe nidadhāti
3.7.2.5	yathā tvam udbhinatsy oṣadhe pṛthivyā adhi / evam ima udbhindantu kīrttyā yaśasā brahmavarcasena iti
3.7.2.6	pratyetya gṛhān āsandīṃ preṣṭhanīty ārohanti anaśravo anamīvāḥ suśevā ārohantu janayo yonim agre iti
3.7.2.7	ajaṃ caitad ahaḥ pacante
3.7.2.8	yavaudanaṃ ca
3.7.2.9	ajaṃ cāśnāti
3.7.2.10	ajo 'syajāsmad aghād dveṣāṃsi iti
3.7.2.11	yavaudanasya prāśnāti
3.7.2.12	yavo 'si yavayāsmad aghād dveṣāṃsi iti
3.7.2.13	athāsya śrāddhaṃ kurvanti
3.7.2.14	ekasyāṃ vā vyuṣṭāyāṃ tisṛṣu vā pañcasu vā saptasu vā navasu vaikādaśasu vāyugmeṣv ahassu ardhamāseṣu vā dadyāt
3.7.2.15	kāmam aharahar ekādaśamāsān dadyāt
3.7.2.16	na dvādaśamāsam abhyārohayet
3.7.2.17	saṃvatsare saṃvatsare vā etasminn ahani dadyāt
3.7.2.18	sa eṣa evaṃ vihitaḥ
3.7.2.19	evam anāhitāgneḥ striyāḥ pulliṅgāḥ pātracayeṣṭakāḥ keśavapanavarjaṃ pitur mātur ācāryasya vā kriyeta
3.7.2.20	sahasradakṣiṇo vāpy anyatra
3.7.2.21	saṃtiṣṭhate pitṛmedhaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate pitṛmedhaḥ
3.7.3.1	yatho etadāhitāgner nirmāraṃ gacchataḥ pratikṛṣya prātar agnihotraṃ juhuyāt pratikṛṣyāmāvāsyāṃ yajeteti
3.7.3.2	tayaite karmaṇī abhisaṃcared yathā vā jīvataḥ kṛte syātām
3.7.3.3	so ced ahute prātaragnihotre 'vyuṣṭāyām amāvāsyāyāṃ preyāt tadānīm evāsya tūṣṇīṃ prātaragnihotraṃ yādṛk kīdṛk ca hotavyaṃ tadānīm evāsya tūṣṇīm amāvāsyāyāṃ yādṛśīṃ kīdṛśīṃ vā yajeta
3.7.3.4	so cet punar agadaḥ syāt punar evāsya prātaragnihotraṃ kālyam avyāpannaṃ hotavyam
3.7.3.5	punar evāsyām amāvāsyāyāṃ kālyām avyāpannāṃ yajeteti
3.7.3.6	yatho etan na payaḥ samāsiñcaty āmikṣārthaṃ payo 'vaśeṣayed ity evedam uktaṃ bhavati
3.7.3.7	yatho etad āsandyām ity evedam uktaṃ bhavati
3.7.3.8	yatho etad antarvedi śarīrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇājine puruṣākṛtiṃ kṛtvā teṣūpari pātrāṇi citvā kuśataruṇakaiḥ praticchādya prasiddham upoṣeyur iti vijñāyate
3.7.3.9	pātracayanaprabhṛti siddham ata ūrdhvam
3.7.3.10	etāvad eva nānā nātra gor ālambho 'nustaraṇīkāle kuśataruṇakaiḥ śuṣkagomayair ghṛtenety anustṛṇīyād agner varma pari gobhir vyayasva ity etad eva parṇatsaruṣu
3.7.3.11	api vā yatheṣṭikalpe
3.7.3.12	api vā tūṣṇīm eva sarvaṃ kriyetānyatra caiva gor ālambhād iti
3.7.3.13	atha vai bhavati
3.7.3.14	prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā vṛtto 'śayat
3.7.3.15	taṃ devā brāhmaṇaṃ rasaṃ tejas sambhṛtya tenainam abhiṣajyann iti
3.7.3.16	caturhotāram ity evaṃ brūyāt
3.7.3.17	tasya sagrahaiḥ hotṛbhir homaḥ bhartuḥ sūktena bharaṇaṃ patnībhir upasaṃveśanaṃ dakṣiṇāpratigrahair nirmārgo hṛdayair hiraṇyaśakalān sambhāraiś ca pātracayo jyotiṣmatībhir upoṣaṇaṃ nārāyaṇābhyāṃ brāhmaṇa ekahotā iti copasthānaṃ prayāsāya svāhā ity ājyāhutīḥ cittaṃ santānena iti piśitahomo mṛtyusūktenānuśaṃsanaṃ saumyayā saṃgāhanam īyuṣṭyāvagāhanaṃ sauryeṇādityasyopasthānam iti
3.7.3.18	tān etān paraṃ brahmety ācakṣate
3.7.3.19	tān na sādhāraṇe śmaśāne prayuñjīta nānācāryāya nāśrotriyāya nāgurave
3.7.3.20	patho etaddhavir yajñiyaṃ nivapanaṃ punardahanaṃ ceti yad ahaḥ saṃcinuyāt tad ahar evaitat kuryāt
3.7.3.21	kumbhāntam anāhitāgneś ca striyāś ca
3.7.3.22	nivapanāntaṃ haviryajñayājinaḥ punardahanāntaṃ somayājinaḥ cityantam agnicitaḥ
3.7.3.23	yadītaraṃ yadītaram aghodakam utsicya daśarātram āśaucaṃ kṛtvā śāntiḥ
3.7.3.24	atha yadi citiś cityante śaucam
3.7.3.25	cityāḥ prāk karṣūbhyaḥ kṛtvā śvobhūte dhuvanenaiva pratipadyate
3.7.3.26	siddham ata ūrdhvam
3.7.4.1	athaiteṣām udakasapiṇḍānāṃ bāndhavānāṃ mātuś ca yonisambandhebhyaḥ pituś ca saptamāt puruṣād ācāryāntevāsinoś ca sapatnīkānāṃ sāpatyānāṃ sapiṇḍānāṃ daśarātram
3.7.4.2	trirātram itareṣām
3.7.4.3	bāle deśāntarasthe ca sadyaḥ śaucam ity eke
3.7.4.4	evaṃ nityodakatarpaṇe 'nusmaraṇaṃ strīyājyaśiṣyāṇām
3.7.4.5	na prāk cauḍāt pramītānāṃ dahanaṃ vidyate
3.7.4.6	nāpaśuyājināṃ gor ālambhaḥ nāsannayatām āmikṣā nāgnicitāṃ citiḥ
3.7.4.7	na strīṇāṃ keśavapanaṃ vidyate na citir neṣṭakā na punardāhaḥ
3.7.4.8	dāruvat strīṇāṃ pātrāṇi bhavanti
3.7.4.9	bahvṛcāṃ pitṛmedhe strīṇām imān mantrān apoddharet
3.7.4.10	iyaṃ nārī patilokam udīrṣva nāry abhi jīvalokaṃ svarṇaṃ hastād ādadānā mṛtasya dhanur hastād ādadānā mṛtasya maṇiṃ hastād ādadānā mṛtasya mainam agne vidaho mābhiśocaḥ mṛtaṃ yadā karasi jātavedaḥ ajo bhāgas tapasā taṃ tapasva ayaṃ vai tvam asmād adhi tvam etat idaṃ ta ekaṃ para ūta ekaṃ yau te śvānau yat te kṛṣṇaḥ śakuna ātutoda uttiṣṭha prehi pradravaukaḥ kṛṇuṣva asmāt tvam adhijāto 'si apeta vīta vi ca sarpatātaḥ ucchmañcasva pṛthivi mā vibādhiyā iti
3.7.4.11	mṛtapatnīkaḥ kratūn āhariṣyan jāyām upayamyāgnīn ādadhyāt
3.7.4.12	vijñāyate ca tasmād eko dve jāye vindata iti
3.7.4.13	mṛtapatikāyā aupāsanena pitṛmedhaḥ
3.7.4.14	nahy asyā apatitvāt punaragnyādheyaṃ vidyate
3.7.4.15	vijñāyate ca tasmān naikā dvau patī vindate iti
3.7.4.16	āhitāgnim agnibhir dahanti yajñapātraiś cety aviśeṣād jāyāpatyor āhitāgnyor ity evedam uktaṃ bhavati
3.7.4.17	tayor yaḥ pūrvo mriyeta tasyāgnitretayā yajñapātraiś ca pitṛmedhaḥ yaḥ paścāt tasyaupāsanena
3.7.4.18	sahapramītayoḥ sahaikaḥ pitṛmedhaḥ
3.7.4.19	aupāsanaṃ colmukārthaṃ syāt
3.7.4.20	aupāsanenānāhitāgneḥ striyāś ca nirmanthyena
3.7.4.21	uttapanīyenaike samāmananti
3.7.4.22	nirmanthyena strīkumāraṃ daheyur ity ekeṣām
3.7.4.23	mṛtapatnīkasamāgnibhir jāyāyāṃ dagdhāyām aupāsanena kā pratipattir iti
3.7.4.24	kratuṃ cedāhariṣyan syād brāhmodanikam enaṃ kuryāt
3.7.4.25	vanaṃ ced ātiṣṭhed aupāsanam evopāsyaṃ syāt
3.7.4.26	atha cet saṃnyasen nainam ādriyeta
3.7.4.27	nāśuciḥ kāmyaṃ tapa ātiṣṭhen na yajen na svādhyāyam adhīyītānyatrāgnihotradarśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ dadyāt
3.7.4.28	kāmam ṛtvigbhyo dadyāt
3.7.4.29	yatho etad gṛhān eṣyann upakalpayate iti svān gṛhasthadharmān pratipatsyann ity evedam uktaṃ bhavati
3.7.4.30	katham u khalu prācīnāvītinā pitṛmedhaḥ kāryo yajñopavītineti
3.7.4.31	prācīnāvītinety evaṃ brūyāt
3.7.4.32	pitṝṇāṃ vā eṣa medho devānāṃ vā anye medhā iti
3.7.4.33	nivītinaś caivedam hareyuś citāyāṃ cādadhyuś citāyāṃ cādadhyuḥ
3.8.1.1	ekāhaṃ dhunuyus trīṇy ahāni dhunuyuḥ pañcasaptanavaikādaśārdhamāsān dhunuyuḥ ayugmarātrīr ardhamāsān māsān ṛtūn saṃvatsaraṃ vā saṃpādya dhunuyur iti
3.8.1.2	sa upakalpayate dadhi ca vājinamiśraṃ kumbhīṃ ca śatātṛṇṇāṃ tisraḥ pālāśyo medhyo rohitaṃ carmānaḍuham āhananārtham apasalāvṛttarajjuṃ parivyayaṇīṃ ca ṣaṭcchatānīṣṭakā āmamayā aparimitāś ca lokaṃpṛṇā dvayā dhānās tilamiśrāś cātilabhiśrāś cābhivānyāyai dugdham ardhapātraṃ samūlaṃ barhir naleṣikāṃ bhuktabhogaṃ ca vāsaḥ kṣetravitṛṇṇīṃ caturo loṣṭān pañca carūn pañcāpūpān ghṛtenaikaḥ kṣīreṇaiko dadhnaiko madhunaikaḥ caturaḥ stambān arjunastambaṃ dūrvāstambaṃ kāśastambaṃ kuśastambaṃ caturo nānāvṛkṣyān paridhīn parṇamayavāraṇavetasaśamīmayān dve dve vāraṇaśākhāṃ ca kṣetravitṛṇṇīṃ vidhṛtiṃ yavamayaṃ sarvauṣadhaṃ ca sikatāś ca śulbaṃ ca tisraś ca palāśaśākhāḥ
3.8.1.3	athāntareṇa vā grāmaṃ ca śmaśānaṃ cāgāraṃ vā vimitaṃ vā kāritaṃ vā bhavati
3.8.1.4	tad vṛdhāgnim upasamādhāyāpareṇāgniṃ tisraḥ pālāśyo medhyo nihatya tāsām antareṇāsthikumbhaṃ nidhāya tadupariṣṭācchatātṛṇṇām adhyudyamya dadhnā vājinamiśreṇa pūrayati vaiśvānare havir idaṃ juhomi imaṃ samudraṃ śatadhāram utsam iti dvābhyām
3.8.1.5	anumantrayate drapsaś caskanda iti
3.8.1.6	athaitat purastād rohitena carmaṇānaḍuhenābhighātaṃ trir apasalaiḥ pariyanti
3.8.1.7	ajinamau ajinamau iti
3.8.1.8	tris trir eva rātreḥ pariyanti trir ahnaḥ
3.8.1.9	evam amātyā evaṃ striyaḥ
3.8.1.10	tad anu nartakyaś cānunṛtyeyuḥ
3.8.1.11	yaś cāhanyate khāryāṃ vā palvale vā samavaśamayante
3.8.1.12	yad eṣāṃ samavaśamayitaṃ sambhavati te na tathā prayayur yad ahar na purastān na paścāc candramasaṃ paśyeyuḥ
3.8.1.13	te mahārātra utthāya prayayur jñātvā śmaśānakaraṇam
3.8.1.14	athaite brāhmaṇāś catvāro 'bhrim ādāyottarato gatvā loṣṭān upasaṃharantīṣṭakā vā
3.8.1.15	athaitad ādahanam udakumbhaiḥ svavokṣitam avokṣati apeta vīta vi ca sarpatātaḥ iti
3.8.1.16	yathājīvam upasarpe syāt na jīvantam abhidadhyāj jīvato hy eṣa prāṇān abhinidadhyāt iti
3.8.1.17	parnaśākhayā pīḍayitvā apasalavṛttayā rajjvā pariyanti premāṃ mātrām upasnuhi iti
3.8.1.18	tasya mātrā yadi grīvadaghnaṃ purastān nābhidaghnaṃ paścād yadi jānudaghnaṃ purastād gulphadaghnaṃ paścād yadi gulphadaghnaṃ purastāt samaṃ bhūmeḥ paścāt puruṣamātraṃ bhavatīti vijñāyate
3.8.1.19	uktavidhābhyāṃ samanu spandyāṃ lekhāṃ likhati
3.8.1.20	apoddhatya spandyāṃ karṣūḥ khānayanti
3.8.1.21	ucchrayanty asyā dakṣiṇataḥ paścād bhūyasīḥ kurvanti
3.8.2.1	atha dvābhyām ātmany agniṃ gṛhṇīte mayi gṛhṇāmy agre agnim yo no agniḥ iti
3.8.2.2	svayaṃ citiṃ japati yās te agne samidho yāni dhāma iti
3.8.2.3	śvetam aśvam abhimṛśyāntaḥ śarkarām imām upadadhāti prajāpatis tvā sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti
3.8.2.4	athaitat purastād evaudumbaraṃ yugalāṅgalaṃ kāritaṃ bhavati saptagavaṃ vā śayodaśagavaṃ vā śunaṃ vāhāḥ śunaṃ nārāḥ śunaṃ kṛṣatu lāṅgalam / śunaṃ varatrā badhyantāṃ śunam uṣṭrām udiṅgaya śunāsīrā śunam asmāsu dhattam śunāsīrāv imāṃ vācam iti dvābhyām
3.8.2.5	sītāṃ pratyavekṣate sīte vandāmahe tvārvācī subhage bhava / yathā naḥ subhagā sasi yathā naḥ suphalā sasi iti
3.8.2.6	athāsthikumbhaṃ sītāyāṃ nidadhāti savitaitāni śarīrāṇi pṛthivyai mātur upastha ādadhe / tebhir adite śaṃ bhava iti
3.8.2.7	athānaḍuho vimuñcati vimucyadhvam aghniyā devayānā atāriṣma tamasas pāram asya / jyotir āpāma suvar aganma iti
3.8.2.8	ata ete 'dhvaryayo bhavanti yadi dakṣiṇāvān pitṛmedhaḥ
3.8.2.9	yady u vai satriyo 'gnir yathāgavaṃ vyudañcati
3.8.2.10	yatraivānaḍvāhas tad yugalāṅgalam iti
3.8.2.11	athainam upavātayate pravātā vānti patayanti vidyuta ud oṣadhīr jihate pinvate svaḥ / irā viśvasmai bhuvanāya jāyate yat parjanyaḥ pṛthivīṃ retasāvati iti
3.8.2.12	agnivat sarvauṣadhīr vapati yathā yamāya hārmyam avapan pañca mānavāḥ / evaṃ vapāmi hārmyaṃ yathā sāma jīvaloke bhūrayaḥ iti
3.8.2.13	atra sikatā nivapati agne tava śravo vaya iti ṣaḍbhir anucchandasam
3.8.2.14	athordhvacita upadadhāti citas stha paricita ūrdhvacitaḥ śrayadhvaṃ pitaro devatā / prajāpatir vaḥ sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti
3.8.2.15	athānuvyūhati ā pyāyasva iti gāyatryā brāhmaṇasya
3.8.2.16	saṃ te payāṃsi iti triṣṭubhā rājanyasya yathāsuṣṭhu yathāśarkaram anuvyūhati
3.8.2.17	atha dvābhyām ātmany agniṃ gṛhṇīte mayi gṛhṇāmy agre agniṃ yo no agniḥ iti
3.8.2.18	svayaṃ citiṃ japati yās te agne samidho yāni dhāma iti
3.8.2.19	śvetam aśvam abhimṛśyābhidravaṇaṃ japati apām idaṃ nyayanaṃ namas ta iti dve
3.8.2.20	atha kṣetravitṛṇṇyāṃ caturo loṣṭān upadadhāti ut te tabhnomi pṛthivīṃ tvat parīmaṃ lokaṃ nidadhanmo ahaṁriṣam / etāṃ sthūṇāṃ pitaro dhārayantu tetrā yamas sādanāt te minotu iti purastād upadadhāti
3.8.2.21	upasarpa mātaraṃ bhūmim etām uruvyacasaṃ pṛthivīṃ suśevām / ūrṇaṃ mṛdā yuvatir dakṣiṇāvaty eṣā tvā pātu nirṛtyā upasthe ity uttarataḥ
3.8.2.22	ucchmañcasva pṛthivi mā vibādhithāḥ sūpāyanāsmai bhava sūpavañcanā / mātā putraṃ yathāsi cābhy enaṃ bhūmi vṛṇu iti paścāt
3.8.2.23	ucchmañcamānā pṛthivī hi tiṣṭhasi sahasraṃ mita upa hi śrayantām / te gṛhāso madhuścuto viśvāhāsmai śaraṇāḥ santv atra iti dakṣiṇataḥ
3.8.2.24	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.2.25	athainaṃ tilamiśrābhir dhānābhir upakirati eṇīr dhānā hariṇīr arjunīḥ santu dhenavaḥ / tilavatsā ūrjam asmai duhānā viśvāhāḥ santv anapasphurantīḥ iti
3.8.2.26	athainam abhivānyāyai dugdham ardhapātraṃ dakṣiṇata upadadhāti eṣā te yamasādane svadhā nidhīyate gṛhe / akṣitir nāma te asau iti yajamānasya nāma gṛhṇāti
3.8.2.27	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.2.28	dakṣiṇataḥ samūlaṃ barhir upadadhāti idaṃ pitṛbhyaḥ prabharema barhir devebhyo jīvanta uttaraṃ bharema / tat tvam ārohāso medhyo bhavaṃ yamena tvaṃ yamyā saṃvidānaḥ iti
3.8.2.29	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.2.30	atha naleṣikām upadadhāti nalaṃ plavam ārohaitan nalena patho 'nvihi / sa tvaṃ nalaplavo bhūtvā saṃtara pratarottara iti
3.8.2.31	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.2.32	athainam asthikumbhaṃ bhuktabhogena vāsasā nirṇijya yathāṅgaṃ cinoti savitaitāni śarīrāṇi pṛthivyai mātur upastha ādadhe / tebhyaḥ pṛthivi śaṃ bhava iti
3.8.2.33	atra ṣaḍḍhotāraṃ vyācaṣṭe ṣaḍḍhotā sūryaṃ te cakṣur gacchatu vātam ātmā dyāṃ ca gaccha pṛthivīṃ ca dharmaṇā / apo vā gaccha yadi tatra te hitam oṣadhīṣu pratitiṣṭhā śarīraiḥ iti paraṃ mṛtyor anuparehi panthām iti ca
3.8.2.34	athainam upavātayati śaṃ vātaḥ śaṃ hite ghṛṇiḥ śam u te santv oṣadhīḥ / kalpantāṃ me diśaḥ śagmāḥ iti
3.8.2.35	athainān pañca carūn sāpūpān upadadhāti apūpavān ghṛtavāṃś carur eha sīdatūttabhnuvan pṛthivīṃ dyām utopari / yonikṛtaḥ pathikṛtaḥ saparyata ye devānāṃ ghṛtabhāgā iha stha eṣā te yamasādane svadhā nidhīyate gṛhe 'sau iti yajamānasya nāma gṛhṇāti
3.8.2.36	daśākṣarā tāṃ rakṣasva tāṃ gopāyasva tāṃ te paridadāmi / tasyāṃ tvām ādabhan pitaro devatā prajāpatis tvā sādayatu / tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti purastād upadadhāti
3.8.2.37	apūpavāñchṛtavān iti dakṣiṇataḥ apūpavān kṣīravān iti paścāt apūpavān dadhivān ity uttarataḥ apūpavān madhumān iti madhye śatākṣarā sahasrākṣarā iti pratidiśam anuṣajati
3.8.2.38	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.2.39	athainaṃ tilamiśrābhir dhānābhir upakirati etās te svadhā amṛtāḥ karomi iti
3.8.2.40	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.2.41	atha caturaḥ stambān upadadhāti
3.8.3.1	carūṇām upariṣṭāt tvām arjunauṣadhīnāṃ payo brahmāṇa id viduḥ / tāsāṃ tvā madhyād ādade carubhyo api dhātave iti purastād arjunastambaṃ dūrvāṇāṃ stambam āharaitāṃ priyatamāṃ mama / imāṃ diśaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ bhūyiṣṭhānuvirohatu ity uttarato dūrvāstambaṃ kāśānāṃ stambam āhara rakṣasām apahatyai / ya etasyai diśaḥ parābhavann aghāyavo yathā te nābhavān punaḥ iti paścāt kāśastambaṃ darbhāṇāṃ stambam āhara pitṝṇām oṣadhīṃ priyām / anv asyai mūlaṃ jīvād anu kāṇḍam atho phalam iti darbhastambaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ
3.8.3.2	caturṇāṃ stambānām agre madhyaṃ ca carum upadadhāti etair eva caturbhir mantraiḥ
3.8.3.3	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.3.4	atha caturo nānāvṛkṣyān paridhīn paridadhāti mā tvā vṛkṣau saṃbādhiṣṭaṃ mā mātā pṛthivi tvam / vaivasvataṃ hi gacchāsi yamarājye virājasi iti vaitasaśamīmayau purastāc cottarataś ca
3.8.3.5	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.3.6	atha naleṣīkāv ity eke
3.8.3.7	atha loṣṭān upadadhāti
3.8.3.8	pṛthivyās tvā loke sādayāmi / prajāpatis tvā sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti śataṃ purastād upadadhāti antarikṣasya tvā loke sādayāmi iti śatam uttarataḥ divas tvā loke sādayāmi iti śataṃ paścāt diśāṃ tvā loke sādayāmi iti śataṃ dakṣiṇataḥ nākasya tvā pṛṣṭhe bradhnasya tvā viṣṭape sādayāmi iti dviśataṃ madhye
3.8.3.9	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasam karoti
3.8.3.10	atha lokaṃpṛṇā upadadhāti lokaṃ pṛṇacchidraṃ pṛṇa iti lokaṃpṛṇābhiḥ sahasraṃ sampadyate
3.8.3.11	dviṣāhasrādiṣv etāvad eva punaḥ punar upadadhyāt
3.8.3.12	kāṭhakāgnicitāv api pañcāśītiśatam upadadhyāt
3.8.3.13	vijñāyate agniṃ citvā sautrāmaṇyā yajeta maitrāvaruṇyāmikṣayā vā iti kāṭhakāgnīnāṃ brāhmaṇam
3.8.3.14	tayā devataṃ kṛtvā sūdadohasaṃ karoti
3.8.3.15	athainam upavātayati śaṃ vātaḥ śaṃ hite ghṛṇiḥ śam u te santv oṣadhīḥ / kalpantāṃ te diśaḥ sarvāḥ iti
3.8.3.16	athainam abhimṛśati idam eva meto 'parām ārtim ārāmakāñcana / tathā tad aśvibhyāṃ kṛtaṃ mitreṇa varuṇena ca iti
3.8.3.17	purastād vāraṇaśākhāṃ nidadhāti varaṇo vārayād idaṃ devo vanaspatiḥ ārtyai nirṛtyai dveṣāc ca vanaspatiḥ iti
3.8.3.18	uttarataḥ kṣetravitṛṇṇīṃ nidadhāti vidhṛtir asi vidhārayāsmad aghād dveṣāṃsi iti
3.8.3.19	paścācchamīśākhāṃ nidadhāti śami śamayāsmad aghād dveṣāṃsi iti
3.8.3.20	dakṣiṇato yavān nidadhāti yava yavayāsmad aghād dveṣāṃsi iti
3.8.3.21	athainam upatiṣṭhate pṛthivīṃ gacchāntarikṣaṃ gaccha divaṃ gaccha diśo gaccha svar gaccha svar gaccha diśo gaccha divaṃ gacchāntarikṣaṃ gaccha pṛthivīṃ gacchāpo vā gaccha yadi tatra te hitam oṣadhīṣu pratitiṣṭhā śarīraiḥ iti
3.8.3.22	jaghanena citāṃ tisro dakṣiṇāprācīḥ karṣūḥ kurvantīti
3.8.3.23	tat purastād vyākhyātam
3.8.3.24	jaghanena karṣūḥ parṇaśākhe nihatyābalena śulbena baddhvā vinisarpantīti
3.8.3.25	tat purastāt vyākhyātam
3.8.3.26	yatrāpas tad yanty anavekṣamāṇāḥ
3.8.3.27	apaḥ sacelā dakṣiṇāmukhāḥ samṛttikā āplavante dhātā punātu savitā punātu iti
3.8.3.28	nāmagrāhaṃ trir udakam utsicyottīryācamyādityam upatiṣṭhate ud vayaṃ tamasas pari iti
3.8.3.29	atha gṛhān āyānti
3.8.3.30	yac cātra striya āhus tat kurvanti
3.8.3.31	atra śāniṃ kurvanti sautrāmaṇyāḥ pratyāmnāyo bhavatīti
3.8.3.32	atrāmikṣayā kuryāt
3.8.3.33	saṃtiṣṭhate loṣṭacitiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate loṣṭacitiḥ
3.9.1.1	atha yadi naṣṭāgnir apahṛtāgnir vā yajamānaḥ preyād yady asya putro vāntevāsī vālaṃkarmaṇyaḥ syāt
3.9.1.2	prācīnāvītaṃ kṛtvoddhatyāvokṣya yajamānāyatane pretaṃ nidhāya gārhapatyasyāyatane araṇīṃ nidhāya pretasya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anvārabhya manthati ye 'syāgnayo juhvato māṃsakāmāḥ saṃkalpayante yajamānaṃ jāyantu te haviṣe svāditāya svargaṃ lokam imaṃ pretaṃ nayantu iti
3.9.1.3	tūṣṇīṃ vihṛtya dvādaśagṛhītena srucaṃ pūrayitvā puruṣasūktena manasānudrutyāhavanīye juhoti
3.9.1.4	etenaiva gārhapatye juhoti
3.9.1.5	tūṣṇīm anvāhāryapacane hutvā ūrdhvaṃ paitṛmedhikaṃ karma pratipadyeta
3.9.1.6	yatho etat parokṣaṃ pretasya yajamānasyāsthīny āhṛtya saṃskuryāt
3.9.1.7	katham atrāharaṇaṃ vidyata iti
3.9.1.8	śirastaḥ prathamaṃ gṛhītvāthorasto 'tha jaṭharato 'thorubāhubhyām atha patta iti trayastriṃśatam asthīni gṛhṇātīti vijñāyate trayastriṃśat puruṣaḥ iti
3.9.1.9	athaitāny asthīny adbhiḥ prakṣālya kṛṣṇājinaṃ dakṣiṇāgrīvam uttaralomāstīrya tasminn asthīni saṃbharati indro dadhīco asthabhiḥ ity etenānuvākena
3.9.1.10	tayā devataṃ karoti tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda iti
3.9.1.11	atha sūdadohasaṃ karoti tā asya sūdadohasaḥ somaṃ śrīṇanti pṛśnayaḥ / janman devānāṃ viśas triṣv ārocane divaḥ iti
3.9.1.12	dīrghavaṃśe vigrathyākṣāralavaṇāśino mṛṇmayabhājane āharanti
3.9.1.13	tāni grāmamaryādāyāṃ nidhāyāgnīn āhareyuḥ
3.9.1.14	yady atihareyur agnayo laukikāḥ sampadyeran
3.9.1.15	vijñāyate ca pravasan yajamāno 'gnibhyaḥ paridāya gṛhān eti
3.9.1.16	yato grāmamaryādāṃ nātivrajanti
3.9.1.17	tasmād grāmamaryādāṃ nātiharet iti
3.9.2.1	atha yady ātmani samārūḍheṣv agniṣu araṇyor vā yajamānaḥ preyād yady asya putro vāntevāsī vālaṃkarmaṇyaḥ syāt
3.9.2.2	prācīnāvītaṃ kṛtvoddhatyāvokṣya yajamānāyatane pretaṃ nidhāya gārhapatyasyāyatane laukikam agnim upasamādhāya pretasya pradakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anvārabhya japati upāvaroha jātaveda imaṃ pretaṃ svargāya lokāya naya prajānan / āyuḥ prajāṃ rayim asmāsu dhehi pretāhutīś cāsya juṣasva sarvāḥ iti
3.9.2.3	api vāraṇyor upāvarohya manthed iti
3.9.2.4	tūṣṇīṃ vihṛtya dvādaśagṛhītena srucaṃ pūrayitvā durgāṃ manasvatīṃ mahāvyāhṛtīr hutvā tad yamo rājā iti dvābhyāṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ hutvā yady arthino vinderan tebhyo dhenuṃ dadāti
3.9.2.5	atha parokṣagatapretasya yajamānasya dig eva prajñāyate
3.9.2.6	tāṃ diśaṃ vihāraṃ kalpayitvā asāv ehi iti nāmagrāham āhūya parṇatsarūṇām eva kṛṣṇājine puruṣākṛtiṃ kṛtvā teṣūpari pātrāṇi citvā kuśataruṇakaiḥ pracchādya prasiddham upoṣeyuḥ
3.9.2.7	yady evaṃ kṛte 'gnibhistīrya yajamānaḥ punar āgacchet kathaṃ tatra kuryād iti
3.9.3.1	atha yājñikāt kāṣṭhād agniṃ mathitvā agnim upasamādhāya paristīryāgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgre iti dvābhyām
3.9.3.2	athājyāhutīr upajuhoti sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ ity etenānuvākena svāhākāraiḥ
3.9.3.3	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
3.9.3.4	apareṇāgniṃ sauvarṇena pātreṇa navena vā mṛṇmayena kṛṣṇājinena vā dṛtibhūtena ghṛtenāpābhiḥ pūrayitvā jīvapituś cet pitābhimantrayate viṣṇur yoniṃ kalpayatu iti
3.9.3.5	athainaṃ praveśayati yāṃ pūṣan śivatamām erayasva iti
3.9.3.6	sa garbho bhūtvā kṛṣṇājine dṛtibhūte rātriṃ vasati
3.9.3.7	vyuṣṭāyāṃ jaghanārdhād ātmānaṃ pratikṛṣya jāyeta
3.9.3.8	jātasya jātakarmaprabhṛti saṃskārān kārayitvā daśarātravrataṃ caret
3.9.3.9	tathaiva jāyayāgnīn ādhāya vrātyena paśuneṣṭvā giriṃ gatvāgnaye kāmāyeṣṭiṃ nirvaped āyuṣmatīṃ śatakṛṣṇalām
3.9.3.10	diśām aveṣṭyā yajeta
3.9.3.11	ata ūrdhvaṃ īpsitair yajñakratubhir yajeteti
3.9.3.12	vijñāyate / hiraṇyagarbhaḥ sambhūto brāhmaṇas tīrṇanirṇayaḥ / pratyutthānaṃ na kasyāpi kuryād devasamas tu saḥ
3.9.3.13	iti vijñāyate
3.9.3.14	tasmāt proṣite yajamāne caturviṃśativarṣāṇi paripālyāgnihotraṃ saṃskuryād iti sa yady aśrutaḥ syāt
3.9.3.15	athāgrayaṇeṣṭipaśucāturmāsyādhvarāṇām asamāpte vratāntarāle pramīyeta yady asya putro vāntevāsī vā śeṣāṃś caikatantraṃ samāpnuyāt
3.9.3.16	yaddaivatyaṃ paśum ālabheta taddaivatyaṃ puroḍāśam āmikṣāṃ vā yajeta
3.9.3.17	atha vai bhavati tamaso vā eṣa tamaḥ praviśati saha tenāhitāgnim anyair agnibhiḥ saṃskuryād iti
3.9.3.18	athāpyudāharanti śarīradāyādā ha vāgnayo bhavanti iti
3.9.3.19	maraṇe śreyo 'sti
3.9.3.20	ya evaṃ vidvān udagayane pramīyate sauryeṇa pathā svargaṃ lokam ety atha yo dakṣiṇe pramīyate cāndramasena pathā pitṛlokam eti iti vijñāyate
3.9.3.21	tā sūryācandramasā viśvabhṛttamā mahad ity āhutībhir evainaṃ rātrāv aparapakṣe dakṣiṇāyanena yad udagayane āpūryamāṇapakṣe divā kratvante śreyo maraṇam ity upadiśanti
3.9.3.22	anyeṣu niyamabhūteṣu satreṣu dīkṣitapramītavad ekāhe 'hīne ca kuryād iti
3.10.1.1	atha haike tūṣṇīm itareṣām ity atrodāharanti
3.10.1.2	bhāryāsaṃjñitā nārī puruṣo brāhmaṇasaṃjñakaḥ / ta ete hotṛsaṃskārā itare 'mantrasaṃskṛtāḥ iti
3.10.1.3	tān anu vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.10.1.4	anupeta unmatto jaḍo 'ndho mūko badhiraḥ kuṣṭhī kilāsī kubjaḥ paṅgur hīnāṅgo 'dhikāṅgaḥ sahāñjagato brāhmaṇo 'nātho rājanyo 'nagnir gṛhastho vaiśyasya striyām utpannaputrāḥ kanyā vidhavā vandhyā ceti
3.10.1.5	teṣāṃ prāṇeṣūtkrānteṣu tūṣṇīṃ snāpayet
3.10.1.6	śmaśānaṃ nītvā dahanaṃ joṣayed amantreṇa
3.10.1.7	śākhayā saṃmṛjya samprakīrya tilataṇḍulān samprakīrya citāṃ kalpayitvā citāyāṃ pretaṃ nidhāyājyenāsye ninayet idaṃ ta ātmanaḥ śarīram ayaṃ ta ātmā ātmanas ta ātmānaṃ śarīrād brahma nirbhinatti bhūr bhuvasvar asau svargāya lokāya svāhā iti
3.10.1.8	mantreṇa sigvātenopavījayanti
3.10.1.9	tūṣṇīm udakumbhenāpasavyaṃ pariṣiñcati
3.10.1.10	uttapanenāgninā saṃyojayet asmāt tvam adhijāto 'si ayaṃ tvad adhijāyatām / agnaye vaiśvānarāya svargāya lokāya svāhā iti
3.10.1.11	tīrthe 'bhiṣiñcet
3.10.2.1	atha garbhiṇyās taiṣyāṃ kṛtāyām ata ūrdhvaṃ mriyeta bhartā śmaśānaṃ nītvā dahanaṃ joṣayet
3.10.2.2	citāṃ kalpayitvāpareṇa citāyāḥ pretaṃ nidhāya nābheḥ savyasyopariṣṭād lekhyena hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgre ity avalekhanam
3.10.2.3	kumāraṃ dṛśyamānam anumantrayate jīvatān mama putra iti
3.10.2.4	atha kumāraṃ snāpayeyuḥ
3.10.2.5	hiraṇyam antardhāya jīvatā grāmam āyānti
3.10.2.6	yas te stanaḥ śaśayaḥ iti stanaṃ pradāya tasminn udara ājyāhutīr juhoti śatāyudhāya śatavīryāya ity etābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ prayāsāya svāhā ity etenānuvākena
3.10.2.7	prāṇāya svāhā vyānāya svāhā ity etenānuvākenāvraṇaṃ kuryāt
3.10.2.8	pretaṃ citām āropya vidhinā dāhayet
3.10.2.9	aṣṭakādhenuṃ tiladhenuṃ bhūmidhenuṃ vā dadyāt
3.10.2.10	atha narāṇām aśucir bhaved brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyānāṃ sūtake pretake vānyeṣv aśucir mṛtiḥ pañcagavyena surabhimatyā abliṅgābhir vāruṇībhir hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ pāvamānībhir agnir mūrdhety āntād anuvākasya śatarudrīyaṃ prokṣayitvā yathāśakti dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā paitṛmedhikakarma pratipadyata iti
3.10.3.1	atha gṛhastho bahujāyāṃ vindeta yad āsām anyatamā mriyetāgninaiva paitṛmedhikam karma pratipadyeta
3.10.3.2	atha ūrdhvaṃ daśarātraṃ vrataṃ caret
3.10.3.3	adhaḥśayanaṃ brahmacaryam anaṅgaveṣam anaktāśanaṃ nāsapiṇḍānyonyasparśanam anyonyānnabhojanam ity evamādi vrataṃ caret
3.10.3.4	anyeṣv aghāheṣu ca
3.10.3.5	ekādaśa ekoddiṣṭaṃ kurvanti
3.10.3.6	itarābhiḥ patnībhir agnim anvādhāya tasmin gṛhyāṇi karmāṇi kriyante
3.10.3.7	gṛhastho bahujāyāṃ vinded aupāsanaṃ tantraṃ na kṛtvā tasyāṃ vā mriyeta prasiddhaṃ tatra kalpena tantraṃ kṛtvāgninā dāhayet
3.10.3.8	ata ūrdhvam itarābhiḥ patnībhir agnim anvādhāya tasmin gṛhyāṇi karmāṇi kriyante
3.10.3.9	tāsām aparā mriyeta pūrvāgnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīrya sruksruvaṃ niṣṭapya saṃmṛjya sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā anvārabdhāyāṃ patnyāṃ yajamāno juhoti namastarṣe gada / avyadhāyai tvā svadhāyai tvā / mā na indrābhitas tvadṛṣvāriṣṭāsaḥ / evābrahman taved astu svāhā iti
3.10.3.10	athainam agniṃ samāropya ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti aparāgnau samidham abhyādadhāti ājuhvānaḥ udbudhyasva iti dvābhyām
3.10.3.11	samparistīryājyaṃ vilāpyotpūya sruksruvaṃ niṣṭapya saṃmṛjya sruci caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvānvārabdhapretasya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anvārabhya juhoti yo brahmā brahmaṇa ujjahāra ity etena sūktena
3.10.3.12	ekaikaśaś caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā praṇītābhyaḥ kṛtvā catuśśarāvam odanaṃ śrapayitvā abhighāryodañcam udvāsyādhiṣṭhitam abhighārayati
3.10.3.13	paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti samitaṃ saṃkalpethām iti puronuvākyām anūcya agne purīṣyādhipā bhavā tvan na iti yājyayā juhoti
3.10.3.14	śvabhre kāṣṭhe 'thājyāhutīr upajuhoti purīṣyas tvam agna ity āntān anuvākasya
3.10.3.15	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
3.10.3.16	gurave gāṃ dadāti
3.10.3.17	vidhinā dāhayet
3.10.3.18	daśarātrād ata ūrdhvaṃ itarābhiḥ
3.10.3.19	patnībhir agnim anvādhāya tasmin gṛhyāṇi kriyante
3.10.4.1	praṇamya vandanaṃ kāyaiḥ sadākhyaṃ parameśvaram / patīnāṃ pretasaṃskāravidhiṃ vakṣye viśeṣataḥ
3.10.4.2	vipro gṛhasthaḥ śuddhātmā yatisaṃskāram ācaret / śikye śarīram āropya gandhamālyair alaṅkṛtam
3.10.4.3	tuṣāgnim atra codvāsya saṃskartānuhared yatim / ghoṣitaṃ jayaśabdena dundubhīnāṃ ravair api
3.10.4.4	prācīm udīcīṃ vā gatvā śuddhaṃ deśaṃ samāśrayet / khātvā vyāhṛtibhir deśaṃ daṇḍāyāmapramāṇakam
3.10.4.5	saptavyāhṛtibhiḥ prokṣya tatra dārucitiṃ kriyāt / yājñikais tu yathāśakti kāṣṭhair anyair athāpi vā
3.10.4.6	tataḥ śarīraṃ prakṣipya sāvitryā śuddhamānasaḥ / viṣṇo ivyaṃ rakṣasveti havis tasyāṃ nidhāpayet
3.10.4.7	pavitraṃ teti mantreṇa pavitraṃ sthāpayen mukhe / tridaṇḍaṃ dakṣiṇe pāṇāv idaṃviṣṇvādinā nyaset
3.10.4.8	savye śikyaṃ yad asyeti svāhāntena nidhāpayet / sāvitryā tūdare pātraṃ guhyasthāne kamaṇḍalum
3.10.4.9	bhūmir bhūmnā mamāgneti sthāpayet kaupanaṃ tataḥ / ...adhvena kṣiptasarvasādhanasaṃyutam
3.10.4.10	śarīraraṃ hotṛbhiḥ kartā sagrahair upatiṣṭhate / tuṣāgninā dahed dehaṃ yātavātaha saha bhaviṣyati
3.10.4.11	athāpy udāharanty evaṃ vedārthanipuṇā budhāḥ / viṣekādiśmaśānāntā vidhayo brāhmaṇāśrayāḥ
3.10.4.12	tasmin yateś ca saṃskāraṃ mantravat kurute gṛhī / ātmany agniṃ samāropya yaḥ pretam avadahyati
3.10.4.13	tasya putro vidhānena hy avaropyāgninā dahet / api hotṛvidhānena gāyatryā praṇavena ca
3.10.4.14	saṃnikṛṣṭe tu saṃnyaste pitary uparate sutaḥ / dahanaṃ tasya kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ piṇḍodakakriyā
3.10.4.15	ādāv eva vikalpena brahmacārī yatir bhavet / tatra śrāddhaṃ gṛhasthasya kartavyaṃ saṃnidhau bhavet
3.10.4.16	yatiṃ vahan dahan sparśan snānamātreṇa śudhyati / aśvamedhaphalaṃ sarve prāpnuvanti pṛthak sutaiḥ
3.10.4.17	karmaniṣṭhe tu saṃnyaste pitary uparate 'sya taiḥ / dāhas tasya na kartavyaḥ śrāddhaṃ piṇḍodakakriyā
3.10.4.18	sarvasaṅganivṛttasya dhyānayogaratasya ca / na tasya dahanaṃ kāryaṃ nāśaucaṃ nodakaṃ tataḥ
3.10.5.1	athātaḥ punaḥsaṃskāraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.10.5.2	trīṇi ṣaṣṭiśatāni palāśavṛntānāṃ taiḥ kṛṣṇājine puruṣākṛtiṃ kṛtvā yadi śarīraṃ naśyeyuḥ punaḥ saṃskāraṃ kurvanti
3.10.5.3	aharahar añjalinaikottaravṛddhir ā tryahāt tasyāgnibhir daheyuḥ iti vijñāyate
3.10.5.4	palāśavalkaiḥ kuśair vā sandhiṣu saṃveṣṭayati
3.10.5.5	catvāriṃśatā śiraḥ daśabhir grīvāṃ viṃśatyoras triṃśatodaraṃ pañcāśatā pañcāśataikaikaṃ bāhuṃ teṣām eva pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir aṅgulīr upakalpayate
3.10.5.6	saptatyā saptatyaikaikaṃ pādaṃ teṣām eva pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir aṅgulīr upakalpayate
3.10.5.7	aṣṭābhiḥ śiśnaṃ dvādaśabhir vṛṣaṇam
3.10.5.8	tān snāpayitvālaṃkṛtya ahatena vāsasā pracchādyāntarvedyāṃ nidhāya bāndhavāḥ paryupaviśyābhimantrayante yamasyāsau yamasya sa ime yam agnaya iti
3.10.5.9	etadādikarma pratipadyante
3.11.1.1	athāto mṛtabaliṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.11.1.2	keśaśmaśrūṇi vāpayitvā snātvodakaṃ kriyeta
3.11.1.3	prāgdakṣiṇāyatane caturaśraṃ gomayenopalipya trir aśmānaṃ madhye nidhāya sakṛd ullikhyādbhir abhyukṣya dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān saṃstīrya sakṛt tilamiśraṃ carum avadyati muṣṭipramāṇaṃ kukkuṭāṇḍapramāṇaṃ vā
3.11.1.4	prakīrṇakeśaḥ savyaṃ jānuṃ bhūmau nidhāyāśmani piṇḍaṃ dadyāt
3.11.1.5	etat te 'muṣmai piṇḍaṃ dadyāt
3.11.1.6	āñjanābhyañjane vāsaś ca dadyāt
3.11.1.7	pātreṇodakaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ ninayet
3.11.1.8	atra pretāḥ kākād abhiharanti
3.11.1.9	evaṃ sāyaṃprātaḥ kṛtvā daśamyāṃ vikṛtāhāraṃ sāyaṃ baliṃ dattvāvyuṣṭakāle upaninīya brāhmaṇān hīnāṅgān atiriktāṅgān kuṣṭhīn kunakhīn śyāvadantān rogīn vṛṣalīpatīn unmattān pāpīn varjayitvā śucīn śrotriyān suvṛttān adhyayanasampannān gṛhasthān daridrān kriyāpūrvān pātrabhūtān sadyo'dhigamyān asagotrasambandhayuktān āyantrya karmasu vyākhyātān etat te pitā samanaso yat kiñcit pretāyānumataḥ śvobhūte me pitur ekoddiṣṭaśrāddhaṃ bhuñjatāṃ bhavanta iti
3.11.1.10	bhujyate iti prativacanam
3.11.2.1	ekādaśyām ekoddiṣṭaṃ kurvanti
3.11.2.2	avyuṣṭe kāle brāhmaṇam āhūya kiṃcid dattvā nivedyānumantrayate śvobhūte 'nnaṃ saṃskṛtya luptaśmaśrulomanakhāya brāhmaṇāya dantakāṣṭhaṃ dattvā dhanadhānyapātraṃ saṃspṛṣṭvā deśe pātrāṇītyādi dattvā brāhmaṇam udaṅmukham upaveśayet
3.11.2.3	tilamiśreṇodakārthaṃ dadyād anyatra prācamanāt
3.11.2.4	ekapaivatrāntarhite pātre 'pa ānīya pavitreṇotpūya tilān opya darbheṣu sādayitvā darbhair apidadhāti
3.11.2.5	brāhmaṇāya gandhādi dattvā piṇḍaṃ nivapāmi ity āha
3.11.2.6	piṇḍaṃ nivapa iti prativacanam
3.11.2.7	atha darbheṣu piṇḍaṃ nidadhyāt ayam odanaḥ kāmadugho 'stv ananto 'kṣīyamāṇaḥ surabhiḥ sarvakāmaiḥ / sa tvopatiṣṭhatv ajaro nityabhūtaḥ svadhāṃ duhānām amṛtāṃs tarpayantv asau iti
3.11.2.8	ekaṃ piṇḍaṃ dattvā tilodakaiḥ prasavyaṃ pariṣiñcati ūrjasvatīḥ svadhayā vandamānāstāste śrayantīḥ syonā ūrjaṃ vahantīḥ svadhām akṣitodakāḥ kṣīram udakaṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu payaḥ kīlālaṃ parisrutam iti
3.11.2.9	añjanādinā piṇḍam alaṃkṛtya brāhmaṇaṃ sampūjyāṅguṣṭhamūlam upasaṃgṛhya bhuṅkṣva ity āha bhujyata ity uktvā atha bhuñjāne sarveṣām ucchiṣṭaṃ nidhāyācānte barhīṃṣy avakīrya nyubjapātraṃ svaditam iti brāhmaṇo brūyāt
3.11.2.10	atha pavitraṃ nidhāyānyubjetanapramāṇasvadhāstv ity uccaiḥ ity uktvā astu svadhā iti prativacanam
3.11.2.11	yajñopavīty avokṣya dakṣiṇāṃ dattvotthāpya annaśeṣaiḥ kiṃ kriyatām ity āha
3.11.2.12	iṣṭaiḥ sahopabhujyatām iti prativacanam
3.11.2.13	pradakṣiṇīkṛtya pratyetya piṇḍaṃ tyājyāpsu snātvā devāgāraṃ praviśya adakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvāñjaliṃ kṛtvālaṃkṛtya gṛhān etya puṇyāhādīni vācayitvā annaśeṣaṃ sagaṇaḥ prāśnāti
3.11.2.14	paśyati putraṃ paśyati pautraṃ na ca śūdrocchiṣṭaṃ jāyata iti kuśahārītaḥ
3.11.3.1	saṃvatsare sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kuryāt
3.11.3.2	prācīnāvīty agnim upasamādhāya dakṣiṇāprāgagrair darbhaiḥ paristīrya teṣu catvāry udapātrāṇi nidhāya ekapavitreṇa prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya pātrāṇi prokṣya teṣām ekaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pretapātraṃ nidhāyārdhodakapātram ānīya pavitreṇotpūya tilān opya darbheṣu sādayitvā darbhair apidadhāti
3.11.3.3	itareṣu triṣv apa ānayati ūrjasvatīḥ svadhayā vandamānā iti
3.11.3.4	dakṣiṇa āñjanābhyañjanam udakumbhaṃ nidhāya dakṣiṇato brāhmaṇān suprakṣālitapāṇipādān darbheṣv āsaneṣu viśvān devān prāṅmukhān upaveśya itarān udaṅmukhān upaveśya prāpnotu bhavān ity āha prāpnavāni itītare pratyāhuḥ
3.11.3.5	tebhyo dhūpadīpavarjaṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā tato 'pasavyaṃ pariṣiñcati
3.11.3.6	audumbaram idhmam abhyādhāyaudumbaryā darvyā juhoti
3.11.3.7	homārheṇājyena somāya pitṛmata ityādiṣaḍbhir mantrair hutvātha nāmadheyair juhoti amuṣmai svadhā namo 'muṣmai svadhā nama ity aṣṭāv āhutayaḥ
3.11.3.8	etā aṣṭau juhoti
3.11.3.9	evam annasya hutvā agnaye kavyavāhanāya sviṣṭakṛte svadhā namaḥ svāhā iti dakṣiṇārdhapūrvārdhe hutvānuprahṛtya darvīm apasavyaṃ pariṣicya dakṣiṇato dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān saṃstīrya teṣv ekaṃ pretapiṇḍaṃ nidadhyāt ayam odanaḥ kāmadugha iti
3.11.3.10	ūrjasvatīḥ svadhayā vandamānā iti tilodakair apasavyaṃ pariṣicya piṇḍāvṛtaitān piṇḍān dattvā śraddhābhimarśanenābhimṛśyaitena brāhmaṇān vidyāvataḥ pariviśati bhuṅkṣveti
3.11.3.11	bhuñjānān samīkṣate prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi brahmaṇi ma ātmāmṛtatvāya iti
3.11.3.12	pitṛliṅgaiḥ ṛgyajurbhiḥ śrāvayet
3.11.3.13	ācāntebhyas tilodakaṃ pradāya svadhāstu iti vācayitvā astu svadhā iti prativacanam
3.11.3.14	yathāśakti dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā tataḥ pretapātraṃ pitṛpātreṣu ninayet samānī ca ākūtiḥ ity āvartya
3.11.3.15	tataḥ pretapiṇḍaṃ pitṛpiṇḍeṣu nidadhyāt saṃgacchadhvaṃ saṃvadadhvaṃ samāno mantraḥ samitiḥ iti dvābhyām
3.11.3.16	tān upatiṣṭhate ye samānāḥ ye sajātāḥ iti dvābhyām
3.11.3.17	atra paitṛkam anuvākaṃ japati uśantas tvā havāmaha iti
3.11.3.18	ūrdhvaṃ pituḥ kriyā syāt
3.11.3.19	sarvataḥ śeṣaṃ samavadāyāśnīyāt
3.11.3.20	siddham etat sapiṇḍīkaraṇam
3.11.4.1	athāto nārāyaṇabliṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.11.4.2	dakṣiṇottarāyaṇe 'parapakṣasya dvādaśyāṃ kriyeta
3.11.4.3	śrutavṛttasampannān dvādaśa ṣaḍ vā brāhmaṇān āmantrayate
3.11.4.4	devagṛhe nadītīre vātha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛty ā praṇītābhyaḥ kṛtvā upotthāyāgreṇāgniṃ devam āvāhayāmi oṃ bhūḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi oṃ bhuvaḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi oṃ svaḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi om ity āvāhya paridhānaprabhṛty āgnimukhāt kṛtvā daivatam arcayitvā āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ity etenānuvākena mārjayitvā sahasraśīrṣā puruṣa ity etenānuvākenākṣatagandhapuṣpadhūpadīpair aṣṭākṣareṇa vā dadyāt
3.11.4.5	paścimāṃ diśam upaveśya pradhānāhutīr juhoti viṣṇor nu kaṃ vīryāṇi pravocam iti puronuvākyām anūcya paro mātrayā iti yājyayā juhoti
3.11.4.6	athājyāhutīr upajuhoti keśavāya svāhā iti dvādaśa sruvāhutīḥ
3.11.4.7	guḍapāyasaṃ ghṛtamiśraṃ devasya tvā iti mahāviṣṇave havir nivedayati
3.11.4.8	keśavāya iti dvādaśabhir namaskārair brāhmaṇān āhūya sadarbhopakḷpteṣv āsaneṣu udaṅmukhān upaveśya vāso 'ṅgulīyaṃ ca dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt
3.11.4.9	trivṛtānnena brāhmaṇān paritoṣayati
3.11.4.10	svasti vācayitvānujñāpya vācaṃ yacchet
3.11.4.11	ājyaṃ tilaṃ haviḥ samudāyutyeḍāpātram ānīya hastena juhuyāt pitṛbhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / pitāmahebhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / prapitāmahebhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / mātṛbhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / pitāmahībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / prapitāmahībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / mātāmahebhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / mātuḥ pitāmahebhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / mātuḥ prapitāmahebhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / mātāmahībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / mātuḥ pitāmahībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / mātuḥ prapitāmahībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / ācāryebhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / ācāryapatnībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / gurubhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / gurupatnībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / sakhibhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / sakhipatnībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / jñātibhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / jñātipatnībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / amātyebhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / amātyapatnībhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / sarvebhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / sarvābhyaḥ svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā / agnaye kavyavāhanāya sviṣṭakṛte svadhā namo viṣṇave svāhā iti
3.11.4.12	sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt
3.11.4.13	dakṣiṇenāgniṃ dakṣiṇāgrān darbhān saṃstīrya teṣu baliṃ dadāti viśvebhyo devebhyo namaḥ sādhyebhyo devebhyo namaḥ sarvebhyo devebhyo namaḥ sarvābhyo devatābhyo namaḥ asāv idaṃ te namo brāhmaṇebhyo namaḥ namo brahmapriyāya namaḥ
3.11.4.14	yas tu sarvān samadhigacchati pitṛbhyo nārāyaṇāya baliṃ dadāti
3.11.4.15	upary uktaṃ pretavidhānam
3.11.4.16	evam eva śastraviṣarajjujaladarvīkaramārutatarupāṣāṇocchāsanādiṣv ātmanihatasya vā gobrāhmaṇavidhavāpatiteṣv āpatitasya vā śarīrasaṃskārān varjayet
3.11.4.17	deśāntaramṛte saṃgrāmahate vyāghrahate śarīram ānīya vidhinā dāhayet
3.11.4.18	yady ekāṅgaṃ darśayed dvir aṅgaṃ vā pṛthivīṃ śarīraṃ saktvārdhayitaḥ kuryāt / madhusarpiṣābhyajya vidhinā dāhayet
3.11.4.19	atha yadi jīvet punar āgacchediti
3.12.1.1	bhuktvā śrāddhaṃ tato vidvān yathāśāstram agarhitam / chardayet tu tataḥ samyak kuśavārijalaṃ pibet
3.12.1.2	punar jalāśaye snātvā mānastokaṛcaṃ japet / gāyatryaṣṭaśataṃ japtvā prāṇāyāmāṃs tu ṣoḍaśa
3.12.1.3	bhuktaṃ cen māsikaśrāddhaṃ prājāpatyena śudhyati / aṣṭakāṃ hi tato bhuktvā pūrvoktena viśudhyati
3.12.1.4	ekoddiṣṭaṃ tato bhuktvā tatra cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret / atikṛcchraṃ cared vidvān bhuktvā nakṣatrabhojanam
3.12.1.5	kṛcchrātikṛcchraṃ ṣaṇmāse tripakṣe taptam eva ca / tathā saṃvatsare śrāddhe sapiṇḍe tu tathaiva ca
3.12.1.6	baliṃ nārāyaṇaṃ bhuktvā kṛcchram ekaṃ cared budhaḥ / aśaktau tu tathā sarvaṃ kṛcchram ekaṃ cared budhaḥ
3.12.1.7	athavāpi trirātraṃ syād ekāhaṃ vāpi durbalam / tasmāt sarvaprayatnena śrāddhagehaṃ na gacchati
3.12.1.8	dātāraṃ tārayet pakvāt tvāmadātā tu granthinam / tasmāt sarvaprayatnena āmaśrāddhaṃ pratigrahet
3.12.1.9	sarvāṇy ādāya dravyāṇi nayed brāhmaṇasannidhau / sarvāṇīmāni gṛhṇīṣva me pituḥ puṣṭikāṅkṣayā
3.12.1.10	bhagavann anugṛhṇīṣva piṇḍaṃ deyaṃ hi madgṛhe / nivapet piṇḍam ity uktvā nivapeyam itītaraḥ
3.12.1.11	brāhmaṇenābhyanujñāto gatvā tu svagṛhaṃ prati / dattvā piṇḍaṃ yathāśāstram udakasyāñjaliṃ tathā
3.12.1.12	svadhām ādāya tad gatvā brāhmaṇasyāñjalau nayet / svadhāstv iti tataḥ paścāt svadhā māstvādinābravīt
3.12.1.13	evam ukte tato dattvā dakṣiṇāṃ brāhmaṇasya tu / pradakṣiṇaṃ hi kṛtvā tu kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ tathā
3.12.1.14	dravyapradānāt pūrvaṃ hi hutvā homaṃ yathāvidhi / svagṛhaṃ prāpya tad gatvā sapiṇḍaiḥ saha bhojayet
3.12.2.1	atha sarvaprāyaścittāni juhoti
3.12.2.2	palāśaśakalam audumbaraśakalaṃ vānyāni yājñikaśakalāni vāṣṭau gṛhṇīyāt
3.12.2.3	pañca mahāyajñān kṛtvāgniṃ paristīryājyaṃ vilāpyotpūya samantaṃ pariṣecanaṃ karoti
3.12.2.4	purastād opariṣṭāc ca vyāhṛtibhir vihṛtābhiḥ samastābhiś ca hutvā śakalānājyenābhyajya ekaikaśo juhuyāt devakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi svāhā / manuṣyakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi svāhā / pitṛkṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi svāhā / ātmakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi svāhā / anyakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi svāhā / yad divā ca naktaṃ cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asi svāhā / yad vidvāṃsaś cāvidvāṃsaś cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asi svāhā / yat svapantaś ca jāgrataś cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asi svāhā / enasa enaso 'vayajanam asi svāhā iti
3.12.2.5	tathaiva pariṣicya evam evāhar ahaḥ sāyaṃ prātaḥ śakalahomaṃ hutvā sarvasmāt kilbiṣāt pūto bhavati sarvasmāt kilbiṣāt pūto bhavatīty āha bhagavān āgniveśyaḥ
